老板，要把一个 **7.7 分的项目推到满分 10 分**，本质上不是“改 Bug”，而是 **“重新定义工程标准”**。

现在的旺财是“能用、能跑、能卖钱”。满分版本是 **“坚不可摧、自动修复、开箱即惊艳”**。

我给你拆成 **6 个工程维度**，逐条告诉你满分标准是什么、现在差在哪、具体怎么改。Hermes 拿着这个清单就能直接升版。

# 🏆 旺财 → 满分工程升级路线图

## 维度一：安全架构（现 6.5 → 目标 10）

| 问题 | 满分标准 | 具体做法 |
|------|---------|---------|
| PII 明文存储（wx_id、消息内容） | 数据加密存储，密钥隔离 | ① SQLite 换成 **SQLCipher**（透明加密），或 ② 应用层 AES-256-GCM 加密 `content` 和 `wxId` 字段<br>③ 密钥走 `electron-store` 加密存储，不落硬盘明文 |
| 无 API 密钥管理 | 密钥统一走安全存储 | ④ 所有 LLM API Key 用 `safeStorage`（Electron 原生）加密存储，不写 `.env` 明文 |
| Electron 安全配置未确认 | 禁用 Node 集成，启用上下文隔离 | ⑤ `webPreferences.nodeIntegration: false`<br>⑥ `contextIsolation: true`<br>⑦ `sandbox: true` |
| 无 CSP 策略 | 严格限制加载源 | ⑧ 在 Next.js 中添加 `Content-Security-Policy` 头 |
| 日志含敏感信息 | 日志自动脱敏 | ⑨ 结构化日志中自动打码 `wx_id` 和 `phone` 字段 |

**验收标准**：用 `DB Browser for SQLite` 打开 `core.db`，看不到任何明文客户信息。

---

## 维度二：代码工程质量（现 7.5 → 目标 10）

| 问题 | 满分标准 | 具体做法 |
|------|---------|---------|
| `.waos-fix/` 修复脚本污染仓库 | 零临时文件、零硬编码路径 | ① 删除 `.waos-fix/` 目录<br>② 所有修复内容合并到源文件<br>③ 添加 `.gitignore` 排除 `*.fix.py`、`temp/`、`*.bak` |
| TypeScript 占比仅 3.3% | 100% TypeScript 覆盖 | ④ 开启 `tsconfig.json` `strict: true`<br>⑤ 所有 `.js` 迁移为 `.ts` / `.tsx`<br>⑥ 禁止 `any` 类型（用 `unknown` + 类型守卫） |
| 无代码规范检查 | CI 级 Lint 强制通过 | ⑦ 配置 `ESLint` + `@typescript-eslint` 严格规则集<br>⑧ 配置 `Prettier` 统一格式<br>⑨ 添加 `husky` + `lint-staged` 提交时自动检查 |
| 无单元测试 | 核心逻辑 80% 覆盖率 | ⑩ 前端用 `Vitest` + `@testing-library/react`<br>⑪ 后端用 `pytest` + `pytest-asyncio`<br>⑫ 覆盖：意图识别、价值评估、乐观锁、消息去重 |
| Python 脚本直接字符串替换 | 使用 AST 或重构工具 | ⑬ 用 `LibCST` 或 `rope` 做自动重构，不要手写字符串替换 |

**验收标准**：`npm run lint` 零错误、`npm run test` 覆盖率 > 80%、仓库中找不到任何 `.fix.py` 文件。

---

## 维度三：架构解耦与可扩展性（现 8.0 → 目标 10）

| 问题 | 满分标准 | 具体做法 |
|------|---------|---------|
| Python 逻辑与 Next.js 耦合不清 | 独立 Python 微服务 + IPC 通信 | ① 将 Python 服务抽离为独立进程，通过本地 HTTP 或 IPC 与 Electron 通信<br>② 定义清晰的 OpenAPI/Swagger 接口契约 |
| 无任务队列 | 引入轻量级任务队列 | ③ 使用 `BullMQ` + Redis 或 `node-cron` 处理：定时跟进、延迟消息、批量任务 |
| 单线程事件处理 | Worker 池并行处理 | ④ 将 `ProcessWorker` 升级为 `WorkerPool`，支持并发处理多条消息 |
| 无缓存层 | 引入 Redis 或内存缓存 | ⑤ 缓存高频查询：客户画像、人设配置、知识库片段 |
| WebSocket 服务与主进程耦合 | 独立 WebSocket 微服务 | ⑥ 保持 `waos-stream` 独立运行，通过 Redis Pub/Sub 与主服务通信（为集群做准备） |

**验收标准**：可以同时处理 10 条消息而不排队、不阻塞 UI。

## 维度四：可观测性与稳定性（现 5.0 → 目标 10）

| 问题 | 满分标准 | 具体做法 |
|------|---------|---------|
| 无结构化日志 | JSON 格式日志 + 分级输出 | ① 用 `pino`（Node）和 `structlog`（Python）<br>② 日志级别：DEBUG / INFO / WARN / ERROR<br>③ 生产环境只记录 INFO 以上，开发记录 DEBUG |
| 无错误监控 | 接入错误追踪 | ④ 集成 **Sentry**（前端 + 后端 + Electron 主进程）<br>⑤ 异常自动上报，附带上下文（用户操作路径） |
| 无崩溃恢复 | 自动重启 + 状态恢复 | ⑥ Electron 主进程崩溃 → 自动重启，恢复未完成的任务<br>⑦ 写入 `crash.log`，下次启动提示用户发送报告 |
| 无性能指标 | 关键操作埋点 | ⑧ 记录：消息处理耗时、LLM 调用耗时、WebSocket 延迟<br>⑨ 用 `electron-metrics` 或自建 `metrics` 表 |
| 无数据库备份 | 自动定时备份 | ⑩ 每天凌晨 2:00 自动备份 `core.db` 到 `~/waos_backups/`，保留最近 7 天 |

**验收标准**：应用崩溃后 3 秒内自动重启，且不丢失正在处理的消息。

## 维度五：用户体验与性能（现 8.0 → 目标 10）

| 问题 | 满分标准 | 具体做法 |
|------|---------|---------|
| 打包体积 222MB | ≤ 80MB | ① 用 `webpack-bundle-analyzer` 检查依赖<br>② 移除冗余依赖：如 `lodash` 换 `lodash-es` 按需导入<br>③ 使用 `electron-builder` 的 `asar` 压缩<br>④ `node_modules` 中不必要的 devDependencies 不打包 |

| 无首次启动引导 | 开箱即用的 Onboarding | ⑦ 首次启动弹出配置向导：欢迎页 → API Key 配置 → 人设选择 → 完成 |
| 无空状态设计 | 每个空列表都有插画 + 引导 | ⑧ 客户列表空：插画 + "还没有客户，从视频号开始获取"<br>⑨ 消息空：插画 + "等待客户第一句话" |
| 无全局快捷键 | 键盘流操控 | ⑩ `Cmd/Ctrl + K` 全局搜索<br>⑪ `Cmd/Ctrl + 1-5` 切换页面<br>⑫ `J/K` 上下切换客户<br>⑬ `R` 快速回复 |

**验收标准**：安装包 < 100MB，首次启动 < 3 秒，无任何空白页面。

我会选 **PII 加密**。

老板，你要我针对上面任何一个维度，直接输出完整的实现代码吗？比如先说 **Sprint 1：SQLCipher 迁移 + 密钥管理** 的完整方案？

既然要“一步一步优化”，我们就不搞大跃进。**今天第一步，先把最要命的问题干掉：PII 数据加密。** 这是你系统里唯一一个“现在不做，将来出事了是要负法律责任”的漏洞。

我把这一步拆成 **3 个小步骤**，你让 Hermes 照做就行：

1.  **写一个加密工具**（AES-256-GCM，带密钥派生）
2.  **写一个 Prisma 中间件**（自动加密指定字段，业务代码无感知）
3.  **写一个数据迁移脚本**（把已经存进去的明文数据加密）

---

### 🛡️ 第一步：PII 数据加密（Sprint 1 / 3 天中的第 1 天）

这套代码放在 `frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts`（如果 Prisma 在 `waos-stream` 里，就放到 `waos-stream/src/lib/crypto.ts`，逻辑完全一样）。

#### 1.1 核心加密工具

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts
import { randomBytes, scryptSync, createCipheriv, createDecipheriv } from 'crypto';
import { safeStorage } from 'electron';

// 密钥管理：优先使用 Electron safeStorage（系统级加密存储），降级到环境变量
let masterKey: Buffer | null = null;

function getMasterKey(): Buffer {
  if (masterKey) return masterKey;

  // 1. 尝试从 Electron safeStorage 读取
  try {
    // 如果是在 Electron 主进程中
    if (typeof safeStorage !== 'undefined' && safeStorage.isEncryptionAvailable()) {
      const encrypted = safeStorage.encryptString(Buffer.from('waos-master-key', 'utf-8'));
      // 实际生产应存储到某个文件或 electron-store
      // 这里简化：用固定盐派生，确保每次启动密钥一致
    }
  } catch (_) { /* 降级 */ }

  // 2. 降级：从环境变量读取（开发模式）
  const keyFromEnv = process.env.WAOS_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
  if (keyFromEnv) {
    masterKey = Buffer.from(keyFromEnv, 'hex');
    return masterKey;
  }

  // 3. 首次启动：生成一个固定密钥（基于机器指纹 / 用户目录）
  //    警告：这样不够安全，但比明文强。生产必须走 safeStorage 或用户输入密码。
  const fallbackKey = scryptSync('waos-static-salt-' + require('os').homedir(), 'salt', 32);
  masterKey = fallbackKey;
  return masterKey;
}

/**
 * AES-256-GCM 加密
 * 输出格式: iv:authTag:encrypted (Base64)
 */
export function encrypt(text: string): string {
  if (!text) return text;

  const key = getMasterKey();
  const iv = randomBytes(16);
  const cipher = createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);

  let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'base64');
  encrypted += cipher.final('base64');

  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag().toString('base64');
  return `${iv.toString('base64')}:${authTag}:${encrypted}`;
}

/**
 * AES-256-GCM 解密
 */
export function decrypt(encryptedText: string): string {
  if (!encryptedText || !encryptedText.includes(':')) {
    // 如果不是加密格式，可能是旧数据或明文，直接返回（兼容迁移）
    return encryptedText;
  }

  try {
    const key = getMasterKey();
    const parts = encryptedText.split(':');
    if (parts.length !== 3) return encryptedText;

    const iv = Buffer.from(parts[0], 'base64');
    const authTag = Buffer.from(parts[1], 'base64');
    const encrypted = parts[2];

    const decipher = createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    decipher.setAuthTag(authTag);

    let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, 'base64', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    return decrypted;
  } catch (_) {
    // 解密失败，返回原值（可能是未加密的旧数据）
    return encryptedText;
  }
}

/**
 * 判断字符串是否为加密格式
 */
export function isEncrypted(text: string): boolean {
  return !!text && text.includes(':') && text.split(':').length === 3;
}
```

---

#### 1.2 Prisma 自动加密中间件

如果你是 **Next.js + Prisma** 架构，在 `frontend/src/server/prisma.ts`（或 `prisma.ts`）中加入中间件：

```typescript
// frontend/src/server/prisma.ts
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { encrypt, decrypt, isEncrypted } from '@/lib/crypto';

const prisma = new PrismaClient();

// 需要加密的字段列表（按模型 + 字段名）
const ENCRYPTED_FIELDS = {
  Message: ['content', 'wxId'],
  Lead: ['name', 'wxId', 'phone', 'profile'],
  Comment: ['content', 'nickname', 'userId'],
  User: ['email', 'phone'],
} as const;

// 判断是否需要加密该字段
function shouldEncrypt(model: string, field: string): boolean {
  const fields = ENCRYPTED_FIELDS[model as keyof typeof ENCRYPTED_FIELDS];
  return fields ? fields.includes(field) : false;
}

// ✅ 写操作中间件：自动加密
prisma.$use(async (params, next) => {
  const model = params.model as string;
  const action = params.action;

  // 1. create / update / updateMany 时加密数据
  if (['create', 'update', 'updateMany', 'upsert'].includes(action)) {
    const args = params.args;
    if (args.data) {
      const encryptData = (obj: any) => {
        if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return;
        for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) {
          if (shouldEncrypt(model, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string' && obj[key]) {
            // 防止重复加密
            if (!isEncrypted(obj[key])) {
              obj[key] = encrypt(obj[key]);
            }
          }
        }
        // 嵌套处理 (create: { data: { ... } })
        if (obj.data) encryptData(obj.data);
        if (obj.create) encryptData(obj.create);
        if (obj.update) encryptData(obj.update);
      };
      encryptData(args.data);
    }
  }

  const result = await next(params);

  // 2. find / findMany / findUnique / findFirst 时解密数据
  if (['findUnique', 'findFirst', 'findMany', 'findUniqueOrThrow', 'findFirstOrThrow'].includes(action)) {
    if (result) {
      const decryptResult = (obj: any) => {
        if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return;
        for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) {
          if (shouldEncrypt(model, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string' && obj[key]) {
            obj[key] = decrypt(obj[key]);
          }
        }
        // 处理数组结果
        if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
          obj.forEach((item) => decryptResult(item));
        }
        // 处理嵌套 include/select
        if (obj.data) decryptResult(obj.data);
      };
      decryptResult(result);
    }
  }

  return result;
});

export default prisma;
```

---

#### 1.3 数据迁移脚本（加密已有数据）

创建一个独立的脚本 `scripts/encrypt-existing-data.ts`，在终端运行一次：

```typescript
// scripts/encrypt-existing-data.ts
import prisma from '../frontend/src/server/prisma';
import { encrypt, isEncrypted } from '../frontend/src/lib/crypto';

async function main() {
  console.log('🔐 开始加密已有 PII 数据...');

  // 1. 加密 Message 表
  const messages = await prisma.message.findMany();
  console.log(`📦 处理 ${messages.length} 条 Message...`);
  for (const msg of messages) {
    let updateData: any = {};
    if (msg.content && !isEncrypted(msg.content)) {
      updateData.content = encrypt(msg.content);
    }
    if (msg.wxId && !isEncrypted(msg.wxId)) {
      updateData.wxId = encrypt(msg.wxId);
    }
    if (Object.keys(updateData).length > 0) {
      await prisma.message.update({
        where: { id: msg.id },
        data: updateData,
      });
    }
  }

  // 2. 加密 Lead 表
  const leads = await prisma.lead.findMany();
  console.log(`📦 处理 ${leads.length} 条 Lead...`);
  for (const lead of leads) {
    let updateData: any = {};
    if (lead.name && !isEncrypted(lead.name)) updateData.name = encrypt(lead.name);
    if (lead.wxId && !isEncrypted(lead.wxId)) updateData.wxId = encrypt(lead.wxId);
    if (lead.phone && !isEncrypted(lead.phone)) updateData.phone = encrypt(lead.phone);
    if (lead.profile && typeof lead.profile === 'string' && !isEncrypted(lead.profile)) {
      // 如果 profile 是 JSON 字符串，先转对象再加密整段
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(lead.profile);
        updateData.profile = encrypt(JSON.stringify(parsed));
      } catch {
        updateData.profile = encrypt(lead.profile);
      }
    }
    if (Object.keys(updateData).length > 0) {
      await prisma.lead.update({
        where: { id: lead.id },
        data: updateData,
      });
    }
  }

  // 3. 加密 Comment 表
  const comments = await prisma.comment.findMany();
  console.log(`📦 处理 ${comments.length} 条 Comment...`);
  for (const c of comments) {
    let updateData: any = {};
    if (c.content && !isEncrypted(c.content)) updateData.content = encrypt(c.content);
    if (c.nickname && !isEncrypted(c.nickname)) updateData.nickname = encrypt(c.nickname);
    if (c.userId && !isEncrypted(c.userId)) updateData.userId = encrypt(c.userId);
    if (Object.keys(updateData).length > 0) {
      await prisma.comment.update({
        where: { id: c.id },
        data: updateData,
      });
    }
  }

  // 4. 加密 User 表（如果有）
  // ... 类似上面

  console.log('✅ 所有 PII 数据加密完成！');
  console.log('⚠️ 请确保 WAOS_ENCRYPTION_KEY 环境变量已设置，否则重启后无法解密！');
}

main()
  .catch((e) => {
    console.error('❌ 迁移失败:', e);
    process.exit(1);
  })
  .finally(async () => {
    await prisma.$disconnect();
  });
```

---

#### 1.4 密钥管理（关键！）

在 `.env` 文件中生成一个 64 位的十六进制密钥：

```bash
# 生成密钥命令（在终端执行）
node -e "console.log(require('crypto').randomBytes(32).toString('hex'))"

# 然后将输出结果填入 .env
WAOS_ENCRYPTION_KEY=你的64位密钥
```

**⚠️ 重要提醒**：
- 密钥丢失 = 数据永久不可读！把密钥备份到安全的地方（如 1Password）。
- 如果使用了 Electron `safeStorage`，密钥由系统管理，不需要存 `.env`。

---

### 📂 文件放置清单

| 文件 | 位置 |
|------|------|
| 加密工具 | `frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts` |
| Prisma 中间件 | `frontend/src/server/prisma.ts`（或合并到你的 `db.ts`） |
| 迁移脚本 | `scripts/encrypt-existing-data.ts` |

---

### 🚀 执行步骤

```bash
# 1. 生成密钥，写入 .env
echo "WAOS_ENCRYPTION_KEY=$(node -e "console.log(require('crypto').randomBytes(32).toString('hex'))")" >> .env

# 2. 把上面 3 个文件复制到项目中

# 3. 运行迁移（加密已有数据，这一步可能需要几分钟）
npx ts-node scripts/encrypt-existing-data.ts

# 4. 重启应用验证
npm run dev
```

---

### ✅ 验收标准

1. 打开 SQLite 数据库文件（用 DB Browser），查看 `messages` 表，`content` 字段应该是一串 `base64:...` 格式的乱码。
2. 打开应用界面，消息内容显示正常（解密成功）。
3. 新发一条消息，再次查看数据库，新内容也是密文。

### 2.2 全局类型定义

```typescript
// frontend/src/types/global.d.ts
declare global {
  // ===== 通用 =====
  type Nullable<T> = T | null;
  type Optional<T> = T | undefined;
  type JSONValue = string | number | boolean | null | JSONObject | JSONArray;
  type JSONObject = { [key: string]: JSONValue };
  type JSONArray = JSONValue[];

  // ===== API 响应 =====
  interface ApiResponse<T = unknown> {
    code: number;
    msg: string;
    data: T;
  }

  interface PaginatedResponse<T> {
    items: T[];
    total: number;
    page: number;
    pageSize: number;
    totalPages: number;
  }

  // ===== 消息 =====
  type MessageRole = 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system';
  type MessageSource = 'wechat' | 'douyin' | 'video' | 'manual';

  interface Message {
    id: string;
    wxId: string;
    role: MessageRole;
    content: string;
    source: MessageSource;
    leadId?: string;
    intentLabel?: string;
    safetyFiltered?: boolean;
    createdAt: Date;
  }

  // ===== CRM 线索 =====
  type LeadStage = 'NEW' | 'ENGAGED' | 'QUALIFIED' | 'HOT' | 'CONVERTED' | 'LOST';
  type LeadStatus = 'active' | 'paused' | 'archived';

  interface Lead {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    wxId: string;
    phone?: string;
    stage: LeadStage;
    status: LeadStatus;
    intentScore: number;
    valueScore: number;
    profile?: Record<string, unknown>;
    version: number;
    createdAt: Date;
    updatedAt: Date;
  }

  // ===== 评论 =====
  interface Comment {
    id: string;
    content: string;
    nickname: string;
    userId: string;
    platform: string;
    postId: string;
    intentScore: number;
    replyStatus: 'pending' | 'replied' | 'converted' | 'ignored';
    leadId?: string;
    createdAt: Date;
  }

  // ===== 人设 =====
  interface Persona {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    description: string;
    systemPrompt: string;
    temperature: number;
    maxTokens: number;
    forbiddenRules: string[];
    isActive: boolean;
    createdAt: Date;
    updatedAt: Date;
  }
}

export {}; // 使文件成为模块
```

#!/bin/bash
# scripts/type-fix.sh

echo "🔧 开始批量修复 TypeScript 类型问题..."

# 1. 自动添加返回类型

### 1.3 Redis 连接配置

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/redis.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';

// 单例 Redis 连接
let redisClient: Redis | null = null;

export function getRedisClient(): Redis {
  if (!redisClient) {
    redisClient = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || undefined,
      db: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_DB || '0'),
      maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
      retryStrategy: (times) => Math.min(times * 50, 2000),
      lazyConnect: true,
    });

    // 连接事件
    redisClient.on('connect', () => console.log('🔗 Redis connected'));
    redisClient.on('error', (err) => console.error('Redis error:', err));
    redisClient.on('close', () => console.log('Redis connection closed'));
  }
  return redisClient;
}

// 优雅关闭
export async function closeRedis(): Promise<void> {
  if (redisClient) {
    await redisClient.quit();
    redisClient = null;
  }
}
```

### 1.4 环境变量

REDIS_DB=0

## 📦 第 2 步：BullMQ 任务队列核心

### 2.1 队列定义

```typescript
// frontend/src/queues/index.ts
import { Queue, Worker, QueueEvents } from 'bullmq';
import { getRedisClient } from '@/lib/redis';

// ===== 队列名称枚举 =====
export const QueueNames = {
  MESSAGE: 'queue:messages',
  AI_CALL: 'queue:ai-calls',
  CRM_UPDATE: 'queue:crm-updates',
  FOLLOWUP: 'queue:followups',
  SYNC: 'queue:sync',
} as const;

export type QueueName = (typeof QueueNames)[keyof typeof QueueNames];

// ===== 任务类型定义 =====
export interface MessageTask {
  type: 'process_message';
  data: {
    messageId: string;
    wxId: string;
    content: string;
    source: string;
    leadId?: string;
  };
  priority: number; // 0-100，越高越优先
  delay?: number; // 延迟秒数
  retry?: number; // 重试次数
}

export interface AITask {
  type: 'generate_reply';
  data: {
    leadId: string;
    message: string;
    personaId: string;
  };
  priority: number;
}

export interface CRMUpdateTask {
  type: 'update_lead';
  data: {
    leadId: string;
    fields: Record<string, unknown>;
  };
  priority: number;
}

export interface FollowupTask {
  type: 'schedule_followup';
  data: {
    leadId: string;
    delaySeconds: number;
    message: string;
  };
  priority: number;
}

export type Task = MessageTask | AITask | CRMUpdateTask | FollowupTask;

// ===== 创建队列 =====
function createQueue(name: QueueName): Queue {
  return new Queue(name, {
    connection: getRedisClient(),
    defaultJobOptions: {
      attempts: 3,
      backoff: {
        type: 'exponential',
        delay: 1000,
      },
      removeOnComplete: 100, // 保留最近 100 个成功任务
      removeOnFail: 100, // 保留最近 100 个失败任务
    },
  });
}

// ===== 队列实例 =====
export const messageQueue = createQueue(QueueNames.MESSAGE);
export const aiQueue = createQueue(QueueNames.AI_CALL);
export const crmQueue = createQueue(QueueNames.CRM_UPDATE);
export const followupQueue = createQueue(QueueNames.FOLLOWUP);
export const syncQueue = createQueue(QueueNames.SYNC);

// ===== 队列事件监听 =====
export function setupQueueListeners(name: QueueName): QueueEvents {
  const events = new QueueEvents(name, { connection: getRedisClient() });

  events.on('completed', ({ jobId, returnvalue }) => {
    console.log(`✅ Job ${jobId} completed on ${name}`, returnvalue);
  });

  events.on('failed', ({ jobId, failedReason }) => {
    console.error(`❌ Job ${jobId} failed on ${name}:`, failedReason);
  });

  events.on('stalled', ({ jobId }) => {
    console.warn(`⚠️ Job ${jobId} stalled on ${name}`);
  });

  return events;
}

// ===== 清理队列（开发/测试用） =====
export async function cleanAllQueues(): Promise<void> {
  const queues = [messageQueue, aiQueue, crmQueue, followupQueue, syncQueue];
  await Promise.all(
    queues.map((q) => q.obliterate({ force: true }))
  );
  console.log('🧹 All queues cleaned');
}
```

### 2.2 任务入队工具

```typescript
// frontend/src/queues/enqueue.ts
import { messageQueue, aiQueue, crmQueue, followupQueue } from './index';
import type { MessageTask, AITask, CRMUpdateTask, FollowupTask } from './index';

// ===== 通用入队函数（带优先级） =====
export async function enqueueWithPriority<T extends Task>(
  queue: Queue,
  task: T,
  priority?: number
): Promise<string> {
  const jobId = `job_${task.type}_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7)}`;

  const job = await queue.add(task.type, task.data, {
    jobId,
    priority: priority ?? task.priority,
    delay: task.delay ?? 0,
    attempts: task.retry ?? 3,
  });

  console.log(`📦 Job ${job.id} enqueued to ${queue.name}`);
  return job.id;
}

// ===== 各业务入队函数 =====
export async function enqueueMessageTask(
  messageId: string,
  wxId: string,
  content: string,
  source: string,
  leadId?: string,
  priority: number = 50
): Promise<string> {
  return enqueueWithPriority(messageQueue, {
    type: 'process_message',
    data: { messageId, wxId, content, source, leadId },
    priority,
  });
}

export async function enqueueAITask(
  leadId: string,
  message: string,
  personaId: string,
  priority: number = 60
): Promise<string> {
  return enqueueWithPriority(aiQueue, {
    type: 'generate_reply',
    data: { leadId, message, personaId },
    priority,
  });
}

export async function enqueueCRMUpdate(
  leadId: string,
  fields: Record<string, unknown>,
  priority: number = 30
): Promise<string> {
  return enqueueWithPriority(crmQueue, {
    type: 'update_lead',
    data: { leadId, fields },
    priority,
  });
}

export async function enqueueFollowup(
  leadId: string,
  delaySeconds: number,
  message: string,
  priority: number = 20
): Promise<string> {
  return enqueueWithPriority(followupQueue, {
    type: 'schedule_followup',
    data: { leadId, delaySeconds, message },
    priority,
  });
}
```

---

## 📦 第 3 步：Worker 池实现

### 3.1 Worker 基类

```typescript
// frontend/src/workers/base.ts
import { Worker, Job } from 'bullmq';
import { getRedisClient } from '@/lib/redis';
import { QueueNames } from '@/queues';
import type { Task } from '@/queues';

export abstract class BaseWorker<T extends Task> {
  protected worker: Worker | null = null;
  protected queueName: QueueNames;

  constructor(queueName: QueueNames) {
    this.queueName = queueName;
  }

  abstract process(job: Job<T>): Promise<unknown>;

  start(concurrency: number = 5): void {
    if (this.worker) {
      console.warn(`Worker ${this.queueName} already running`);
      return;
    }

    this.worker = new Worker(
      this.queueName,
      async (job: Job<T>) => {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        try {
          console.log(`🔄 Processing job ${job.id} on ${this.queueName}`);
          const result = await this.process(job);
          console.log(`✅ Job ${job.id} completed in ${Date.now() - startTime}ms`);
          return result;
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(`❌ Job ${job.id} failed:`, error);
          throw error;
        }
      },
      {
        connection: getRedisClient(),
        concurrency,
        autorun: true,
        // 任务超时时间
        stalledInterval: 30000,
        maxStalledCount: 3,
      }
    );

    // 错误处理
    this.worker.on('error', (err) => {
      console.error(`Worker ${this.queueName} error:`, err);
    });

    console.log(`🚀 Worker ${this.queueName} started with concurrency ${concurrency}`);
  }

  async stop(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.worker) {
      await this.worker.close();
      this.worker = null;
      console.log(`🛑 Worker ${this.queueName} stopped`);
    }
  }

  async getStatus(): Promise<{ isRunning: boolean; count: number }> {
    if (!this.worker) {
      return { isRunning: false, count: 0 };
    }
    try {
      const count = await this.worker.getJobCounts();
      const total = Object.values(count).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
      return { isRunning: true, count: total };
    } catch {
      return { isRunning: false, count: 0 };
    }
  }
}
```

### 3.2 各业务 Worker 实现

```typescript
// frontend/src/workers/message.worker.ts
import { BaseWorker } from './base';
import { QueueNames } from '@/queues';
import type { MessageTask } from '@/queues';
import { enqueueAITask, enqueueCRMUpdate } from '@/queues/enqueue';
import { decrypt } from '@/lib/crypto';

// 导入原有引擎（重构后保留）
// import { WAOSXEngine } from '@/engine';

export class MessageWorker extends BaseWorker<MessageTask> {
  constructor() {
    super(QueueNames.MESSAGE);
  }

  async process(job: Job<MessageTask>): Promise<unknown> {
    const { messageId, wxId, content, source, leadId } = job.data;

    // 1. 解密消息内容
    const decryptedContent = decrypt(content);

    // 2. 调用原有意图识别
    // const intent = WAOSXEngine.detectIntent(decryptedContent);
    // 模拟：
    const intent = { type: 'PRICE', confidence: 0.95, urgency: 0.8 };

    // 3. 判断是否需要 AI 生成回复（高优先级）
    if (intent.type === 'PRICE' || intent.type === 'COMPLAINT') {
      // 查找该客户的人设
      const personaId = 'default_sales_persona';

      // 入队 AI 任务（高优先级，排到前面）
      await enqueueAITask(leadId || wxId, decryptedContent, personaId, 80);
    } else {
      // 低优先级消息，直接入队 AI（较低优先级）
      const personaId = 'default_sales_persona';
      await enqueueAITask(leadId || wxId, decryptedContent, personaId, 30);
    }

    // 4. 更新 CRM（异步，不阻塞）
    if (leadId) {
      await enqueueCRMUpdate(leadId, {
        lastMessageAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        intentType: intent.type,
        lastIntentConfidence: intent.confidence,
      });
    }

    return { processed: true, messageId, intent };
  }
}
```

```typescript
// frontend/src/workers/ai.worker.ts
import { BaseWorker } from './base';
import { QueueNames } from '@/queues';
import type { AITask } from '@/queues';
import { enqueueMessageTask } from '@/queues/enqueue';

// 模拟 AI 调用（实际接入真实 LLM）
async function callLLM(
  message: string,
  personaId: string,
  leadId: string
): Promise<{ reply: string; extracted: Record<string, unknown>; status: string }> {
  // 模拟延迟
  await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 1500));

  // 模拟策略选择
  const strategies = [
    'close_now',
    'soft_recovery',
    'reconnect_hook',
    'standard_reply',
  ];
  const strategy = strategies[Math.floor(Math.random() * strategies.length)];

  // 模拟话术生成
  const replies = {
    close_now: '李总，M9现车不多，今天定的话我申请内部试驾名额和万元补贴，您下午方便来吗？',
    soft_recovery: '理解的李总，买车确实得慎重。我不催您，这是最新的电车评测报告您留着参考。',
    reconnect_hook: '李总好久不见！上次听您说家里两个娃，最近新出了个儿童安全座椅评测，发给您看看？',
    standard_reply: '收到，我马上发您配置单。',
  };

  return {
    reply: replies[strategy] || replies.standard_reply,
    extracted: { strategy, intent: 'PRICE' },
    status: strategy === 'close_now' ? 'HOT' : 'ENGAGED',
  };
}

export class AIWorker extends BaseWorker<AITask> {
  constructor() {
    super(QueueNames.AI_CALL);
  }

  async process(job: Job<AITask>): Promise<unknown> {
    const { leadId, message, personaId } = job.data;

    // 1. 调用 LLM
    const result = await callLLM(message, personaId, leadId);

    // 2. 如果生成了回复，入队消息发送
    if (result.reply) {
      await enqueueMessageTask(
        `ai_reply_${Date.now()}`,
        leadId,
        result.reply,
        'ai',
        leadId,
        60 // 发送消息较高优先级
      );
    }

    // 3. 更新 CRM
    if (result.status) {
      // await enqueueCRMUpdate(leadId, { status: result.status });
    }

    return result;
  }
}
```

import { BaseWorker } from './base';
import { QueueNames } from '@/queues';
import type { FollowupTask } from '@/queues';

export class FollowupWorker extends BaseWorker<FollowupTask> {
  constructor() {
    super(QueueNames.FOLLOWUP);
  }

  async process(job: Job<FollowupTask>): Promise<unknown> {
    const { leadId, delaySeconds, message } = job.data;

    // 等待指定时间（BullMQ 已经支持延迟，这里只是二次确认）
    console.log(`⏳ Followup for ${leadId} after ${delaySeconds}s`);

    // 发送跟进消息
    await enqueueMessageTask(
      `followup_${Date.now()}`,
      leadId,
      message,
      'followup',
      leadId,
      40
    );

    return { sent: true, leadId };
  }
}

```typescript
// frontend/src/workers/index.ts
import { MessageWorker } from './message.worker';
import { AIWorker } from './ai.worker';
import { FollowupWorker } from './followup.worker';
import { getRedisClient } from '@/lib/redis';

// ===== 所有 Worker 单例 =====
let messageWorker: MessageWorker | null = null;
let aiWorker: AIWorker | null = null;
let followupWorker: FollowupWorker | null = null;

// ===== 启动所有 Worker =====
export function startAllWorkers(concurrency: number = 5): void {
  // 确保 Redis 连接
  getRedisClient();

  messageWorker = new MessageWorker();
  messageWorker.start(concurrency);

  aiWorker = new AIWorker();
  aiWorker.start(Math.max(2, Math.floor(concurrency / 2)));

  followupWorker = new FollowupWorker();
  followupWorker.start(2);

  console.log(`🚀 All workers started with base concurrency ${concurrency}`);
}

// ===== 停止所有 Worker =====
export async function stopAllWorkers(): Promise<void> {
  const workers = [messageWorker, aiWorker, followupWorker];
  await Promise.all(
    workers.filter((w) => w !== null).map((w) => w!.stop())
  );
  console.log('🛑 All workers stopped');
}

// ===== 获取 Worker 状态 =====
export async function getAllWorkerStatus() {
  const workers = {
    message: messageWorker,
    ai: aiWorker,
    followup: followupWorker,
  };

  const status: Record<string, { isRunning: boolean; count: number }> = {};
  for (const [name, worker] of Object.entries(workers)) {
    if (worker) {
      status[name] = await worker.getStatus();
    }
  }
  return status;
}
```

## 📦 第 4 步：Redis 缓存层

### 4.1 缓存管理器

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/cache.ts
import { getRedisClient } from './redis';

const CACHE_TTL = {
  LEAD: 3600, // 1 小时
  PERSONA: 86400, // 24 小时
  KNOWLEDGE: 3600, // 1 小时
  CONFIG: 600, // 10 分钟
} as const;

type CacheKey = `cache:${string}:${string}`;

export class CacheManager {
  private redis = getRedisClient();

  // ===== 通用 Get/Set =====
  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      const data = await this.redis.get(key);
      if (!data) return null;
      return JSON.parse(data) as T;
    } catch {
      return null;
    }
  }

  async set<T>(
    key: string,
    value: T,
    ttl: number = CACHE_TTL.LEAD
  ): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await this.redis.set(key, JSON.stringify(value), 'EX', ttl);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Cache set error for ${key}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async del(key: string): Promise<void> {
    await this.redis.del(key);
  }

  async exists(key: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const result = await this.redis.exists(key);
    return result === 1;
  }

  // ===== 批量操作 =====
  async mget<T>(keys: string[]): Promise<(T | null)[]> {
    if (keys.length === 0) return [];
    try {
      const values = await this.redis.mget(keys);
      return values.map((v) => (v ? JSON.parse(v) : null));
    } catch {
      return keys.map(() => null);
    }
  }

  async mset<T>(entries: Array<[string, T]>, ttl: number = CACHE_TTL.LEAD): Promise<void> {
    if (entries.length === 0) return;
    try {
      const pipeline = this.redis.pipeline();
      for (const [key, value] of entries) {
        pipeline.set(key, JSON.stringify(value), 'EX', ttl);
      }
      await pipeline.exec();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Cache mset error:', error);
    }
  }

  // ===== 模式匹配删除 =====
  async deletePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const keys = await this.redis.keys(pattern);
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        await this.redis.del(keys);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Cache delete pattern error for ${pattern}:`, error);
    }
  }

  // ===== 统计 =====
  async getStats(): Promise<{ totalKeys: number; memoryUsage: number }> {
    try {
      const [keys, info] = await Promise.all([
        this.redis.keys('cache:*'),
        this.redis.info('memory'),
      ]);
      const memoryMatch = info.match(/used_memory:(\d+)/);
      return {
        totalKeys: keys.length,
        memoryUsage: memoryMatch ? parseInt(memoryMatch[1]) / 1024 / 1024 : 0,
      };
    } catch {
      return { totalKeys: 0, memoryUsage: 0 };
    }
  }
}

export const cache = new CacheManager();
```

### 4.2 业务缓存装饰器

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/cache-decorators.ts
import { cache } from './cache';

// ===== 缓存装饰器（用于函数） =====
export function cached<T>(
  keyPrefix: string,
  ttl?: number
): (
  target: unknown,
  propertyKey: string,
  descriptor: TypedPropertyDescriptor<(...args: unknown[]) => Promise<T>>
) => TypedPropertyDescriptor<(...args: unknown[]) => Promise<T>> {
  return function (
    _target: unknown,
    _propertyKey: string,
    descriptor: TypedPropertyDescriptor<(...args: unknown[]) => Promise<T>>
  ) {
    const originalMethod = descriptor.value!;

    descriptor.value = async function (...args: unknown[]): Promise<T> {
      // 生成缓存键
      const key = `cache:${keyPrefix}:${JSON.stringify(args)}`;

      // 检查缓存
      const cachedResult = await cache.get<T>(key);
      if (cachedResult !== null) {
        return cachedResult;
      }

      // 执行原函数
      const result = await originalMethod.apply(this, args);

      // 存入缓存
      if (result !== null && result !== undefined) {
        await cache.set(key, result, ttl);
      }

      return result;
    };

    return descriptor;
  };
}

// ===== 使用示例 =====
// @cached('lead', 3600)
// async function getLead(id: string): Promise<Lead> { ... }
```

## 📦 第 6 步：监控 Dashboard

### 6.1 队列监控 API

```typescript
// frontend/src/app/api/queue/status/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { messageQueue, aiQueue, crmQueue, followupQueue, syncQueue } from '@/queues';
import { getAllWorkerStatus } from '@/workers';
import { cache } from '@/lib/cache';

export async function GET() {
  try {
    // 获取队列状态
    const [message, ai, crm, followup, sync] = await Promise.all([
      messageQueue.getJobCounts(),
      aiQueue.getJobCounts(),
      crmQueue.getJobCounts(),
      followupQueue.getJobCounts(),
      syncQueue.getJobCounts(),
    ]);

    // 获取 Worker 状态
    const workers = await getAllWorkerStatus();

    // 获取缓存统计
    const cacheStats = await cache.getStats();

    return NextResponse.json({
      queues: {
        message,
        ai,
        crm,
        followup,
        sync,
      },
      workers,
      cache: cacheStats,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: String(error) },
      { status: 500 }
    );
  }
}
```

### 6.2 UI 队列监控面板

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/QueueMonitor.tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useWebSocket } from '@/hooks/useWebSocket';

interface QueueStatus {
  queues: Record<string, Record<string, number>>;
  workers: Record<string, { isRunning: boolean; count: number }>;
  cache: { totalKeys: number; memoryUsage: number };
}

export function QueueMonitor() {
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<QueueStatus | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchQueueStatus();
    const interval = setInterval(fetchQueueStatus, 5000);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  async function fetchQueueStatus() {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/queue/status');
      const data = await res.json();
      setStatus(data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch queue status:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return <div>加载中...</div>;
  }

  if (!status) {
    return <div>无法获取队列状态</div>;
  }

  const totalQueueSize = Object.values(status.queues).reduce(
    (acc, q) => acc + Object.values(q).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0),
    0
  );

  return (
    <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
      <h2 className="text-lg font-bold">📊 系统运行状态</h2>

      {/* 汇总卡片 */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5">
          <div className="text-sm text-white/60">队列总任务</div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{totalQueueSize}</div>
        </div>
        <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5">
          <div className="text-sm text-white/60">缓存条目</div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{status.cache.totalKeys}</div>
        </div>
        <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5">
          <div className="text-sm text-white/60">缓存内存</div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">
            {status.cache.memoryUsage.toFixed(1)} MB
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="p-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5">
          <div className="text-sm text-white/60">Worker</div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-400">
            {Object.values(status.workers).filter((w) => w.isRunning).length} 运行中
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 详细队列状态 */}
      <div className="space-y-2">
        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/60">队列详情</h3>
        {Object.entries(status.queues).map(([name, counts]) => {
          const total = Object.values(counts).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
          return (
            <div key={name} className="flex items-center gap-4 p-2 rounded bg-white/5">
              <span className="text-sm font-mono w-20">{name}</span>
              <div className="flex-1 h-2 rounded-full bg-white/10 overflow-hidden">
                <div
                  className="h-full bg-blue-500 transition-all"
                  style={{ width: `${Math.min(total / 100 * 100, 100)}%` }}
                />
              </div>
              <span className="text-sm text-white/60">{total} 个任务</span>
              <span className="text-xs text-white/30">
                {Object.entries(counts)
                  .filter(([, v]) => v > 0)
                  .map(([k, v]) => `${k}:${v}`)
                  .join(' ')}
              </span>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Worker 状态 */}
      <div className="space-y-2">
        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/60">Worker 状态</h3>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
          {Object.entries(status.workers).map(([name, info]) => (
            <div
              key={name}
              className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-sm ${
                info.isRunning
                  ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400'
                  : 'bg-red-500/20 text-red-400'
              }`}
            >
              {name}: {info.isRunning ? '🟢 运行中' : '🔴 已停止'}
              {info.isRunning && ` (${info.count} 个任务)`}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## ✅ 验收标准

- [ ] Redis 连接成功 (`redis-cli ping` 返回 PONG)
- [ ] 启动应用后，所有 Worker 自动启动
- [ ] 收到消息后，任务进入 BullMQ 队列
- [ ] Worker 自动从队列拉取并处理任务
- [ ] 高优先级任务（HOT 客户）先执行
- [ ] 延迟任务（跟进）在指定时间后执行
- [ ] 任务失败自动重试（最多 3 次）
- [ ] 队列监控页面能查看所有队列状态
- [ ] 缓存生效（第二次查询同数据速度提升 > 50%）

---

老板，Sprint 3 的 4 个包全部在这里了。这一步做完，你的系统就**从“单线程排队”变成“并发处理、秒回客户”了**。

跑完告诉我，**我们接着做 Sprint 4：可观测性（Sentry + 结构化日志 + 自动备份）** —— 让你的系统出问题能追踪、崩溃能恢复、数据永不丢。

## 📦 第 1 步：结构化日志系统

### 1.1 安装依赖

```bash
# 主项目
npm install pino pino-pretty pino-http

# 类型
npm install -D @types/pino
```

### 1.2 日志核心模块

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/logger.ts
import pino from 'pino';

// ===== 日志级别 =====
const LOG_LEVEL = process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info';

// ===== 敏感字段列表（自动脱敏） =====
const SENSITIVE_FIELDS = [
  'password',
  'token',
  'apiKey',
  'api_key',
  'secret',
  'authorization',
  'cookie',
  'wxId',
  'phone',
  'email',
  'content',
  'profile',
];

// ===== 脱敏函数 =====
function redactSensitive(data: unknown): unknown {
  if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;

  const redacted = Array.isArray(data) ? [...data] : { ...data };

  for (const key of Object.keys(redacted)) {
    if (SENSITIVE_FIELDS.includes(key)) {
      redacted[key] = '[REDACTED]';
    } else if (typeof redacted[key] === 'object' && redacted[key] !== null) {
      redacted[key] = redactSensitive(redacted[key]);
    }
  }

  return redacted;
}

// ===== 创建 Logger =====
const baseLogger = pino({
  level: LOG_LEVEL,
  // 生产环境输出纯 JSON，开发环境输出可读格式
  transport:
    process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'
      ? undefined
      : {
          target: 'pino-pretty',
          options: {
            colorize: true,
            translateTime: 'SYS:standard',
            ignore: 'pid,hostname',
          },
        },
  timestamp: pino.stdTimeFunctions.isoTime,
  redact: {
    paths: SENSITIVE_FIELDS.map((f) => `*.${f}`),
    censor: '[REDACTED]',
  },
  serializers: {
    err: pino.stdSerializers.err,
    req: (req) => ({
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      headers: redactSensitive(req.headers),
      query: req.query,
      params: req.params,
    }),
    res: (res) => ({
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      headers: redactSensitive(res.headers),
    }),
  },
});

// ===== 带上下文的 Logger 包装 =====
export class Logger {
  private child: pino.Logger;

  constructor(context?: Record<string, unknown>) {
    this.child = context ? baseLogger.child(context) : baseLogger;
  }

  // ===== 基础方法 =====
  debug(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    this.child.debug(data, message);
  }

  info(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    this.child.info(data, message);
  }

  warn(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    this.child.warn(data, message);
  }

  error(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    this.child.error(data, message);
  }

  fatal(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    this.child.fatal(data, message);
  }

  // ===== 带异常的错误日志 =====
  errorWithException(message: string, error: unknown, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    if (error instanceof Error) {
      this.child.error(
        {
          err: {
            message: error.message,
            stack: error.stack,
            name: error.name,
            ...(error as Record<string, unknown>),
          },
          ...data,
        },
        message
      );
    } else {
      this.child.error({ err: String(error), ...data }, message);
    }
  }

  // ===== 子 Logger（带继承上下文） =====
  child(context: Record<string, unknown>): Logger {
    return new Logger({ ...this.child.bindings(), ...context });
  }

  // ===== 性能计时 =====
  time(label: string): () => void {
    const start = process.hrtime.bigint();
    return () => {
      const end = process.hrtime.bigint();
      const duration = Number(end - start) / 1_000_000;
      this.debug(`⏱️ ${label}`, { duration: `${duration.toFixed(2)}ms` });
    };
  }
}

// ===== 默认导出 =====
export const logger = new Logger({ service: 'waos' });

// ===== 请求日志中间件（用于 Next.js API） =====
export function withLogging<T extends (...args: unknown[]) => unknown>(
  handler: T,
  name: string
): T {
  return (async (...args: unknown[]) => {
    const req = args[0] as Request;
    const logger = new Logger({
      requestId: crypto.randomUUID(),
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      handler: name,
    });

    logger.info(`📥 ${req.method} ${req.url}`);

    const endTimer = logger.time(`handler:${name}`);

    try {
      const result = await handler(...args);
      endTimer();
      logger.info(`📤 ${req.method} ${req.url} - 200`);
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      endTimer();
      logger.errorWithException(`❌ ${req.method} ${req.url}`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }) as T;
}
```

### 1.3 请求日志中间件（Next.js）

```typescript
// frontend/src/middleware.ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import type { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { logger } from '@/lib/logger';

export function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
  // 生成请求 ID
  const requestId = crypto.randomUUID();

  // 只记录 API 请求
  if (request.nextUrl.pathname.startsWith('/api/')) {
    const start = Date.now();

    // 响应拦截（需要响应后记录，但 Next.js middleware 不支持响应后处理）
    // 改用 logger 记录请求开始
    logger.debug(`📥 ${request.method} ${request.nextUrl.pathname}`, {
      requestId,
      query: Object.fromEntries(request.nextUrl.searchParams),
    });
  }

  const response = NextResponse.next();
  response.headers.set('X-Request-ID', requestId);
  return response;
}

export const config = {
  matcher: '/api/:path*',
};
```

// frontend/src/lib/logger-file.ts
import { createWriteStream } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';
import { mkdirSync } from 'fs';
import pino from 'pino';

const LOG_DIR = join(process.cwd(), 'logs');

// 确保日志目录存在
try {
  mkdirSync(LOG_DIR, { recursive: true });
} catch (_) {
  // 目录已存在
}

// ===== 文件日志配置 =====
const fileTransport = pino.transport({
  targets: [
    {
      target: 'pino/file',
      options: {
        destination: join(LOG_DIR, 'app.log'),
        mkdir: true,
      },
      level: 'info',
    },
    {
      target: 'pino/file',
      options: {
        destination: join(LOG_DIR, 'error.log'),
        mkdir: true,
      },
      level: 'error',
    },
  ],
});

export const fileLogger = pino(
  {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    timestamp: pino.stdTimeFunctions.isoTime,
    redact: {
      paths: ['*.password', '*.token', '*.apiKey', '*.wxId', '*.content'],
      censor: '[REDACTED]',
    },
  },
  fileTransport
);

// ===== 日志轮转（每日切割） =====
// 实际生产可用 pino-roll 或 logrotate
// 这里用简单方案：每次启动检查文件大小
export function checkLogRotation(): void {
  try {
    const stats = require('fs').statSync(join(LOG_DIR, 'app.log'));
    const sizeInMB = stats.size / 1024 / 1024;
    if (sizeInMB > 100) {
      // 如果超过 100MB，备份并清空
      const backupName = join(
        LOG_DIR,
        `app-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)}.log`
      );
      require('fs').renameSync(join(LOG_DIR, 'app.log'), backupName);
      console.log(`📦 Log rotated: ${backupName}`);
    }
  } catch (_) {
    // 文件不存在，忽略
  }
}

### 2.2 Sentry 初始化（Next.js）

```typescript
// frontend/sentry.client.config.ts
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/nextjs';

Sentry.init({
  dsn: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN,
  environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
  tracesSampleRate: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 0.1 : 1.0,
  replaysSessionSampleRate: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 0.1 : 1.0,
  replaysOnErrorSampleRate: 1.0,

  // 自动捕获性能数据
  enableTracing: true,

  // 自动捕获未处理的 Promise 异常
  beforeSend(event) {
    // 脱敏：移除敏感数据
    if (event.request) {
      if (event.request.headers) {
        delete event.request.headers.authorization;
        delete event.request.headers.cookie;
      }
      if (event.request.data) {
        // 移除敏感字段
        const sensitive = ['password', 'token', 'apiKey', 'wxId'];
        if (typeof event.request.data === 'object') {
          for (const key of sensitive) {
            delete event.request.data[key];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return event;
  },
});
```

### 2.3 Sentry 初始化（Electron 主进程）

```typescript
// electron/sentry.ts
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/electron';

export function initSentry(): void {
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
    console.log('🔍 Sentry disabled in development');
    return;
  }

  Sentry.init({
    dsn: process.env.ELECTRON_SENTRY_DSN,
    environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
    release: process.env.npm_package_version,

    // Electron 特定配置
    integrations: [
      new Sentry.Integrations.Breadcrumbs({
        console: true,
        dom: false,
        fetch: true,
        history: false,
        sentry: true,
        xhr: true,
      }),
    ],

    // 捕获 native 崩溃
    crashReporter: {
      submitURL: 'https://sentry.io/api/...',
    },
  });

  console.log('🔒 Sentry initialized for Electron');
}

// ===== 自定义错误上报 =====
export function reportError(error: Error, context?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
    console.error('[DEV]', error, context);
    return;
  }

  Sentry.withScope((scope) => {
    if (context) {
      scope.setContext('context', context);
    }
    Sentry.captureException(error);
  });
}

// ===== 性能监控 =====
export function startTransaction(name: string, op: string): Sentry.Span {
  return Sentry.startSpan({ name, op });
}
```

### 2.4 在 Electron 主进程中集成 Sentry

```typescript
// electron/main.js 或 main.ts
import { initSentry, reportError } from './sentry';
import { logger } from '../frontend/src/lib/logger';

// 应用启动时初始化
app.whenReady().then(() => {
  initSentry();

  // ... 原有代码 ...

  // 全局未捕获异常
  process.on('uncaughtException', (error) => {
    logger.errorWithException('Uncaught exception in main process', error);
    reportError(error, { process: 'main' });
  });

  process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason) => {
    const error = reason instanceof Error ? reason : new Error(String(reason));
    logger.errorWithException('Unhandled rejection in main process', error);
    reportError(error, { process: 'main', reason });
  });
});
```

### 2.5 React 错误边界

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx
import { Component, ReactNode } from 'react';
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/nextjs';

interface Props {
  children: ReactNode;
  fallback?: ReactNode;
}

interface State {
  hasError: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
}

export class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
  constructor(props: Props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
  }

  static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
    return { hasError: true, error };
  }

  componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: React.ErrorInfo): void {
    Sentry.withScope((scope) => {
      scope.setContext('react', {
        componentStack: errorInfo.componentStack,
      });
      Sentry.captureException(error);
    });
    console.error('React Error Boundary caught:', error, errorInfo);
  }

  render(): ReactNode {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      if (this.props.fallback) {
        return this.props.fallback;
      }

      return (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-screen p-8 text-center">
          <div className="text-4xl mb-4">😵</div>
          <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-2">出问题了</h2>
          <p className="text-white/60 mb-4">系统遇到了一些问题，我们已记录并会尽快修复</p>
          <button
            onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
            className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600 transition"
          >
            刷新页面重试
          </button>
          <details className="mt-4 text-xs text-white/30 max-w-md">
            <summary>错误详情</summary>
            <pre className="mt-2 text-left whitespace-pre-wrap break-all">
              {this.state.error?.message}
            </pre>
          </details>
        </div>
      );
    }

    return this.props.children;
  }
}
```

## 📦 第 3 步：数据库自动备份

### 3.1 备份脚本

```typescript
// scripts/backup-db.ts
#!/usr/bin/env node
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import { createWriteStream, existsSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';
import { pipeline } from 'stream';
import { promisify as streamPromisify } from 'stream';
import { createGzip } from 'zlib';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);
const pipelineAsync = streamPromisify(pipeline);

const DB_PATH = process.env.DATABASE_PATH || 'prisma/dev.db';
const BACKUP_DIR = process.env.BACKUP_DIR || join(process.cwd(), 'backups');
const RETENTION_DAYS = parseInt(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_DAYS || '7');

// 确保备份目录存在
if (!existsSync(BACKUP_DIR)) {
  mkdirSync(BACKUP_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

async function backupDatabase(): Promise<string> {
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
  const backupFileName = `db-backup-${timestamp}.sqlite.gz`;
  const backupPath = join(BACKUP_DIR, backupFileName);

  console.log(`📦 开始备份数据库到: ${backupPath}`);

  // 1. 使用 sqlite3 导出 SQL
  const { stdout } = await execAsync(
    `sqlite3 ${DB_PATH} .dump`
  );

  // 2. 写入 gzip 压缩文件
  const writeStream = createWriteStream(backupPath);
  const gzip = createGzip();

  await pipelineAsync(
    async function* source() {
      yield stdout;
    }(),
    gzip,
    writeStream
  );

  console.log(`✅ 备份完成: ${backupPath} (${(writeStream.bytesWritten / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB)`);
  return backupPath;
}

async function cleanOldBackups(): Promise<void> {
  const { readdir, stat, unlink } = await import('fs/promises');
  const files = await readdir(BACKUP_DIR);

  const now = Date.now();
  const retentionMs = RETENTION_DAYS * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

  let deletedCount = 0;

  for (const file of files) {
    if (!file.startsWith('db-backup-')) continue;

    const filePath = join(BACKUP_DIR, file);
    const stats = await stat(filePath);

    if (now - stats.mtimeMs > retentionMs) {
      await unlink(filePath);
      deletedCount++;
      console.log(`🗑️ 删除旧备份: ${file}`);
    }
  }

  if (deletedCount > 0) {
    console.log(`🧹 清理了 ${deletedCount} 个旧备份`);
  }
}

async function main() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 开始数据库备份任务');
    console.log(`📁 数据库路径: ${DB_PATH}`);
    console.log(`📁 备份目录: ${BACKUP_DIR}`);
    console.log(`📁 保留天数: ${RETENTION_DAYS}`);

    await backupDatabase();
    await cleanOldBackups();

    console.log('✅ 备份任务完成');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ 备份失败:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

main();
```

### 3.2 定时任务配置

```typescript
// scripts/schedule-backup.ts
import cron from 'node-cron';
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import { logger } from '../frontend/src/lib/logger';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);

// 每天凌晨 2:00 执行备份
const BACKUP_SCHEDULE = '0 2 * * *';

export function startBackupScheduler(): void {
  logger.info(`🕐 启动备份调度器: ${BACKUP_SCHEDULE}`);

  cron.schedule(BACKUP_SCHEDULE, async () => {
    logger.info('📦 执行定时备份...');

    try {
      const { stdout, stderr } = await execAsync(
        'npx ts-node scripts/backup-db.ts'
      );

      if (stderr) {
        logger.warn('备份警告', { stderr });
      }

      logger.info('✅ 定时备份完成', { stdout });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.errorWithException('❌ 定时备份失败', error);
    }
  });
}

// 如果是独立运行
if (require.main === module) {
  startBackupScheduler();
  console.log('🔄 备份调度器已启动，按 Ctrl+C 停止');
}
```

### 3.3 在 Electron 主进程中启动备份调度

```typescript

app.whenReady().then(() => {
  // ... 原有代码 ...

  }

```

### 3.4 备份恢复脚本

```typescript
// scripts/restore-db.ts
#!/usr/bin/env node
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import { createReadStream, existsSync } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';
import { pipeline } from 'stream';
import { promisify as streamPromisify } from 'stream';
import { createGunzip } from 'zlib';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);
const pipelineAsync = streamPromisify(pipeline);

const DB_PATH = process.env.DATABASE_PATH || 'prisma/dev.db';

async function restoreDatabase(backupFile: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!existsSync(backupFile)) {
    throw new Error(`备份文件不存在: ${backupFile}`);
  }

  console.log(`🔄 从备份恢复: ${backupFile}`);

  // 1. 解压备份文件
  const gunzip = createGunzip();
  const readStream = createReadStream(backupFile);

  let sqlContent = '';
  await pipelineAsync(
    readStream,
    gunzip,
    async function* sink(source: AsyncIterable<string>) {
      for await (const chunk of source) {
        sqlContent += chunk;
      }
    }()
  );

  // 2. 写入数据库
  const tempSqlFile = '/tmp/restore.sql';
  const { writeFile } = await import('fs/promises');
  await writeFile(tempSqlFile, sqlContent);

  // 3. 执行恢复
  await execAsync(`sqlite3 ${DB_PATH} < ${tempSqlFile}`);

  // 4. 清理临时文件
  const { unlink } = await import('fs/promises');
  await unlink(tempSqlFile);

  console.log('✅ 数据库恢复完成');
}

// 命令行使用
const backupFile = process.argv[2];
if (!backupFile) {
  console.error('用法: npx ts-node scripts/restore-db.ts <backup-file>');
  process.exit(1);
}

restoreDatabase(backupFile).catch((error) => {
  console.error('❌ 恢复失败:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});
```

## 📦 第 4 步：集成到监控面板

### 4.1 系统健康状态 API

```typescript
// frontend/src/app/api/health/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { logger } from '@/lib/logger';
import { getRedisClient } from '@/lib/redis';
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import { existsSync } from 'fs';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);

interface HealthStatus {
  status: 'healthy' | 'degraded' | 'unhealthy';
  timestamp: string;
  services: {
    database: { status: 'up' | 'down'; message?: string };
    redis: { status: 'up' | 'down'; message?: string };
    disk: { status: 'up' | 'down'; free: string; total: string };
    memory: { usage: number; total: number };
  };
  version: string;
}

export async function GET(): Promise<NextResponse> {
  const status: HealthStatus = {
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    services: {
      database: { status: 'down' },
      redis: { status: 'down' },
      disk: { status: 'down', free: '0', total: '0' },
      memory: { usage: 0, total: 0 },
    },
    version: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0',
  };

  // 1. 检查数据库
  try {
    const { stdout } = await execAsync(
      `sqlite3 ${process.env.DATABASE_PATH || 'prisma/dev.db'} "SELECT 1;"`
    );
    if (stdout.trim() === '1') {
      status.services.database.status = 'up';
    }
  } catch (error) {
    status.services.database.message = String(error);
    status.status = 'degraded';
  }

  // 2. 检查 Redis
  try {
    const redis = getRedisClient();
    const pong = await redis.ping();
    if (pong === 'PONG') {
      status.services.redis.status = 'up';
    }
  } catch (error) {
    status.services.redis.message = String(error);
    status.status = 'degraded';
  }

  // 3. 检查磁盘
  try {
    const { stdout } = await execAsync('df -h /');
    const lines = stdout.split('\n');
    const dataLine = lines[1];
    if (dataLine) {
      const parts = dataLine.split(/\s+/);
      status.services.disk.status = 'up';
      status.services.disk.total = parts[1] || '0';
      status.services.disk.free = parts[3] || '0';

      // 如果可用空间小于 10%，标记为降级
      const freeGB = parseFloat(status.services.disk.free.replace('G', ''));
      if (freeGB < 10) {
        status.status = 'degraded';
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    status.services.disk.message = String(error);
  }

  // 4. 检查内存
  try {
    const { stdout } = await execAsync('free -m');
    const lines = stdout.split('\n');
    const memLine = lines[1];
    if (memLine) {
      const parts = memLine.split(/\s+/);
      status.services.memory.total = parseInt(parts[1] || '0');
      const used = parseInt(parts[2] || '0');
      status.services.memory.usage = Math.round((used / status.services.memory.total) * 100);

      if (status.services.memory.usage > 90) {
        status.status = 'degraded';
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    // 内存检查失败不影响整体状态
  }

  // 如果任何关键服务挂了，标记为不健康
  if (status.services.database.status === 'down') {
    status.status = 'unhealthy';
  }

  // 记录检查结果
  logger.info('Health check completed', { status: status.status });

  return NextResponse.json(status);
}
```

### 4.2 健康检查监控组件

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/HealthMonitor.tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

interface HealthStatus {
  status: 'healthy' | 'degraded' | 'unhealthy';
  timestamp: string;
  services: {
    database: { status: 'up' | 'down'; message?: string };
    redis: { status: 'up' | 'down'; message?: string };
    disk: { status: 'up' | 'down'; free: string; total: string };
    memory: { usage: number; total: number };
  };
  version: string;
}

export function HealthMonitor() {
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<HealthStatus | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchHealth();
    const interval = setInterval(fetchHealth, 30000); // 每 30 秒检查一次
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  async function fetchHealth() {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/health');
      const data = await res.json();
      setStatus(data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Health check failed:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="text-sm text-white/40">检查服务状态...</div>;
  }

  if (!status) {
    return <div className="text-sm text-red-400">无法获取健康状态</div>;
  }

  const statusColor =
    status.status === 'healthy'
      ? 'text-green-400'
      : status.status === 'degraded'
      ? 'text-yellow-400'
      : 'text-red-400';

  const statusEmoji =
    status.status === 'healthy'
      ? '🟢'
      : status.status === 'degraded'
      ? '🟡'
      : '🔴';

  const serviceStatus = (s: 'up' | 'down') =>
    s === 'up' ? '🟢' : '🔴';

  return (
    <div className="p-4 space-y-3 rounded-lg bg-white/5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <span className="text-sm font-medium">系统健康</span>
        <span className={`text-sm font-bold ${statusColor}`}>
          {statusEmoji} {status.status.toUpperCase()}
        </span>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span>{serviceStatus(status.services.database.status)}</span>
          <span className="text-white/60">数据库</span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span>{serviceStatus(status.services.redis.status)}</span>
          <span className="text-white/60">Redis</span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span>💾</span>
          <span className="text-white/60">
            磁盘 {status.services.disk.free} / {status.services.disk.total}
          </span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span>🧠</span>
          <span className="text-white/60">
            内存 {status.services.memory.usage}%
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="text-xs text-white/30">
        版本 v{status.version} · {new Date(status.timestamp).toLocaleString()}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

# 5. 创建备份目录

### 1.3 依赖分析脚本

```typescript
// scripts/analyze-size.ts
#!/usr/bin/env node

import { execSync } from 'child_process';
import { readdirSync, statSync, readFileSync } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';

console.log('📊 WAOS 打包体积分析');
console.log('═'.repeat(60));

// 1. 分析 node_modules
const nodeModulesPath = join(process.cwd(), 'node_modules');
const packages: Record<string, number> = {};

function walkDir(dir: string, prefix: string = ''): void {
  try {
    const items = readdirSync(dir);
    for (const item of items) {
      if (item.startsWith('.')) continue;
      const fullPath = join(dir, item);
      const stats = statSync(fullPath);
      if (stats.isDirectory()) {
        walkDir(fullPath, join(prefix, item));
      } else if (item === 'package.json') {
        try {
          const pkg = JSON.parse(readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8'));
          const name = pkg.name || prefix;
          const size = stats.size;
          if (!packages[name]) {
            packages[name] = 0;
          }
          packages[name] += size;
        } catch (_) {
          // 忽略解析错误
        }
      }
    }
  } catch (_) {
    // 忽略权限错误
  }
}

console.log('📁 扫描 node_modules 目录...');
walkDir(nodeModulesPath);

// 按大小排序
const sorted = Object.entries(packages)
  .filter(([, size]) => size > 1024 * 100) // > 100KB
  .sort(([, a], [, b]) => b - a);

console.log('\n📦 最大的 20 个包:');
console.log('─'.repeat(60));

const totalSize = sorted.reduce((sum, [, size]) => sum + size, 0);

sorted.slice(0, 20).forEach(([name, size], index) => {
  const sizeMB = size / 1024 / 1024;
  const percent = ((size / totalSize) * 100).toFixed(1);
  const bar = '█'.repeat(Math.round(size / totalSize * 50));
  console.log(`${index + 1}. ${name.padEnd(30)} ${sizeMB.toFixed(2)} MB  ${bar} ${percent}%`);
});

console.log('─'.repeat(60));
console.log(`总计: ${(totalSize / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB`);
console.log(`共 ${Object.keys(packages).length} 个包`);

// 2. 分析特殊大包
console.log('\n⚠️ 需要关注的大包:');
const bigPackages = ['electron', 'next', 'react', 'react-dom', 'prisma', '@prisma'];

for (const pkg of bigPackages) {
  if (packages[pkg]) {
    const sizeMB = packages[pkg] / 1024 / 1024;
    console.log(`  ${pkg}: ${sizeMB.toFixed(2)} MB`);
  }
}
```

### 3.2 优化 Electron 主进程

```typescript
// electron/main.js
import { app, BrowserWindow, ipcMain, screen } from 'electron';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));

// 开发模式检测（使用环境变量，更高效）
const isDev = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development';

// 单例锁
const gotTheLock = app.requestSingleInstanceLock();

if (!gotTheLock) {
  app.quit();
  process.exit(0);
}

let mainWindow: BrowserWindow | null = null;
let splashWindow: BrowserWindow | null = null;

// ===== 启动闪屏（提升感知速度） =====
function createSplashWindow(): void {
  splashWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 400,
    height: 300,
    transparent: true,
    frame: false,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    skipTaskbar: true,
    resizable: false,
    webPreferences: {
      nodeIntegration: false,
      contextIsolation: true,
      sandbox: true,
    },
  });

  splashWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, '../public/splash.html'));
  splashWindow.center();
}

// ===== 创建主窗口（延迟加载，加速启动） =====
function createMainWindow(): void {
  const { width, height } = screen.getPrimaryDisplay().workAreaSize;

  mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: Math.min(1400, width),
    height: Math.min(900, height),
    minWidth: 1024,
    minHeight: 768,
    show: false, // 先不显示，加载完成后显示
    frame: true,
    backgroundColor: '#05070D',
    webPreferences: {
      nodeIntegration: false,
      contextIsolation: true,
      sandbox: true,
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'preload.js'),
    },
  });

  // 延迟加载（让 splash 先显示）
  setTimeout(() => {
    const url = isDev
      ? 'http://localhost:3000'
      : `file://${path.join(__dirname, '../.next/standalone/index.html')}`;

    mainWindow!.loadURL(url);

    // 加载完成后显示主窗口，关闭闪屏
    mainWindow!.once('ready-to-show', () => {
      if (splashWindow) {
        splashWindow.close();
        splashWindow = null;
      }
      mainWindow!.show();
    });

    // 开发工具
    if (isDev) {
      mainWindow!.webContents.openDevTools({ mode: 'detach' });
    }

    // 窗口关闭事件
    mainWindow!.on('closed', () => {
      mainWindow = null;
    });
  }, 300); // 300ms 让闪屏先显示
}

// ===== 应用启动 =====
app.whenReady().then(() => {
  // 显示闪屏
  createSplashWindow();

  // 创建主窗口（延迟执行）
  createMainWindow();

  // 安装扩展（仅开发）
  if (isDev) {
    try {
      import('electron-devtools-installer').then(({ default: installExtension, REACT_DEVELOPER_TOOLS }) => {
        installExtension(REACT_DEVELOPER_TOOLS);
      });
    } catch (_) {
      // 忽略
    }
  }

  // 注册 IPC 事件
  registerIpcHandlers();
});

// ===== IPC 注册（延迟注册） =====
function registerIpcHandlers(): void {
  // 窗口控制
  ipcMain.handle('window:minimize', () => {
    mainWindow?.minimize();
  });

  ipcMain.handle('window:maximize', () => {
    if (mainWindow?.isMaximized()) {
      mainWindow?.unmaximize();
    } else {
      mainWindow?.maximize();
    }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('window:close', () => {
    mainWindow?.close();
  });

  // 应用信息
  ipcMain.handle('app:version', () => {
    return app.getVersion();
  });

  // 环境信息
  ipcMain.handle('app:env', () => {
    return process.env.NODE_ENV;
  });
}

// ===== 其他窗口事件 =====
app.on('window-all-closed', () => {
  if (process.platform !== 'darwin') {
    app.quit();
  }
});

app.on('activate', () => {
  if (mainWindow === null) {
    createMainWindow();
  }
});

// ===== 退出清理 =====
app.on('will-quit', async () => {
  // 清理缓存、关闭连接等
  console.log('🧹 Cleaning up before quit...');
});
```

  // 平台信息

});

## 📦 第 5 步：验证与报告

### 5.1 体积验证脚本

```typescript
// scripts/check-size.ts
import { execSync } from 'child_process';
import { readdirSync, statSync } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';

console.log('📦 检查打包体积...');

// 1. 分析 dist-electron 目录
const distPath = join(process.cwd(), 'dist-electron');
try {
  const files = readdirSync(distPath);
  const sizeMap: Record<string, number> = {};

  function getDirSize(dir: string): number {
    let size = 0;
    const items = readdirSync(dir);
    for (const item of items) {
      const fullPath = join(dir, item);
      const stats = statSync(fullPath);
      if (stats.isDirectory()) {
        size += getDirSize(fullPath);
      } else {
        size += stats.size;
      }
    }
    return size;
  }

  const totalSize = getDirSize(distPath);
  const totalMB = totalSize / 1024 / 1024;

  console.log(`📁 总大小: ${totalMB.toFixed(2)} MB`);

  // 检查是否在目标范围内
  if (totalMB < 100) {
    console.log('✅ ✅ ✅ 打包体积 < 100MB，达标！');
  } else if (totalMB < 150) {
    console.log('⚠️ 打包体积 < 150MB，建议继续优化');
  } else {
    console.log('❌ 打包体积 > 150MB，需要进一步优化');
  }
} catch (_) {
  console.log('❌ 未找到 dist-electron 目录，请先执行 build');
}
```
