## 📦 第 1 步：Onboarding 首次启动引导

### 1.1 Onboarding 状态管理

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/onboarding.ts
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export type OnboardingStep =
  | 'welcome'
  | 'config'
  | 'persona'
  | 'connect'
  | 'complete';

export interface OnboardingState {
  currentStep: OnboardingStep;
  completed: boolean;
  config: {
    apiKey?: string;
    model?: string;
    personaId?: string;
    accountId?: string;
  };
}

// ===== 存储 Onboarding 状态 =====
const STORAGE_KEY = 'waos_onboarding_state';

export function getOnboardingState(): OnboardingState {
  try {
    const stored = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    if (stored) {
      return JSON.parse(stored);
    }
  } catch (_) {
    // 忽略
  }

  return {
    currentStep: 'welcome',
    completed: false,
    config: {},
  };
}

export function saveOnboardingState(state: OnboardingState): void {
  localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
}

export function completeOnboarding(): void {
  const state = getOnboardingState();
  state.completed = true;
  state.currentStep = 'complete';
  saveOnboardingState(state);
}

export function resetOnboarding(): void {
  localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
}

// ===== React Hook =====
export function useOnboarding(): {
  state: OnboardingState;
  goToStep: (step: OnboardingStep) => void;
  updateConfig: (config: Partial<OnboardingState['config']>) => void;
  complete: () => void;
  reset: () => void;
  isFirstRun: boolean;
} {
  const [state, setState] = useState<OnboardingState>(() => getOnboardingState());

  const goToStep = (step: OnboardingStep) => {
    const newState = { ...state, currentStep: step };
    setState(newState);
    saveOnboardingState(newState);
  };

  const updateConfig = (config: Partial<OnboardingState['config']>) => {
    const newState = {
      ...state,
      config: { ...state.config, ...config },
    };
    setState(newState);
    saveOnboardingState(newState);
  };

  const complete = () => {
    const newState = { ...state, completed: true, currentStep: 'complete' };
    setState(newState);
    saveOnboardingState(newState);
  };

  const reset = () => {
    resetOnboarding();
    setState(getOnboardingState());
  };

  return {
    state,
    goToStep,
    updateConfig,
    complete,
    reset,
    isFirstRun: !state.completed,
  };
}
```

### 1.2 Onboarding 组件

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/Onboarding.tsx
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { useOnboarding } from '@/lib/onboarding';

const steps = [
  {
    id: 'welcome',
    title: '👋 欢迎使用旺财',
    description: '你的 AI 私域营销助手已就位',
    icon: '🚀',
  },
  {
    id: 'config',
    title: '⚙️ 配置 AI 模型',
    description: '输入你的 API Key 和模型偏好',
    icon: '🤖',
  },
  {
    id: 'persona',
    title: '🎭 选择人设',
    description: '选择你的销售风格，AI 将以此方式与客户对话',
    icon: '🧠',
  },
  {
    id: 'connect',
    title: '📱 连接微信',
    description: '绑定你的微信账号，开始接收客户消息',
    icon: '💬',
  },
  {
    id: 'complete',
    title: '🎉 准备就绪！',
    description: '你的旺财已经配置完成，开始使用吧',
    icon: '✨',
  },
];

export function Onboarding() {
  const { state, goToStep, updateConfig, complete } = useOnboarding();

  const [config, setConfig] = useState({
    apiKey: '',
    model: 'deepseek-chat',
    personaId: 'sales-expert',
    accountId: '',
  });

  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleNext = () => {
    const currentIndex = steps.findIndex((s) => s.id === state.currentStep);
    if (currentIndex < steps.length - 1) {
      // 验证当前步骤
      if (state.currentStep === 'config') {
        if (!config.apiKey) {
          setError('请输入 API Key');
          return;
        }
        updateConfig({ apiKey: config.apiKey, model: config.model });
      }

      if (state.currentStep === 'persona') {
        updateConfig({ personaId: config.personaId });
      }

      if (state.currentStep === 'connect') {
        updateConfig({ accountId: config.accountId });
      }

      setError(null);
      goToStep(steps[currentIndex + 1].id as OnboardingStep);
    } else {
      // 最后一步
      complete();
      window.location.href = '/';
    }
  };

  const handleSkip = () => {
    complete();
    window.location.href = '/';
  };

  const currentStep = steps.find((s) => s.id === state.currentStep) || steps[0];
  const currentIndex = steps.findIndex((s) => s.id === state.currentStep);
  const isLast = currentIndex === steps.length - 1;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-[#05070D] p-4">
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        className="w-full max-w-2xl"
      >
        {/* 进度条 */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm text-white/40 mb-2">
            {steps.map((s, i) => (
              <span
                key={s.id}
                className={i <= currentIndex ? 'text-waos-primary' : ''}
              >
                {i + 1}
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className="h-1 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
            <motion.div
              className="h-full bg-waos-primary rounded-full"
              initial={{ width: 0 }}
              animate={{ width: `${((currentIndex + 1) / steps.length) * 100}%` }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
            />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 内容区 */}
        <div className="glass p-8 rounded-2xl border border-white/10">
          <div className="text-center mb-8">
            <div className="text-5xl mb-4">{currentStep.icon}</div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{currentStep.title}</h2>
            <p className="text-white/60 mt-2">{currentStep.description}</p>
          </div>

          {/* 步骤内容 */}
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {state.currentStep === 'config' && (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">API Key</label>
                  <input
                    type="password"
                    value={config.apiKey}
                    onChange={(e) => setConfig({ ...config, apiKey: e.target.value })}
                    className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none transition"
                    placeholder="输入你的 API Key"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">模型</label>
                  <select
                    value={config.model}
                    onChange={(e) => setConfig({ ...config, model: e.target.value })}
                    className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none transition"
                  >
                    <option value="deepseek-chat">DeepSeek-V3</option>
                    <option value="gpt-4o">GPT-4o</option>
                    <option value="gpt-4o-mini">GPT-4o-mini</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                {error && <div className="text-red-400 text-sm">{error}</div>}
              </div>
            )}

            {state.currentStep === 'persona' && (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  {[
                    { id: 'sales-expert', name: '🎯 销售专家', desc: '专业成交导向' },
                    { id: 'friendly', name: '🤝 亲和顾问', desc: '温和建立信任' },
                    { id: 'professional', name: '📊 专业咨询', desc: '深度专业解答' },
                    { id: 'warm', name: '💛 温暖关怀', desc: '情感维系客户' },
                  ].map((p) => (
                    <button
                      key={p.id}
                      onClick={() => setConfig({ ...config, personaId: p.id })}
                      className={`p-4 rounded-xl text-left transition-all ${
                        config.personaId === p.id
                          ? 'bg-waos-primary/20 border-2 border-waos-primary'
                          : 'bg-white/5 border-2 border-transparent hover:bg-white/10'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <div className="text-lg font-medium text-white">{p.name}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-white/40">{p.desc}</div>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {state.currentStep === 'connect' && (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                <div className="p-4 rounded-xl bg-white/5 border border-dashed border-white/20 text-center">
                  <div className="text-2xl mb-2">📱</div>
                  <div className="text-white/60 text-sm">
                    微信账号绑定功能即将上线
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-white/30 text-xs mt-2">
                    目前可通过 WebSocket 接收测试消息
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">账号名称（测试）</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={config.accountId}
                    onChange={(e) => setConfig({ ...config, accountId: e.target.value })}
                    className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none transition"
                    placeholder="输入测试账号名"
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {state.currentStep === 'complete' && (
              <div className="text-center py-4 space-y-4">
                <div className="text-6xl">🎉</div>
                <div className="text-white/80">你的旺财已经准备好了！</div>
                <div className="text-sm text-white/40">
                  你可以开始接收消息，或探索其他功能
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* 操作按钮 */}
          <div className="flex justify-between mt-8 pt-4 border-t border-white/5">
            {state.currentStep !== 'welcome' && state.currentStep !== 'complete' && (
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  const prevIndex = steps.findIndex((s) => s.id === state.currentStep) - 1;
                  if (prevIndex >= 0) {
                    goToStep(steps[prevIndex].id as OnboardingStep);
                  }
                }}
                className="text-white/40 hover:text-white/80 transition"
              >
                上一步
              </button>
            )}
            <div className="flex gap-3 ml-auto">
              <button
                onClick={handleSkip}
                className="text-white/30 hover:text-white/60 transition text-sm"
              >
                跳过
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleNext}
                className="px-6 py-2 rounded-lg bg-waos-primary text-black font-medium hover:opacity-80 transition disabled:opacity-50"
                disabled={loading}
              >
                {loading ? '处理中...' : isLast ? '开始使用 🚀' : '下一步 →'}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 1.3 在 App 中集成 Onboarding

```tsx
// frontend/src/app/page.tsx
'use client';

import { useOnboarding } from '@/lib/onboarding';
import { Onboarding } from '@/components/Onboarding';
import { MainLayout } from '@/components/layout/MainLayout';
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export default function HomePage() {
  const { isFirstRun } = useOnboarding();
  const [showOnboarding, setShowOnboarding] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    // 如果已完成 Onboarding，直接进入主界面
    if (!isFirstRun) {
      setShowOnboarding(false);
    }
  }, [isFirstRun]);

  if (showOnboarding) {
    return <Onboarding />;
  }

  return <MainLayout />;
}
```

## 📦 第 2 步：空状态设计

### 2.1 空状态组件

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/EmptyState.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react';

interface EmptyStateProps {
  icon?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  action?: {
    label: string;
    onClick: () => void;
  };
  secondaryAction?: {
    label: string;
    onClick: () => void;
  };
  children?: ReactNode;
}

export function EmptyState({
  icon = '📭',
  title,
  description,
  action,
  secondaryAction,
  children,
}: EmptyStateProps) {
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full p-8 text-center">
      <div className="text-6xl mb-4">{icon}</div>
      <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-white mb-2">{title}</h3>
      <p className="text-white/40 text-sm max-w-md">{description}</p>
      {action && (
        <button
          onClick={action.onClick}
          className="mt-4 px-6 py-2 rounded-lg bg-waos-primary text-black font-medium hover:opacity-80 transition"
        >
          {action.label}
        </button>
      )}
      {secondaryAction && (
        <button
          onClick={secondaryAction.onClick}
          className="mt-2 text-sm text-white/30 hover:text-white/60 transition"
        >
          {secondaryAction.label}
        </button>
      )}
      {children && <div className="mt-4">{children}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ===== 预设空状态 =====
export const EmptyStatePresets = {
```

## 📦 第 3 步：全局快捷键系统

### 3.1 快捷键注册中心

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/keyboard.ts
export interface Shortcut {
  id: string;
  keys: string[];
  description: string;
  category: 'global' | 'navigation' | 'action' | 'chat';
  action: () => void;
  enabled?: boolean;
}

// ===== 快捷键存储 =====
const SHORTCUTS: Shortcut[] = [];
const shortcutsMap = new Map<string, Shortcut>();

export function registerShortcut(shortcut: Shortcut): void {
  SHORTCUTS.push(shortcut);
  const key = shortcut.keys.sort().join('+');
  shortcutsMap.set(key, shortcut);
}

export function getShortcut(key: string): Shortcut | undefined {
  return shortcutsMap.get(key);
}

export function getShortcuts(): Shortcut[] {
  return SHORTCUTS;
}

export function getShortcutsByCategory(category: Shortcut['category']): Shortcut[] {
  return SHORTCUTS.filter((s) => s.category === category);
}

// ===== 快捷键帮助文本 =====
export function getShortcutDisplay(shortcut: Shortcut): string {
  return shortcut.keys.map((k) => {
    const replacements: Record<string, string> = {
      'Control': 'Ctrl',
      'Command': '⌘',
      'Shift': '⇧',
      'Alt': '⌥',
      'Meta': '⌘',
      'Escape': 'Esc',
      'ArrowUp': '↑',
      'ArrowDown': '↓',
      'ArrowLeft': '←',
      'ArrowRight': '→',
    };
    return replacements[k] || k;
  }).join(' + ');
}
```

### 3.2 快捷键绑定 Hook

```tsx
// frontend/src/hooks/useKeyboardShortcuts.ts
'use client';

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { registerShortcut, getShortcut, Shortcut } from '@/lib/keyboard';

// ===== 默认快捷键注册 =====
const DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS: Omit<Shortcut, 'action'>[] = [
  // 全局
  { id: 'global.search', keys: ['Control', 'K'], description: '全局搜索', category: 'global' },
  { id: 'global.settings', keys: ['Control', ','], description: '打开设置', category: 'global' },
  { id: 'global.help', keys: ['Control', 'H'], description: '帮助中心', category: 'global' },
  { id: 'global.escape', keys: ['Escape'], description: '关闭弹窗', category: 'global' },

  // 导航
  { id: 'nav.workbench', keys: ['Control', '1'], description: '工作台', category: 'navigation' },
  { id: 'nav.customers', keys: ['Control', '2'], description: '客户管理', category: 'navigation' },
  { id: 'nav.comments', keys: ['Control', '3'], description: '评论中心', category: 'navigation' },
  { id: 'nav.knowledge', keys: ['Control', '4'], description: '知识库', category: 'navigation' },
  { id: 'nav.sop', keys: ['Control', '5'], description: 'SOP 引擎', category: 'navigation' },
  { id: 'nav.analytics', keys: ['Control', '6'], description: '数据看板', category: 'navigation' },

  // 动作
  { id: 'action.reply', keys: ['R'], description: '快速回复', category: 'action' },
  { id: 'action.escale', keys: ['E'], description: '提升优先级', category: 'action' },
  { id: 'action.human', keys: ['H'], description: '转人工', category: 'action' },
  { id: 'action.ignore', keys: ['I'], description: '标记已处理', category: 'action' },
  { id: 'action.pin', keys: ['P'], description: '钉住/取消钉住', category: 'action' },

  // 聊天
  { id: 'chat.send', keys: ['Enter'], description: '发送消息', category: 'chat' },
  { id: 'chat.newline', keys: ['Shift', 'Enter'], description: '换行', category: 'chat' },
  { id: 'chat.ai', keys: ['Control', 'Enter'], description: 'AI 生成回复', category: 'chat' },
];

export function useKeyboardShortcuts(
  actions: Partial<Record<string, () => void>>
): void {
  const actionsRef = useRef(actions);

  useEffect(() => {
    actionsRef.current = actions;
  }, [actions]);

  useEffect(() => {
    // 注册默认快捷键
    for (const shortcutDef of DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS) {
      const action = actionsRef.current[shortcutDef.id];
      if (action) {
        registerShortcut({
          ...shortcutDef,
          action,
        });
      }
    }

    // 全局键盘监听
    const handler = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
      // 忽略输入框中的快捷键（除了 Enter 等）
      const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
      if (target.tagName === 'INPUT' || target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') {
        // 只允许特定的快捷键
        const allowed = ['Enter', 'Control+Enter'];
        const key = [event.key, ...(event.ctrlKey ? ['Control'] : []), ...(event.shiftKey ? ['Shift'] : [])]
          .sort()
          .join('+');
        if (!allowed.includes(key)) {
          return;
        }
      }

      // 构建按键组合
      const keys: string[] = [];
      if (event.ctrlKey) keys.push('Control');
      if (event.shiftKey) keys.push('Shift');
      if (event.altKey) keys.push('Alt');
      if (event.metaKey) keys.push('Meta');
      keys.push(event.key);

      const shortcutKey = keys.sort().join('+');
      const shortcut = getShortcut(shortcutKey);

      if (shortcut && shortcut.enabled !== false) {
        event.preventDefault();
        shortcut.action();
      }
    };

    window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
  }, []);
}
```

## ⚡ 第一优先级：P0 + P1（三天内必须落地）

### 📦 1. ClawBot 真实接入 + Session 管理（P0 核心）

这个模块放 `waos-stream/src/wechat/`，它专门负责**真实收发微信消息**，对接 iLink 协议，并管理多账号登录态。

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/types.ts
export interface WeChatConnector {
  login(accountId: string): Promise<{ qrCode?: string; token: string }>;
  sendText(to: string, content: string, accountId: string): Promise<any>;
  sendImage(to: string, imageUrl: string, accountId: string): Promise<any>;
  fetchMessages(accountId: string, sinceSeq?: number): Promise<any[]>;
  heartbeat(accountId: string): Promise<boolean>;
  logout(accountId: string): Promise<void>;
}

// waos-stream/src/wechat/clawbot.adapter.ts
import axios from 'axios';

export class ClawBotAdapter implements WeChatConnector {
  private baseUrl: string;
  private apiKey: string;

  constructor() {
    this.baseUrl = process.env.CLAWBOT_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8080/api';
    this.apiKey = process.env.CLAWBOT_API_KEY || '';
  }

  private async request<T>(path: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
    const res = await axios.post(`${this.baseUrl}${path}`, data, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${this.apiKey}` },
      timeout: 15000,
    });
    if (res.data.code !== 0) throw new Error(res.data.msg);
    return res.data.data;
  }

  async login(accountId: string) {
    return this.request<{ qrCode?: string; token: string }>('/login', { accountId });
  }

  async sendText(to: string, content: string, accountId: string) {
    return this.request('/send/text', { accountId, to, content });
  }

  async sendImage(to: string, imageUrl: string, accountId: string) {
    return this.request('/send/image', { accountId, to, imageUrl });
  }

  async fetchMessages(accountId: string, sinceSeq?: number) {
    return this.request<any[]>('/messages/pull', { accountId, sinceSeq });
  }

  async heartbeat(accountId: string) {
    return this.request('/heartbeat', { accountId });
  }

  async logout(accountId: string) {
    return this.request('/logout', { accountId });
  }
}
```

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/session.manager.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379');

export class SessionManager {
  private static SESSION_TTL = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60; // 7天

  static async saveToken(accountId: string, token: string, extra?: any) {
    await redis.hset(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, {
      token,
      extra: JSON.stringify(extra || {}),
      updatedAt: Date.now(),
    });
    await redis.expire(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, this.SESSION_TTL);
  }

  static async getToken(accountId: string): Promise<string | null> {
    const data = await redis.hgetall(`wechat:session:${accountId}`);
    return data?.token || null;
  }

  static async updateHeartbeat(accountId: string) {
    await redis.hset(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, 'lastHeartbeat', Date.now());
  }

  static async isOnline(accountId: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const data = await redis.hgetall(`wechat:session:${accountId}`);
    if (!data?.lastHeartbeat) return false;
    return Date.now() - parseInt(data.lastHeartbeat) < 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5分钟超时
  }

  static async remove(accountId: string) {
    await redis.del(`wechat:session:${accountId}`);
  }
}

// 消息同步循环（独立线程）
export async function startMessageSync(adapter: ClawBotAdapter) {
  const accounts = await redis.smembers('wechat:active_accounts');
  for (const accountId of accounts) {
    // 独立的拉取循环
    setInterval(async () => {
      if (!(await SessionManager.isOnline(accountId))) return;
      const messages = await adapter.fetchMessages(accountId);
      for (const msg of messages) {
        // 标准化后扔进消息队列（BullMQ）
        await enqueueMessageTask({
          wxId: msg.from,
          content: msg.text,
          source: 'wechat',
          accountId,
        });
      }
    }, 2000 + Math.random() * 1000); // 随机间隔
  }
}
```

### 🔐 2. PII 数据加密（P0 合规底线）

在 `frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts` 中，给微信 ID 和消息内容加密。这样你的 SQLite 里存的就全是密文了，彻底解决数据泄露风险。

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts
import { createCipheriv, createDecipheriv, randomBytes, scryptSync } from 'crypto';

const ALGORITHM = 'aes-256-gcm';
const IV_LENGTH = 16;
const SALT = 'waos-static-salt'; // 生产环境可以从环境变量读取
const KEY = scryptSync(process.env.ENCRYPTION_SECRET || 'default-secret', SALT, 32);

export function encrypt(text: string): string {
  if (!text) return text;
  const iv = randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
  const cipher = createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
  let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
  encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
  return `${iv.toString('hex')}:${authTag.toString('hex')}:${encrypted}`;
}

export function decrypt(text: string): string {
  if (!text || !text.includes(':')) return text;
  try {
    const [ivHex, authTagHex, encrypted] = text.split(':');
    const decipher = createDecipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, Buffer.from(ivHex, 'hex'));
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(authTagHex, 'hex'));
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    return decrypted;
  } catch {
    return text;
  }
}
```

```typescript
// 在 Prisma 中间件中自动加解密
// frontend/src/server/prisma.ts
import { encrypt, decrypt } from '@/lib/crypto';

prisma.$use(async (params, next) => {
  const sensitive = ['content', 'wxId', 'name', 'phone', 'nickname'];
  if (['create', 'update'].includes(params.action)) {
    const data = params.args.data;
    for (const key of Object.keys(data)) {
      if (sensitive.includes(key) && typeof data[key] === 'string') {
        data[key] = encrypt(data[key]);
      }
    }
  }
  const result = await next(params);
  if (['findUnique', 'findFirst', 'findMany'].includes(params.action)) {
    const decryptFields = (obj: any) => {
      if (!obj) return;
      for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) {
        if (sensitive.includes(key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
          obj[key] = decrypt(obj[key]);
        }
      }
    };
    if (Array.isArray(result)) result.forEach(decryptFields);
    else decryptFields(result);
  }
  return result;
});
```

### 📡 3. 结构化日志与 Sentry（P1 监控）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/logger.ts
import pino from 'pino';

const transport = pino.transport({
  targets: [
    { target: 'pino-pretty', level: 'info', options: { colorize: true } },
    { target: 'pino/file', level: 'error', options: { destination: './logs/error.log' } },
  ],
});

export const logger = pino(
  {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    redact: ['*.password', '*.token', '*.wxId', '*.content'],
  },
  transport
);

// 封装的 Sentry 上报（先装好 @sentry/nextjs）
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/nextjs';
export const reportError = (error: Error, context?: any) => {
  logger.error({ err: error, ...context }, error.message);
  Sentry.captureException(error, { extra: context });
};
```

## ⚙️ 第二优先级：P2（真实引擎与调度）

### 🧠 4. 替换硬编码话术：接入真实 LLM

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/llm.ts
export async function generateReply(params: {
  message: string;
  leadId: string;
  persona: string;
  history: string[];
}): Promise<{ reply: string; extracted: any }> {
  const response = await fetch('https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.DEEPSEEK_API_KEY}`,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: 'deepseek-chat',
      messages: [
        {
          role: 'system',
          content: `你是${params.persona}，请根据上下文回复。要求：提取客户意向、预算、情绪。返回 JSON 格式。`,
        },
        ...params.history.map((h) => ({ role: 'user', content: h })),
        { role: 'user', content: params.message },
      ],
      response_format: { type: 'json_object' },
    }),
  });
  const data = await response.json();
  return JSON.parse(data.choices[0].message.content);
}
```

### 📊 5. 多级调度器（HOT/WARM/COLD）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/scheduler.ts
import { Queue } from 'bullmq';
import { getRedisClient } from './redis';

const hotQueue = new Queue('hot-queue', { connection: getRedisClient() });
const warmQueue = new Queue('warm-queue', { connection: getRedisClient() });
const coldQueue = new Queue('cold-queue', { connection: getRedisClient() });

export function enqueueLead(leadId: string, score: number, data: any) {
  const jobData = { leadId, ...data };
  if (score > 80) hotQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 1 });
  else if (score > 50) warmQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 2 });
  else coldQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 3, delay: 60000 }); // 冷用户延迟1分钟处理
}

// 老化机制：每10分钟把冷队列的分数+5，防止饿死
setInterval(async () => {
  const jobs = await coldQueue.getJobs();
  for (const job of jobs) {
    // 这里模拟重新计算分数并升级
    // 实际可以重新评估后移入 warmQueue
  }
}, 10 * 60 * 1000);
```

## 🧠 第三优先级：P3（护城河与引擎）

### 🧬 6. 对话图引擎与身份核（架构预留）

这个我们不用急着全部写出来，但你必须先建好表结构。Hermes 只需要把这个 `schema.prisma` 合并进去，后面的逻辑慢慢长。

```prisma
// 新增：对话图引擎表
model ConversationGraph {
  id         String   @id @default(cuid())
  leadId     String   @unique
  nodes      Json     // 存储序列化的对话节点
  edges      Json     // 存储序列化的连线关系
  updatedAt  DateTime @updatedAt
}

// 新增：身份核向量表
model IdentityKernel {
  id              String   @id @default(cuid())
  leadId          String   @unique
  trustLevel      Float    @default(0.5)
  emotionState    String   // 'neutral' | 'positive' | 'negative'
  valueSensitivity Float   @default(0.5)
  urgency         Float    @default(0.5)
  resistance      Float    @default(0.5)
  conversionDistance Float @default(1.0)
  updatedAt       DateTime @updatedAt
}
```

## 🔴 P0-1：ClawBot 真实 API 对接 + Session 管理

**文件位置**：`waos-stream/src/wechat/`

### ① clawbot-adapter.ts（真实 HTTP 调用）

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/clawbot-adapter.ts
import axios, { AxiosInstance } from 'axios';

export interface ClawBotConfig {
  baseURL: string;
  apiKey: string;
  timeout?: number;
}

export interface ClawBotMessage {
  id: string;
  from: string;
  to: string;
  content: string;
  type: 'text' | 'image' | 'voice' | 'video';
  timestamp: number;
}

export class ClawBotAdapter {
  private client: AxiosInstance;
  private config: ClawBotConfig;

  constructor(config: ClawBotConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.client = axios.create({
      baseURL: config.baseURL,
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${config.apiKey}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      timeout: config.timeout || 30000,
    });
  }

  // ===== 登录 =====
  async login(accountId: string): Promise<{ qrCode?: string; token: string; status: string }> {
    const response = await this.client.post('/login', { accountId });
    return response.data.data;
  }

  // ===== 检查登录状态 =====
  async checkStatus(accountId: string): Promise<{ status: 'online' | 'offline' | 'expired'; token?: string }> {
    const response = await this.client.get(`/status/${accountId}`);
    return response.data.data;
  }

  // ===== 发送文本消息 =====
  async sendText(accountId: string, to: string, content: string): Promise<{ msgId: string }> {
    const response = await this.client.post('/send/text', { accountId, to, content });
    return response.data.data;
  }

  // ===== 发送图片 =====
  async sendImage(accountId: string, to: string, imageUrl: string): Promise<{ msgId: string }> {
    const response = await this.client.post('/send/image', { accountId, to, imageUrl });
    return response.data.data;
  }

  // ===== 拉取消息（增量） =====
  async fetchMessages(accountId: string, sinceSeq?: number): Promise<ClawBotMessage[]> {
    const response = await this.client.post('/messages/pull', { accountId, sinceSeq });
    return response.data.data || [];
  }

  // ===== 心跳 =====
  async heartbeat(accountId: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const response = await this.client.post('/heartbeat', { accountId });
    return response.data.code === 0;
  }

  // ===== 登出 =====
  async logout(accountId: string): Promise<void> {
    await this.client.post('/logout', { accountId });
  }
}
```

### ② session-manager.ts（Redis 持久化登录态）

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/session-manager.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { ClawBotAdapter } from './clawbot-adapter';

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379');

const SESSION_TTL = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60; // 7天
const HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL = 60; // 60秒
const HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT = 5 * 60; // 5分钟无心跳则视为离线

export interface WeChatSession {
  accountId: string;
  token: string;
  status: 'online' | 'offline' | 'expired';
  lastHeartbeat: number;
  extra?: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export class SessionManager {
  // ===== 保存会话 =====
  static async save(accountId: string, token: string, extra?: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
    await redis.hset(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, {
      token,
      status: 'online',
      lastHeartbeat: Date.now(),
      extra: JSON.stringify(extra || {}),
    });
    await redis.expire(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, SESSION_TTL);
  }

  // ===== 获取会话 =====
  static async get(accountId: string): Promise<WeChatSession | null> {
    const data = await redis.hgetall(`wechat:session:${accountId}`);
    if (!data || !data.token) return null;
    return {
      accountId,
      token: data.token,
      status: data.status as 'online' | 'offline' | 'expired',
      lastHeartbeat: parseInt(data.lastHeartbeat || '0'),
      extra: data.extra ? JSON.parse(data.extra) : undefined,
    };
  }

  // ===== 更新心跳 =====
  static async heartbeat(accountId: string): Promise<void> {
    await redis.hset(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, 'lastHeartbeat', Date.now());
    await redis.expire(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, SESSION_TTL);
  }

  // ===== 检查是否在线 =====
  static async isOnline(accountId: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const session = await this.get(accountId);
    if (!session || session.status !== 'online') return false;
    const now = Date.now();
    return now - session.lastHeartbeat < HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT * 1000;
  }

  // ===== 标记离线 =====
  static async markOffline(accountId: string): Promise<void> {
    await redis.hset(`wechat:session:${accountId}`, 'status', 'offline');
  }

  // ===== 删除会话 =====
  static async delete(accountId: string): Promise<void> {
    await redis.del(`wechat:session:${accountId}`);
  }

  // ===== 获取所有在线账号 =====
  static async getOnlineAccounts(): Promise<string[]> {
    const keys = await redis.keys('wechat:session:*');
    const accounts: string[] = [];
    for (const key of keys) {
      const accountId = key.replace('wechat:session:', '');
      if (await this.isOnline(accountId)) {
        accounts.push(accountId);
      }
    }
    return accounts;
  }
}

// ===== 后台心跳循环 =====
export function startHeartbeatLoop(adapter: ClawBotAdapter): NodeJS.Timeout {
  return setInterval(async () => {
    const accounts = await SessionManager.getOnlineAccounts();
    for (const accountId of accounts) {
      try {
        const ok = await adapter.heartbeat(accountId);
        if (ok) {
          await SessionManager.heartbeat(accountId);
        } else {
          await SessionManager.markOffline(accountId);
          console.warn(`[WeChat] Account ${accountId} heartbeat failed, marked offline`);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`[WeChat] Heartbeat error for ${accountId}:`, error);
        await SessionManager.markOffline(accountId);
      }
    }
  }, HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL * 1000);
}
```

### ③ message-sync.ts（消息同步循环）

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/message-sync.ts
import { ClawBotAdapter, ClawBotMessage } from './clawbot-adapter';
import { SessionManager } from './session-manager';
import { enqueueMessageTask } from '@/queues/enqueue';
import { normalizeWeChatMessage } from './message-normalizer';

const SYNC_INTERVAL = 2000; // 2秒拉一次

export function startMessageSync(adapter: ClawBotAdapter): NodeJS.Timeout {
  return setInterval(async () => {
    const accounts = await SessionManager.getOnlineAccounts();
    for (const accountId of accounts) {
      try {
        // 获取上次拉取的位置
        const sinceSeq = await getLastSeq(accountId);
        const messages = await adapter.fetchMessages(accountId, sinceSeq);
        if (messages.length === 0) continue;

        let maxSeq = sinceSeq || 0;
        for (const raw of messages) {
          // 标准化消息
          const normalized = normalizeWeChatMessage(raw, accountId);
          // 入队（BullMQ）
          await enqueueMessageTask({
            wxId: normalized.from,
            content: normalized.content,
            source: 'wechat',
            accountId,
            msgId: normalized.id,
          });
          maxSeq = Math.max(maxSeq, parseInt(raw.id) || maxSeq);
        }
        // 保存游标
        await saveLastSeq(accountId, maxSeq);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`[WeChat] Sync error for ${accountId}:`, error);
      }
    }
  }, SYNC_INTERVAL);
}

async function getLastSeq(accountId: string): Promise<number | undefined> {
  const val = await redis.get(`wechat:sync:${accountId}`);
  return val ? parseInt(val) : undefined;
}

async function saveLastSeq(accountId: string, seq: number): Promise<void> {
  await redis.set(`wechat:sync:${accountId}`, seq);
}
```

### ④ message-normalizer.ts（标准化 + 去重）

```typescript
// waos-stream/src/wechat/message-normalizer.ts
import { ClawBotMessage } from './clawbot-adapter';
import crypto from 'crypto';
import Redis from 'ioredis';

const redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379');

// 5分钟滑动窗口去重
const DEDUP_WINDOW = 5 * 60;

export function normalizeWeChatMessage(raw: ClawBotMessage, accountId: string): {
  id: string;
  from: string;
  content: string;
  type: string;
  timestamp: number;
  accountId: string;
} {
  // 生成去重指纹
  const fingerprint = crypto
    .createHash('sha256')
    .update(`${accountId}:${raw.from}:${raw.content}:${Math.floor(raw.timestamp / 60)}`)
    .digest('hex');

  return {
    id: raw.id || fingerprint,
    from: raw.from,
    content: raw.content,
    type: raw.type || 'text',
    timestamp: raw.timestamp || Date.now(),
    accountId,
  };
}

// 去重检查
export async function isDuplicate(accountId: string, from: string, content: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const fingerprint = crypto
    .createHash('sha256')
    .update(`${accountId}:${from}:${content}`)
    .digest('hex');
  const key = `wechat:dedup:${fingerprint}`;
  const exists = await redis.exists(key);
  if (!exists) {
    await redis.setex(key, DEDUP_WINDOW, '1');
  }
  return exists === 1;
}
```

## 🔴 P0-2：PII 数据加密（AES-256-GCM）

**文件位置**：`frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts`

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts
import { createCipheriv, createDecipheriv, randomBytes, scryptSync } from 'crypto';

const ALGORITHM = 'aes-256-gcm';
const IV_LENGTH = 16;
const SALT = 'waos-salt-v1';

// 从环境变量读取密钥，如果没有则用 scrypt 派生
function getKey(): Buffer {
  const secret = process.env.ENCRYPTION_SECRET;
  if (secret && secret.length >= 32) {
    return Buffer.from(secret.slice(0, 32), 'utf8');
  }
  // 降级：从固定盐派生（生产环境必须设置 ENCRYPTION_SECRET）
  return scryptSync('waos-fallback-secret', SALT, 32);
}

const KEY = getKey();

/**
 * 加密文本
 * 输出格式: iv:authTag:encrypted (hex)
 */
export function encrypt(text: string): string {
  if (!text) return text;
  const iv = randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
  const cipher = createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
  let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
  encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
  return `${iv.toString('hex')}:${authTag.toString('hex')}:${encrypted}`;
}

/**
 * 解密文本
 */
export function decrypt(encryptedText: string): string {
  if (!encryptedText) return encryptedText;
  if (!encryptedText.includes(':')) return encryptedText; // 兼容旧数据
  try {
    const parts = encryptedText.split(':');
    if (parts.length !== 3) return encryptedText;
    const [ivHex, authTagHex, encrypted] = parts;
    const decipher = createDecipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, Buffer.from(ivHex, 'hex'));
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(authTagHex, 'hex'));
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    return decrypted;
  } catch {
    return encryptedText;
  }
}

/**
 * 判断是否为加密格式
 */
export function isEncrypted(text: string): boolean {
  if (!text) return false;
  return text.includes(':') && text.split(':').length === 3;
}
```

### Prisma 中间件（自动加解密）

```typescript
// frontend/src/server/prisma-middleware.ts
import { Prisma } from '@prisma/client';
import { encrypt, decrypt, isEncrypted } from '@/lib/crypto';

const ENCRYPTED_FIELDS: Record<string, string[]> = {
  Message: ['content', 'wxId'],
  Lead: ['name', 'wxId', 'phone', 'profile'],
  Comment: ['content', 'nickname', 'userId'],
  User: ['email', 'phone'],
};

export function createEncryptionMiddleware(): Prisma.Middleware {
  return async (params, next) => {
    const model = params.model as string;
    const action = params.action;

    // ===== 写操作：加密 =====
    if (['create', 'update', 'updateMany', 'upsert'].includes(action)) {
      const fields = ENCRYPTED_FIELDS[model] || [];
      const data = params.args.data;
      if (data && typeof data === 'object') {
        for (const key of Object.keys(data)) {
          if (fields.includes(key) && typeof data[key] === 'string' && data[key]) {
            if (!isEncrypted(data[key])) {
              data[key] = encrypt(data[key]);
            }
          }
        }
        // 递归处理嵌套对象
        if (data.data) encryptFields(fields, data.data);
        if (data.create) encryptFields(fields, data.create);
        if (data.update) encryptFields(fields, data.update);
      }
    }

    const result = await next(params);

    // ===== 读操作：解密 =====
    if (['findUnique', 'findFirst', 'findMany'].includes(action)) {
      const fields = ENCRYPTED_FIELDS[model] || [];
      if (result) {
        if (Array.isArray(result)) {
          for (const item of result) decryptFields(fields, item);
        } else {
          decryptFields(fields, result);
        }
      }
    }

    return result;
  };
}

function encryptFields(fields: string[], obj: any) {
  if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return;
  for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) {
    if (fields.includes(key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string' && obj[key]) {
      if (!isEncrypted(obj[key])) {
        obj[key] = encrypt(obj[key]);
      }
    }
  }
}

function decryptFields(fields: string[], obj: any) {
  if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return;
  for (const key of Object.keys(obj)) {
    if (fields.includes(key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string' && obj[key]) {
      obj[key] = decrypt(obj[key]);
    }
  }
}
```

## 🔴 P0-3：结构化日志（pino JSON）

**文件位置**：`frontend/src/lib/logger.ts`

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/logger.ts
import pino from 'pino';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';

const LOG_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'logs');
if (!fs.existsSync(LOG_DIR)) {
  fs.mkdirSync(LOG_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

const isProduction = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';

// ===== 日志传输配置 =====
const targets: pino.TransportTargetOptions[] = [
  // 生产环境写入文件，开发环境输出到控制台
  {
    target: isProduction ? 'pino/file' : 'pino-pretty',
    options: isProduction
      ? { destination: path.join(LOG_DIR, 'app.log'), mkdir: true }
      : { colorize: true, translateTime: 'SYS:standard' },
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  },
];

// 错误日志单独输出
if (isProduction) {
  targets.push({
    target: 'pino/file',
    options: { destination: path.join(LOG_DIR, 'error.log'), mkdir: true },
    level: 'error',
  });
}

const transport = pino.transport({ targets });

// ===== 主 Logger =====
export const logger = pino(
  {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    timestamp: pino.stdTimeFunctions.isoTime,
    redact: {
      paths: [
        '*.password',
        '*.token',
        '*.apiKey',
        '*.wxId',
        '*.content',
        '*.phone',
        '*.email',
        '*.profile',
      ],
      censor: '[REDACTED]',
    },
    serializers: {
      err: pino.stdSerializers.err,
    },
  },
  transport
);

// ===== 子 Logger（带上下文） =====
export function createLogger(context: Record<string, unknown>) {
  return logger.child(context);
}

// ===== 性能计时 =====
export function timer(label: string): () => void {
  const start = process.hrtime.bigint();
  return () => {
    const end = process.hrtime.bigint();
    const duration = Number(end - start) / 1_000_000;
    logger.debug(`⏱️ ${label}`, { duration: `${duration.toFixed(2)}ms` });
  };
}
```

```typescript
// frontend/sentry.client.config.ts
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/nextjs';

Sentry.init({
  dsn: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN,
  environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
  tracesSampleRate: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 0.1 : 1.0,
  replaysSessionSampleRate: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 0.1 : 1.0,
  replaysOnErrorSampleRate: 1.0,

  beforeSend(event) {
    // 脱敏
    if (event.request?.data) {
      const sensitive = ['password', 'token', 'apiKey', 'wxId', 'content'];
      if (typeof event.request.data === 'object') {
        for (const key of sensitive) {
          delete event.request.data[key];
        }
      }
    }
    return event;
  },
});
```

### 错误上报工具

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/error-report.ts
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/nextjs';
import { logger } from './logger';

export function reportError(error: Error, context?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
  // 结构化日志
  logger.error({ err: error, ...context }, error.message);

  // Sentry 上报
  Sentry.withScope((scope) => {
    if (context) {
      scope.setContext('context', context);
    }
    Sentry.captureException(error);
  });
}

export function reportMessage(message: string, level: 'info' | 'warning' | 'error' = 'info'): void {
  logger[level](message);
  Sentry.captureMessage(message, level === 'error' ? 'error' : 'info');
}
```

## 🔴 P0-5：数据库自动备份

**文件位置**：`scripts/backup-db.ts`

```typescript
// scripts/backup-db.ts
#!/usr/bin/env node

import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import { createWriteStream, existsSync, mkdirSync, readdirSync, statSync, unlinkSync } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';
import { createGzip } from 'zlib';
import { pipeline } from 'stream';
import { promisify as streamPromisify } from 'stream';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);
const pipelineAsync = streamPromisify(pipeline);

// ===== 配置 =====
const DB_PATH = process.env.DATABASE_PATH || 'prisma/dev.db';
const BACKUP_DIR = process.env.BACKUP_DIR || join(process.cwd(), 'backups');
const RETENTION_DAYS = parseInt(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_DAYS || '7');
const BACKUP_SCHEDULE = process.env.BACKUP_SCHEDULE || '0 2 * * *'; // 每天凌晨2点

// ===== 确保目录存在 =====
if (!existsSync(BACKUP_DIR)) {
  mkdirSync(BACKUP_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

// ===== 执行备份 =====
async function backupDatabase(): Promise<string> {
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
  const fileName = `db-backup-${timestamp}.sqlite.gz`;
  const filePath = join(BACKUP_DIR, fileName);

  console.log(`📦 开始备份: ${DB_PATH} → ${filePath}`);

  // 1. 导出 SQL
  const { stdout } = await execAsync(`sqlite3 ${DB_PATH} .dump`);

  // 2. 压缩写入
  const writeStream = createWriteStream(filePath);
  const gzip = createGzip();

  await pipelineAsync(
    async function* source() {
      yield stdout;
    }(),
    gzip,
    writeStream
  );

  const sizeMB = (writeStream.bytesWritten / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2);
  console.log(`✅ 备份完成: ${filePath} (${sizeMB} MB)`);
  return filePath;
}

// ===== 清理旧备份 =====
function cleanOldBackups(): void {
  const files = readdirSync(BACKUP_DIR);
  const now = Date.now();
  let deleted = 0;

  for (const file of files) {
    if (!file.startsWith('db-backup-')) continue;
    const filePath = join(BACKUP_DIR, file);
    const stats = statSync(filePath);
    const age = (now - stats.mtimeMs) / (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    if (age > RETENTION_DAYS) {
      unlinkSync(filePath);
      deleted++;
      console.log(`🗑️ 删除旧备份: ${file}`);
    }
  }

  if (deleted > 0) {
    console.log(`🧹 清理了 ${deleted} 个旧备份 (保留 ${RETENTION_DAYS} 天)`);
  }
}

// ===== 主函数 =====
async function main() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 数据库备份任务开始');
    console.log(`📁 数据库: ${DB_PATH}`);
    console.log(`📁 备份目录: ${BACKUP_DIR}`);
    console.log(`📁 保留天数: ${RETENTION_DAYS} 天`);

    await backupDatabase();
    cleanOldBackups();

    console.log('✅ 备份任务完成');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ 备份失败:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// ===== 执行 =====
main();
```

### 定时任务集成

```typescript
// scripts/schedule-backup.ts
import cron from 'node-cron';
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';

const execAsync = promisify(exec);

const BACKUP_SCHEDULE = process.env.BACKUP_SCHEDULE || '0 2 * * *';

console.log(`🕐 启动备份调度器: ${BACKUP_SCHEDULE}`);

cron.schedule(BACKUP_SCHEDULE, async () => {
  console.log('📦 执行定时备份...');
  try {
    const { stdout, stderr } = await execAsync('npx ts-node scripts/backup-db.ts');
    if (stderr) console.warn('备份警告:', stderr);
    console.log(stdout);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ 定时备份失败:', error);
  }
});

console.log('🔄 备份调度器已启动，按 Ctrl+C 停止');
```

```json
  }
}
```

```bash
# 1. 创建目录结构

# 6. 启动测试
```

# 🟡 P1：让系统变聪明

## P1-1：真实 LLM 接入（DeepSeek API）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/llm.ts
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface LLMConfig {
  apiKey: string;
  baseURL?: string;
  model?: string;
  timeout?: number;
}

export interface LLMResponse {
  reply: string;
  extracted: Record<string, unknown>;
  status: string;
  tokensUsed: number;
  costUSD: number;
}

const DEFAULT_CONFIG: LLMConfig = {
  apiKey: process.env.DEEPSEEK_API_KEY || '',
  baseURL: 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1',
  model: 'deepseek-chat',
  timeout: 15000,
};

// ===== 调用 LLM =====
export async function generateReply(params: {
  message: string;
  leadId: string;
  persona: string;
  history: Array<{ role: 'user' | 'assistant'; content: string }>;
  systemPrompt?: string;
}): Promise<LLMResponse> {
  const config = { ...DEFAULT_CONFIG };
  if (!config.apiKey) {
    logger.warn('LLM API key not configured, using fallback');
    return fallbackReply(params.message);
  }

  const startTime = Date.now();

  try {
    const response = await fetch(`${config.baseURL}/chat/completions`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${config.apiKey}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: config.model,
        messages: [
          {
            role: 'system',
            content:
              params.systemPrompt ||
              `你是${params.persona}，请根据上下文回复客户。
               要求：
               1. 回复要自然、专业、有温度
               2. 提取客户的关键信息：意向、预算、情绪、家庭情况
               3. 判断客户阶段：新客/跟进中/高意向/已成交
               4. 返回 JSON 格式：{"reply":"回复内容","extracted":{"意向":"","预算":"","情绪":"","家庭":""},"status":"阶段"}`,
          },
          ...params.history,
          { role: 'user', content: params.message },
        ],
        temperature: 0.7,
        max_tokens: 800,
        response_format: { type: 'json_object' },
      }),
      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(config.timeout!),
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`LLM API error: ${response.status}`);
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    const result = JSON.parse(data.choices[0].message.content);
    const tokensUsed = data.usage?.total_tokens || 0;
    const costUSD = tokensUsed * 0.0000014; // DeepSeek 约 $1.4/1M tokens

    logger.info('LLM response generated', {
      leadId: params.leadId,
      tokensUsed,
      costUSD,
      latency: Date.now() - startTime,
    });

    return {
      reply: result.reply || result.response || result.message || '已收到，我帮您处理。',
      extracted: result.extracted || {},
      status: result.status || '跟进中',
      tokensUsed,
      costUSD,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error({ err: error, leadId: params.leadId }, 'LLM call failed, using fallback');
    return fallbackReply(params.message);
  }
}

// ===== 降级兜底 =====
function fallbackReply(message: string): LLMResponse {
  const replies = {
    price: '收到您的询价，我马上给您整理一份详细的报价方案。',
    rejection: '理解您的考虑，有需要随时找我，我一直在。',
    silence: '好久不见！最近怎么样？有什么我能帮您的吗？',
    default: '收到，我帮您确认一下，稍后回复您。',
  };

  let reply = replies.default;
  if (message.includes('多少钱') || message.includes('价格')) reply = replies.price;
  else if (message.includes('不需要') || message.includes('考虑')) reply = replies.rejection;
  else if (message.includes('在吗') || message.includes('最近')) reply = replies.silence;

  return {
    reply,
    extracted: {},
    status: '跟进中',
    tokensUsed: 0,
    costUSD: 0,
  };
}
```

## P1-2：多级调度器（HOT/WARM/COLD + 老化 + 抢占）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/scheduler.ts
import { Queue, Worker, Job } from 'bullmq';
import { getRedisClient } from './redis';
import { logger } from './logger';

// ===== 三队列 =====
const HOT_QUEUE = 'scheduler:hot';
const WARM_QUEUE = 'scheduler:warm';
const COLD_QUEUE = 'scheduler:cold';

const hotQueue = new Queue(HOT_QUEUE, { connection: getRedisClient() });
const warmQueue = new Queue(WARM_QUEUE, { connection: getRedisClient() });
const coldQueue = new Queue(COLD_QUEUE, { connection: getRedisClient() });

export interface SchedulerTask {
  leadId: string;
  data: Record<string, unknown>;
  score: number;
  enqueuedAt: number;
}

// ===== 入队 =====
export async function enqueueTask(leadId: string, data: Record<string, unknown>, score: number): Promise<void> {
  const task: SchedulerTask = { leadId, data, score, enqueuedAt: Date.now() };
  const jobData = { ...task };

  if (score > 80) {
    await hotQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 1, jobId: `hot:${leadId}` });
    logger.info(`[Scheduler] HOT enqueued: ${leadId} (score: ${score})`);
  } else if (score > 50) {
    await warmQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 2, jobId: `warm:${leadId}` });
    logger.info(`[Scheduler] WARM enqueued: ${leadId} (score: ${score})`);
  } else {
    // COLD 队列延迟 60 秒，防止瞬时涌入
    await coldQueue.add('process', jobData, { priority: 3, delay: 60000, jobId: `cold:${leadId}` });
    logger.info(`[Scheduler] COLD enqueued: ${leadId} (score: ${score})`);
  }
}

// ===== 老化机制：每 10 分钟 COLD 队列统一 +5 分 =====
export function startAgingLoop(): NodeJS.Timeout {
  return setInterval(async () => {
    try {
      const jobs = await coldQueue.getJobs(['waiting', 'delayed']);
      for (const job of jobs) {
        const data = job.data as SchedulerTask;
        const newScore = data.score + 5;
        // 如果达到 50 分，升级到 WARM
        if (newScore > 50) {
          await job.remove();
          await warmQueue.add('process', { ...data, score: newScore }, { priority: 2 });
          logger.info(`[Scheduler] Aged up: ${data.leadId} COLD → WARM (${newScore})`);
        } else {
          // 更新分数，重新入队
          await job.remove();
          await coldQueue.add(
            'process',
            { ...data, score: newScore },
            { priority: 3, delay: 60000, jobId: `cold:${data.leadId}` }
          );
          logger.debug(`[Scheduler] Aged: ${data.leadId} COLD +5 (${newScore})`);
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error({ err: error }, 'Aging loop failed');
    }
  }, 10 * 60 * 1000);
}

// ===== 抢占机制：HOT 进来踢 COLD =====
export async function preemptCold(): Promise<void> {
  try {
    const hotCount = await hotQueue.getJobCounts();
    if (hotCount.waiting > 0) {
      // 取一个 COLD 任务，延迟 30 分钟
      const coldJobs = await coldQueue.getJobs(['waiting', 'delayed']);
      if (coldJobs.length > 0) {
        const job = coldJobs[0];
        const data = job.data as SchedulerTask;
        await job.remove();
        await coldQueue.add('process', data, {
          priority: 3,
          delay: 30 * 60 * 1000,
          jobId: `cold:${data.leadId}`,
        });
        logger.info(`[Scheduler] Preempted: ${data.leadId} COLD delayed 30min due to HOT`);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error({ err: error }, 'Preempt failed');
  }
}

// ===== Worker：消费任务 =====
export function startSchedulerWorker(
  handler: (task: SchedulerTask) => Promise<void>
): { hotWorker: Worker; warmWorker: Worker; coldWorker: Worker } {
  const hotWorker = new Worker(
    HOT_QUEUE,
    async (job: Job) => {
      await handler(job.data as SchedulerTask);
    },
    { connection: getRedisClient(), concurrency: 5 }
  );

  const warmWorker = new Worker(
    WARM_QUEUE,
    async (job: Job) => {
      await handler(job.data as SchedulerTask);
    },
    { connection: getRedisClient(), concurrency: 3 }
  );

  const coldWorker = new Worker(
    COLD_QUEUE,
    async (job: Job) => {
      await handler(job.data as SchedulerTask);
    },
    { connection: getRedisClient(), concurrency: 1 }
  );

  hotWorker.on('completed', (job) => {
    logger.info(`[Scheduler] HOT completed: ${job.id}`);
    // 抢占检查
    preemptCold();
  });

  hotWorker.on('failed', (job, err) => {
    logger.error({ err, jobId: job?.id }, 'HOT job failed');
  });

  return { hotWorker, warmWorker, coldWorker };
}

// ===== 获取队列状态 =====
export async function getSchedulerStatus() {
  const [hot, warm, cold] = await Promise.all([
    hotQueue.getJobCounts(),
    warmQueue.getJobCounts(),
    coldQueue.getJobCounts(),
  ]);

  return {
    hot: hot,
    warm: warm,
    cold: cold,
  };
}
```

## P1-3：对话图引擎（Conversation Graph）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/conversation-graph.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

// ===== 节点类型 =====
export type GraphNodeType = 'user_message' | 'assistant_message' | 'intent' | 'action' | 'state';

export interface GraphNode {
  id: string;
  type: GraphNodeType;
  label: string;
  data: Record<string, unknown>;
  timestamp: number;
}

export interface GraphEdge {
  source: string;
  target: string;
  type: 'response' | 'trigger' | 'transition' | 'semantic';
  weight?: number;
}

export interface ConversationGraph {
  id: string;
  leadId: string;
  nodes: GraphNode[];
  edges: GraphEdge[];
  updatedAt: number;
}

// ===== 创建图 =====
export async function createGraph(leadId: string): Promise<ConversationGraph> {
  const existing = await prisma.conversationGraph.findUnique({
    where: { leadId },
  });

  if (existing) {
    return JSON.parse(existing.graph);
  }

  const graph: ConversationGraph = {
    id: `graph_${Date.now()}`,
    leadId,
    nodes: [],
    edges: [],
    updatedAt: Date.now(),
  };

  await prisma.conversationGraph.create({
    data: {
      leadId,
      graph: JSON.stringify(graph),
    },
  });

  return graph;
}

// ===== 获取图 =====
export async function getGraph(leadId: string): Promise<ConversationGraph | null> {
  const record = await prisma.conversationGraph.findUnique({
    where: { leadId },
  });

  if (!record) return null;
  return JSON.parse(record.graph);
}

// ===== 添加节点 =====
export async function addNode(
  leadId: string,
  node: Omit<GraphNode, 'id' | 'timestamp'>
): Promise<ConversationGraph> {
  const graph = await getGraph(leadId);
  if (!graph) {
    await createGraph(leadId);
    return addNode(leadId, node);
  }

  const newNode: GraphNode = {
    ...node,
    id: `node_${Date.now()}_${graph.nodes.length}`,
    timestamp: Date.now(),
  };

  graph.nodes.push(newNode);
  graph.updatedAt = Date.now();

  await prisma.conversationGraph.update({
    where: { leadId },
    data: { graph: JSON.stringify(graph) },
  });

  logger.debug(`[Graph] Node added: ${newNode.id} (${node.type}) for ${leadId}`);
  return graph;
}

// ===== 添加边 =====
export async function addEdge(
  leadId: string,
  edge: Omit<GraphEdge, 'weight'>
): Promise<ConversationGraph> {
  const graph = await getGraph(leadId);
  if (!graph) throw new Error(`Graph not found for lead ${leadId}`);

  const newEdge: GraphEdge = {
    ...edge,
    weight: 1,
  };

  // 检查是否已存在相同边（去重）
  const exists = graph.edges.some((e) => e.source === edge.source && e.target === edge.target);
  if (exists) {
    // 更新权重
    const existingEdge = graph.edges.find((e) => e.source === edge.source && e.target === edge.target);
    if (existingEdge) {
      existingEdge.weight = (existingEdge.weight || 1) + 1;
    }
  } else {
    graph.edges.push(newEdge);
  }

  graph.updatedAt = Date.now();

  await prisma.conversationGraph.update({
    where: { leadId },
    data: { graph: JSON.stringify(graph) },
  });

  logger.debug(`[Graph] Edge added: ${edge.source} → ${edge.target} for ${leadId}`);
  return graph;
}

// ===== 获取路径 =====
export function findPath(graph: ConversationGraph, from: string, to: string): string[] {
  // BFS 找最短路径
  const visited = new Set<string>();
  const queue: Array<{ node: string; path: string[] }> = [{ node: from, path: [from] }];

  while (queue.length > 0) {
    const { node, path } = queue.shift()!;
    if (node === to) return path;

    if (visited.has(node)) continue;
    visited.add(node);

    const outgoing = graph.edges.filter((e) => e.source === node);
    for (const edge of outgoing) {
      if (!visited.has(edge.target)) {
        queue.push({ node: edge.target, path: [...path, edge.target] });
      }
    }
  }

  return [];
}

// ===== 获取子图（最近 N 个节点） =====
export function getSubgraph(graph: ConversationGraph, n: number): ConversationGraph {
  const lastNNodes = graph.nodes.slice(-n);
  const nodeIds = new Set(lastNNodes.map((n) => n.id));
  const edges = graph.edges.filter((e) => nodeIds.has(e.source) && nodeIds.has(e.target));

  return {
    ...graph,
    nodes: lastNNodes,
    edges,
  };
}
```

## P1-4：消息去重（Redis 滑动窗口）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/dedup.ts
import { getRedisClient } from './redis';
import crypto from 'crypto';
import { logger } from './logger';

const WINDOW_SECONDS = 300; // 5 分钟
const REDIS_PREFIX = 'dedup:';

// ===== 生成指纹 =====
export function generateFingerprint(accountId: string, from: string, content: string): string {
  return crypto
    .createHash('sha256')
    .update(`${accountId}:${from}:${content}`)
    .digest('hex');
}

// ===== 检查去重 =====
export async function isDuplicate(accountId: string, from: string, content: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const fingerprint = generateFingerprint(accountId, from, content);
  const key = `${REDIS_PREFIX}${fingerprint}`;
  const redis = getRedisClient();

  const exists = await redis.exists(key);
  if (exists) {
    logger.debug(`[Dedup] Duplicate message detected: ${fingerprint}`);
    return true;
  }

  await redis.setex(key, WINDOW_SECONDS, '1');
  return false;
}

// ===== 批量去重 =====
export async function batchDedup(
  messages: Array<{ accountId: string; from: string; content: string }>
): Promise<Array<{ index: number; isDuplicate: boolean }>> {
  const redis = getRedisClient();
  const pipeline = redis.pipeline();

  const fingerprints = messages.map((msg) => generateFingerprint(msg.accountId, msg.from, msg.content));

  for (const fp of fingerprints) {
    pipeline.exists(`${REDIS_PREFIX}${fp}`);
  }

  const results = await pipeline.exec();
  const duplicates = results.map((result, index) => {
    const exists = result[1] === 1;
    if (!exists) {
      // 标记为新消息
      redis.setex(`${REDIS_PREFIX}${fingerprints[index]}`, WINDOW_SECONDS, '1');
    }
    return { index, isDuplicate: exists };
  });

  return duplicates;
}

// ===== 手动清除（用于调试） =====
export async function clearDedup(accountId: string, from: string): Promise<void> {
  const redis = getRedisClient();
  const pattern = `${REDIS_PREFIX}*${accountId}:${from}:*`;
  const keys = await redis.keys(pattern);
  if (keys.length > 0) {
    await redis.del(keys);
    logger.info(`[Dedup] Cleared ${keys.length} entries for ${accountId}:${from}`);
  }
}
```

# 🟢 P2：护城河级

## P2-1：身份核（Identity Kernel）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/identity-kernel.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface IdentityVector {
  trustLevel: number; // 0-1
  emotionState: 'neutral' | 'positive' | 'negative' | 'angry';
  valueSensitivity: number; // 0-1
  urgency: number; // 0-1
  resistance: number; // 0-1
  conversionDistance: number; // 0-1，越接近 0 越接近成交
  socialRoleAffinity: number; // 0-1
}

const DEFAULT_IDENTITY: IdentityVector = {
  trustLevel: 0.5,
  emotionState: 'neutral',
  valueSensitivity: 0.5,
  urgency: 0.3,
  resistance: 0.5,
  conversionDistance: 0.8,
  socialRoleAffinity: 0.5,
};

// ===== 获取/创建身份核 =====
export async function getIdentityKernel(leadId: string): Promise<IdentityVector> {
  const record = await prisma.identityKernel.findUnique({
    where: { leadId },
  });

  if (!record) {
    // 创建默认身份核
    await prisma.identityKernel.create({
      data: {
        leadId,
        trustLevel: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.trustLevel,
        emotionState: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.emotionState,
        valueSensitivity: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.valueSensitivity,
        urgency: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.urgency,
        resistance: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.resistance,
        conversionDistance: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.conversionDistance,
        socialRoleAffinity: DEFAULT_IDENTITY.socialRoleAffinity,
      },
    });
    return DEFAULT_IDENTITY;
  }

  return {
    trustLevel: record.trustLevel,
    emotionState: record.emotionState as IdentityVector['emotionState'],
    valueSensitivity: record.valueSensitivity,
    urgency: record.urgency,
    resistance: record.resistance,
    conversionDistance: record.conversionDistance,
    socialRoleAffinity: record.socialRoleAffinity,
  };
}

// ===== 更新身份核 =====
export async function updateIdentityKernel(
  leadId: string,
  delta: Partial<IdentityVector>
): Promise<IdentityVector> {
  const current = await getIdentityKernel(leadId);

  // 如果是情绪状态，直接替换
  const updated: Partial<IdentityVector> = { ...current, ...delta };

  // 边界约束
  if (updated.trustLevel !== undefined) updated.trustLevel = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.trustLevel));
  if (updated.valueSensitivity !== undefined) updated.valueSensitivity = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.valueSensitivity));
  if (updated.urgency !== undefined) updated.urgency = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.urgency));
  if (updated.resistance !== undefined) updated.resistance = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.resistance));
  if (updated.conversionDistance !== undefined) updated.conversionDistance = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.conversionDistance));
  if (updated.socialRoleAffinity !== undefined) updated.socialRoleAffinity = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, updated.socialRoleAffinity));

  await prisma.identityKernel.upsert({
    where: { leadId },
    update: updated,
    create: {
      leadId,
      trustLevel: updated.trustLevel || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.trustLevel,
      emotionState: updated.emotionState || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.emotionState,
      valueSensitivity: updated.valueSensitivity || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.valueSensitivity,
      urgency: updated.urgency || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.urgency,
      resistance: updated.resistance || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.resistance,
      conversionDistance: updated.conversionDistance || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.conversionDistance,
      socialRoleAffinity: updated.socialRoleAffinity || DEFAULT_IDENTITY.socialRoleAffinity,
    },
  });

  logger.debug(`[Identity] Updated ${leadId}:`, updated);
  return updated as IdentityVector;
}

// ===== 基于消息更新身份核 =====
export async function updateFromMessage(leadId: string, message: string, intent: string): Promise<IdentityVector> {
  const delta: Partial<IdentityVector> = {};

  // 消息长度 → 参与度
  if (message.length > 20) {
    delta.urgency = Math.min(1, (delta.urgency || 0) + 0.1);
  }

  // 基于意图调整
  if (intent === 'PRICE') {
    delta.valueSensitivity = Math.min(1, (delta.valueSensitivity || 0) + 0.2);
    delta.urgency = Math.min(1, (delta.urgency || 0) + 0.15);
    delta.conversionDistance = Math.max(0, (delta.conversionDistance || 0) - 0.1);
  } else if (intent === 'REJECTION') {
    delta.resistance = Math.min(1, (delta.resistance || 0) + 0.2);
    delta.trustLevel = Math.max(0, (delta.trustLevel || 0) - 0.05);
  } else if (intent === 'SILENCE_BREAK') {
    delta.urgency = Math.min(1, (delta.urgency || 0) + 0.2);
    delta.conversionDistance = Math.max(0, (delta.conversionDistance || 0) - 0.05);
  } else if (intent === 'POSITIVE') {
    delta.trustLevel = Math.min(1, (delta.trustLevel || 0) + 0.1);
    delta.resistance = Math.max(0, (delta.resistance || 0) - 0.05);
  }

  return updateIdentityKernel(leadId, delta);
}
```

## P2-2：人格编译器（Persona Compiler）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/persona-compiler.ts
import { IdentityVector } from './identity-kernel';
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface PersonaTemplate {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  systemPrompt: string;
  idealVector: Partial<IdentityVector>;
  weight: number;
}

export interface CompiledPersona {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  systemPrompt: string;
  components: Array<{
    templateId: string;
    name: string;
    weight: number;
  }>;
  blendRatio: Record<string, number>;
}

// ===== 获取所有可用人设模板 =====
export async function getPersonaTemplates(): Promise<PersonaTemplate[]> {
  const personas = await prisma.persona.findMany({
    where: { isActive: true },
  });

  return personas.map((p) => ({
    id: p.id,
    name: p.name,
    description: p.description || '',
    systemPrompt: p.systemPrompt || '',
    idealVector: p.idealVector as Partial<IdentityVector> || {},
    weight: p.weight || 1,
  }));
}

// ===== 计算匹配度 =====
function calculateMatch(identity: IdentityVector, template: PersonaTemplate): number {
  let score = 0;
  let totalWeight = 0;

  const fields: Array<keyof IdentityVector> = [
    'trustLevel',
    'valueSensitivity',
    'urgency',
    'resistance',
    'conversionDistance',
    'socialRoleAffinity',
  ];

  for (const field of fields) {
    const ideal = template.idealVector[field];
    if (ideal !== undefined) {
      const diff = Math.abs(identity[field] - ideal);
      score += 1 - diff;
      totalWeight += 1;
    }
  }

  // 情绪状态匹配
  if (template.idealVector.emotionState && identity.emotionState === template.idealVector.emotionState) {
    score += 1;
    totalWeight += 1;
  }

  return totalWeight > 0 ? score / totalWeight : 0.5;
}

// ===== 编译人格 =====
export async function compilePersona(
  identity: IdentityVector,
  templates?: PersonaTemplate[]
): Promise<CompiledPersona> {
  if (!templates) {
    templates = await getPersonaTemplates();
  }

  if (templates.length === 0) {
    // 没有可用人设，返回默认
    return {
      id: 'default',
      name: '默认助手',
      systemPrompt: '你是一个专业、友好的助手。',
      components: [],
      blendRatio: {},
    };
  }

  // 计算每个模板的匹配度
  const matches = templates.map((t) => ({
    template: t,
    match: calculateMatch(identity, t),
  }));

  // 按匹配度排序，取 Top 3
  matches.sort((a, b) => b.match - a.match);
  const topMatches = matches.slice(0, 3);

  // 归一化权重
  const totalMatch = topMatches.reduce((sum, m) => sum + m.match, 0);
  const blendRatio: Record<string, number> = {};
  for (const m of topMatches) {
    blendRatio[m.template.id] = totalMatch > 0 ? m.match / totalMatch : 1 / topMatches.length;
  }

  // 构建混合 System Prompt
  const components: CompiledPersona['components'] = topMatches.map((m) => ({
    templateId: m.template.id,
    name: m.template.name,
    weight: blendRatio[m.template.id],
  }));

  const systemPrompt = topMatches
    .map((m) => `[${m.template.name} (${(blendRatio[m.template.id] * 100).toFixed(0)}%)] ${m.template.systemPrompt}`)
    .join('\n');

  // 生成编译后的人设名称
  const name = topMatches
    .map((m, i) => (i === 0 ? m.template.name : m.template.name))
    .join(' + ');

  logger.info(`[PersonaCompiler] Compiled: ${name}`, { blendRatio });

  return {
    id: `compiled_${Date.now()}`,
    name,
    systemPrompt,
    components,
    blendRatio,
  };
}

// ===== 混合人格输出 =====
export function getPersonaResponse(compiled: CompiledPersona, message: string): string {
  // 这里应该调用 LLM，传入混合后的 systemPrompt
  // 当前返回占位
  return `[${compiled.name}] 收到您的消息: ${message}`;
}
```

## P2-3：身份调度器（Identity Scheduler）

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/identity-scheduler.ts
import { IdentityVector, getIdentityKernel, updateIdentityKernel } from './identity-kernel';
import { compilePersona, CompiledPersona } from './persona-compiler';
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface ScheduledIdentity {
  leadId: string;
  identity: IdentityVector;
  persona: CompiledPersona;
  scheduledAt: number;
  reason: string;
}

// ===== 调度决策 =====
export async function scheduleIdentity(leadId: string): Promise<ScheduledIdentity> {
  const identity = await getIdentityKernel(leadId);

  // 根据身份向量决定调度策略
  let reason = 'default';

  // 高转化距离 → 需要教育
  if (identity.conversionDistance > 0.7) {
    reason = 'education_first';
  }
  // 高紧迫 + 高价值 → 直接成交
  else if (identity.urgency > 0.7 && identity.valueSensitivity > 0.6) {
    reason = 'close_now';
  }
  // 高抵抗 → 软性接触
  else if (identity.resistance > 0.6) {
    reason = 'soft_touch';
  }
  // 低信任 → 建立信任
  else if (identity.trustLevel < 0.3) {
    reason = 'trust_building';
  }
  // 中等一切 → 培育
  else {
    reason = 'nurture';
  }

  // 根据策略调整身份（临时漂移）
  const adjustedIdentity = { ...identity };

  switch (reason) {
    case 'close_now':
      adjustedIdentity.urgency = Math.min(1, adjustedIdentity.urgency + 0.2);
      break;
    case 'soft_touch':
      adjustedIdentity.resistance = Math.max(0, adjustedIdentity.resistance - 0.1);
      break;
    case 'trust_building':
      adjustedIdentity.socialRoleAffinity = Math.min(1, adjustedIdentity.socialRoleAffinity + 0.15);
      break;
    case 'education_first':
      adjustedIdentity.valueSensitivity = Math.min(1, adjustedIdentity.valueSensitivity + 0.15);
      break;
    default:
      break;
  }

  // 编译人格
  const persona = await compilePersona(adjustedIdentity);

  logger.info(`[IdentityScheduler] Scheduled ${leadId}: ${reason}`, {
    identity: adjustedIdentity,
    persona: persona.name,
  });

  return {
    leadId,
    identity: adjustedIdentity,
    persona,
    scheduledAt: Date.now(),
    reason,
  };
}

// ===== 执行调度（回调模式） =====
export async function executeScheduledIdentity(
  leadId: string,
  executor: (identity: ScheduledIdentity) => Promise<void>
): Promise<void> {
  const scheduled = await scheduleIdentity(leadId);
  await executor(scheduled);

  // 执行后更新身份（反馈闭环）
  await updateIdentityKernel(leadId, {
    conversionDistance: Math.max(0, scheduled.identity.conversionDistance - 0.02),
  });
}

// ===== 批量调度 =====
export async function batchSchedule(leadIds: string[]): Promise<ScheduledIdentity[]> {
  const results: ScheduledIdentity[] = [];
  for (const leadId of leadIds) {
    try {
      const scheduled = await scheduleIdentity(leadId);
      results.push(scheduled);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error({ err: error, leadId }, 'Batch schedule failed');
    }
  }
  return results;
}
```
