## P2-4：SOP 引擎

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/sop-engine.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

// ===== 类型定义 =====
export type SOPNodeType = 'start' | 'skill' | 'condition' | 'wait' | 'notify' | 'end';
export type SOPTriggerType = 'manual' | 'auto_schedule' | 'auto_event';

export interface SOPNode {
  id: string;
  type: SOPNodeType;
  label: string;
  skillId?: string;
  config: Record<string, unknown>;
  position: { x: number; y: number };
}

export interface SOPEdge {
  id: string;
  source: string;
  target: string;
  condition?: string;
}

export interface SOPDefinition {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  triggerType: SOPTriggerType;
  triggerCondition: Record<string, unknown>;
  nodes: SOPNode[];
  edges: SOPEdge[];
  isActive: boolean;
}

export interface SOPInstance {
  id: string;
  sopId: string;
  leadId: string;
  currentNodeId: string;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'aborted';
  context: Record<string, unknown>;
  startedAt: number;
  completedAt?: number;
}

export interface SOPNodeLog {
  instanceId: string;
  nodeId: string;
  skillName: string;
  input: Record<string, unknown>;
  output: Record<string, unknown>;
  status: 'success' | 'failed' | 'skipped';
  errorMessage?: string;
  startedAt: number;
  completedAt: number;
  durationMs: number;
}

// ===== Skill 注册中心 =====
export interface Skill {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  category: 'recognition' | 'evaluation' | 'generation' | 'execution' | 'notification';
  execute: (context: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<Record<string, unknown>>;
}

const skillRegistry = new Map<string, Skill>();

export function registerSkill(skill: Skill): void {
  skillRegistry.set(skill.id, skill);
  logger.info(`[SOP] Skill registered: ${skill.id}`);
}

export function getSkill(id: string): Skill | undefined {
  return skillRegistry.get(id);
}

// ===== SOP 定义 CRUD =====
export async function createSOP(data: Omit<SOPDefinition, 'id'>): Promise<SOPDefinition> {
  const sop: SOPDefinition = {
    id: uuidv4(),
    ...data,
  };

  await prisma.sopDefinition.create({
    data: {
      id: sop.id,
      name: sop.name,
      description: sop.description || '',
      triggerType: sop.triggerType,
      triggerCondition: JSON.stringify(sop.triggerCondition),
      nodes: JSON.stringify(sop.nodes),
      edges: JSON.stringify(sop.edges),
      isActive: sop.isActive,
    },
  });

  logger.info(`[SOP] Created: ${sop.name} (${sop.id})`);
  return sop;
}

export async function getSOP(id: string): Promise<SOPDefinition | null> {
  const record = await prisma.sopDefinition.findUnique({ where: { id } });
  if (!record) return null;

  return {
    id: record.id,
    name: record.name,
    description: record.description || '',
    triggerType: record.triggerType as SOPTriggerType,
    triggerCondition: JSON.parse(record.triggerCondition || '{}'),
    nodes: JSON.parse(record.nodes || '[]'),
    edges: JSON.parse(record.edges || '[]'),
    isActive: record.isActive,
  };
}

// ===== SOP 执行引擎 =====
export class SOPRuntime {
  private runningInstances = new Map<string, SOPInstance>();

  async start(sopId: string, leadId: string, initialContext?: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<string> {
    const definition = await getSOP(sopId);
    if (!definition) throw new Error(`SOP not found: ${sopId}`);

    // 找第一个 START 节点
    const startNode = definition.nodes.find((n) => n.type === 'start');
    if (!startNode) throw new Error('SOP has no START node');

    const instanceId = uuidv4();
    const instance: SOPInstance = {
      id: instanceId,
      sopId,
      leadId,
      currentNodeId: startNode.id,
      status: 'running',
      context: initialContext || {},
      startedAt: Date.now(),
    };

    this.runningInstances.set(instanceId, instance);

    // 持久化
    await prisma.sopInstance.create({
      data: {
        id: instanceId,
        sopDefinitionId: sopId,
        leadId,
        currentNodeId: startNode.id,
        status: 'running',
        context: JSON.stringify(initialContext || {}),
        startedAt: new Date(instance.startedAt),
      },
    });

    logger.info(`[SOP] Instance started: ${instanceId} for ${leadId}`);

    // 异步执行
    this.executeLoop(instanceId).catch((error) => {
      logger.error({ err: error, instanceId }, 'SOP execution failed');
    });

    return instanceId;
  }

  private async executeLoop(instanceId: string): Promise<void> {
    const instance = this.runningInstances.get(instanceId);
    if (!instance) return;

    const definition = await getSOP(instance.sopId);
    if (!definition) return;

    const nodeMap = new Map(definition.nodes.map((n) => [n.id, n]));
    const edgeMap = new Map<string, SOPEdge[]>();
    for (const edge of definition.edges) {
      if (!edgeMap.has(edge.source)) edgeMap.set(edge.source, []);
      edgeMap.get(edge.source)!.push(edge);
    }

    let currentNodeId = instance.currentNodeId;

    while (instance.status === 'running' && currentNodeId) {
      const node = nodeMap.get(currentNodeId);
      if (!node) break;

      // 执行节点
      const result = await this.executeNode(instance, node, definition);

      if (result.status === 'failed') {
        instance.status = 'failed';
        break;
      }

      if (result.status === 'paused') {
        instance.status = 'paused';
        break;
      }

      // 找下一个节点
      const edges = edgeMap.get(currentNodeId) || [];
      let nextNodeId: string | undefined;

      if (edges.length === 1) {
        nextNodeId = edges[0].target;
      } else if (edges.length > 1) {
        // 条件分支
        const branch = result.branch || 'DEFAULT';
        const matched = edges.find((e) => e.condition === branch);
        nextNodeId = matched?.target || edges[0].target;
      }

      currentNodeId = nextNodeId;
      instance.currentNodeId = currentNodeId || '';

      // 更新数据库
      await prisma.sopInstance.update({
        where: { id: instanceId },
        data: {
          currentNodeId: currentNodeId || '',
          context: JSON.stringify(instance.context),
          status: instance.status,
        },
      });

      // 检查是否结束
      if (currentNodeId && nodeMap.get(currentNodeId)?.type === 'end') {
        instance.status = 'completed';
        instance.completedAt = Date.now();
        break;
      }
    }

    // 最终状态更新
    await prisma.sopInstance.update({
      where: { id: instanceId },
      data: {
        status: instance.status,
        completedAt: instance.completedAt ? new Date(instance.completedAt) : null,
      },
    });

    this.runningInstances.delete(instanceId);
    logger.info(`[SOP] Instance ${instanceId} finished: ${instance.status}`);
  }

  private async executeNode(
    instance: SOPInstance,
    node: SOPNode,
    definition: SOPDefinition
  ): Promise<{ status: 'success' | 'failed' | 'paused'; branch?: string }> {
    const startedAt = Date.now();
    const log: Partial<SOPNodeLog> = {
      instanceId: instance.id,
      nodeId: node.id,
      skillName: '',
      input: {},
      output: {},
      status: 'success',
      startedAt,
    };

    try {
      if (node.type === 'skill' && node.skillId) {
        const skill = getSkill(node.skillId);
        if (!skill) throw new Error(`Skill not found: ${node.skillId}`);

        log.skillName = skill.name;
        log.input = instance.context;

        const result = await skill.execute(instance.context);
        log.output = result;

        // 合并结果到上下文
        instance.context = { ...instance.context, ...result };
      } else if (node.type === 'condition') {
        const field = node.config.field as string;
        const operator = node.config.operator as string;
        const value = node.config.value;

        const actual = instance.context[field];
        let branch = 'NO';

        if (operator === '>=') branch = actual >= value ? 'YES' : 'NO';
        else if (operator === '>') branch = actual > value ? 'YES' : 'NO';
        else if (operator === '==') branch = actual === value ? 'YES' : 'NO';
        else if (operator === '<=') branch = actual <= value ? 'YES' : 'NO';

        log.output = { branch };
        return { status: 'success', branch };
      } else if (node.type === 'wait') {
        const seconds = (node.config.seconds as number) || 60;
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, seconds * 1000));
        log.output = { waited: seconds };
      } else if (node.type === 'notify') {
        const message = (node.config.message as string) || 'SOP node completed';
        log.output = { notified: true, message };
        logger.info(`[SOP] Notification: ${message}`, { leadId: instance.leadId });
      }

      log.status = 'success';
    } catch (error) {
      log.status = 'failed';
      log.errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
      logger.error({ err: error, instanceId: instance.id }, 'SOP node failed');
    }

    log.completedAt = Date.now();
    log.durationMs = log.completedAt - log.startedAt;

    // 保存日志
    await prisma.sopNodeLog.create({
      data: {
        sopInstanceId: log.instanceId!,
        nodeId: log.nodeId!,
        skillName: log.skillName || '',
        input: JSON.stringify(log.input || {}),
        output: JSON.stringify(log.output || {}),
        status: log.status!,
        errorMessage: log.errorMessage || null,
        startedAt: new Date(log.startedAt!),
        completedAt: new Date(log.completedAt!),
        durationMs: log.durationMs!,
      },
    });

    return { status: log.status };
  }

  async pause(instanceId: string): Promise<void> {
    const instance = this.runningInstances.get(instanceId);
    if (instance) {
      instance.status = 'paused';
      await prisma.sopInstance.update({
        where: { id: instanceId },
        data: { status: 'paused' },
      });
      logger.info(`[SOP] Instance ${instanceId} paused`);
    }
  }

  async resume(instanceId: string): Promise<void> {
    const instance = this.runningInstances.get(instanceId);
    if (instance && instance.status === 'paused') {
      instance.status = 'running';
      await prisma.sopInstance.update({
        where: { id: instanceId },
        data: { status: 'running' },
      });
      logger.info(`[SOP] Instance ${instanceId} resumed`);
      // 继续执行循环
      this.executeLoop(instanceId).catch((error) => {
        logger.error({ err: error, instanceId }, 'SOP resume failed');
      });
    }
  }

  async stop(instanceId: string): Promise<void> {
    const instance = this.runningInstances.get(instanceId);
    if (instance) {
      instance.status = 'aborted';
      await prisma.sopInstance.update({
        where: { id: instanceId },
        data: { status: 'aborted' },
      });
      this.runningInstances.delete(instanceId);
      logger.info(`[SOP] Instance ${instanceId} aborted`);
    }
  }
}

// ===== 注册内置 Skills =====
export function registerBuiltinSkills(): void {
  registerSkill({
    id: 'intent_recognition',
    name: '意图识别',
    description: '识别客户消息的意图',
    category: 'recognition',
    execute: async (ctx) => {
      const message = ctx.message as string;
      let intent = 'GENERAL';
      if (message.includes('多少钱') || message.includes('价格')) intent = 'PRICE';
      else if (message.includes('不需要') || message.includes('考虑')) intent = 'REJECTION';
      else if (message.includes('在吗') || message.includes('好久不见')) intent = 'SILENCE_BREAK';
      return { intent, confidence: 0.9 };
    },
  });

  registerSkill({
    id: 'reply_generate',
    name: '生成话术',
    description: '根据上下文生成回复',
    category: 'generation',
    execute: async (ctx) => {
      // 这里可接入真实 LLM
      const message = ctx.message as string;
      return {
        reply: `收到您的消息: ${message}`,
        extracted: { intent: ctx.intent || 'GENERAL' },
        status: '跟进中',
      };
    },
  });

  registerSkill({
    id: 'crm_update',
    name: '更新CRM',
    description: '更新客户状态',
    category: 'execution',
    execute: async (ctx) => {
      const status = ctx.status as string || '跟进中';
      // 实际会写入数据库
      return { updated: true, status };
    },
  });

  registerSkill({
    id: 'send_message',
    name: '发送消息',
    description: '发送消息给客户',
    category: 'execution',
    execute: async (ctx) => {
      const to = ctx.leadId as string;
      const content = ctx.reply as string;
      logger.info(`[SOP] Sending message to ${to}: ${content}`);
      return { sent: true, to, content };
    },
  });
}
```

## P2-5：视频号爆流量模型

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/video-optimizer.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface VideoPerformance {
  videoId: string;
  title: string;
  views: number;
  likes: number;
  comments: number;
  shares: number;
  watchTime: number; // 平均观看时长（秒）
  completionRate: number; // 0-1
  negativeFeedback: number; // 0-1
  createdAt: number;
}

export interface ViralScore {
  videoId: string;
  score: number;
  breakdown: {
    ctr: number;
    commentRate: number;
    watchTime: number;
    shareRate: number;
  };
  recommendations: string[];
}

// ===== 计算病毒系数 =====
export function calculateViralScore(perf: VideoPerformance): ViralScore {
  const ctr = perf.views > 0 ? perf.likes / perf.views : 0;
  const commentRate = perf.views > 0 ? perf.comments / perf.views : 0;
  const shareRate = perf.views > 0 ? perf.shares / perf.views : 0;

  // 归一化
  const normWatchTime = Math.min(perf.watchTime / 60, 1);
  const normCompletion = perf.completionRate;

  const score =
    ctr * 0.35 +
    commentRate * 0.25 +
    normWatchTime * 0.15 +
    normCompletion * 0.15 +
    shareRate * 0.1;

  // 负向惩罚
  const adjustedScore = Math.max(0, score - perf.negativeFeedback * 0.2);

  const recommendations: string[] = [];

  if (ctr < 0.05) recommendations.push('🎬 优化前3秒内容，提升点击率');
  if (commentRate < 0.02) recommendations.push('💬 增加互动钩子，引导评论');
  if (normWatchTime < 0.3) recommendations.push('📊 前15秒需要更强吸引力');
  if (normCompletion < 0.2) recommendations.push('🔄 结尾加反转或悬念');
  if (shareRate < 0.01) recommendations.push('📤 增加分享引导语');

  return {
    videoId: perf.videoId,
    score: Math.round(adjustedScore * 100),
    breakdown: {
      ctr: Math.round(ctr * 10000) / 100,
      commentRate: Math.round(commentRate * 10000) / 100,
      watchTime: Math.round(normWatchTime * 100),
      shareRate: Math.round(shareRate * 10000) / 100,
    },
    recommendations,
  };
}

// ===== 优化建议生成 =====
export function generateOptimizationSuggestions(perf: VideoPerformance): string[] {
  const score = calculateViralScore(perf);
  return score.recommendations;
}

// ===== 跟踪视频表现 =====
export async function trackVideoPerformance(
  videoId: string,
  data: Omit<VideoPerformance, 'videoId' | 'createdAt'>
): Promise<void> {
  const performance: VideoPerformance = {
    videoId,
    ...data,
    createdAt: Date.now(),
  };

  await prisma.videoPerformance.create({
    data: {
      videoId,
      title: data.title || '',
      views: data.views || 0,
      likes: data.likes || 0,
      comments: data.comments || 0,
      shares: data.shares || 0,
      watchTime: data.watchTime || 0,
      completionRate: data.completionRate || 0,
      negativeFeedback: data.negativeFeedback || 0,
      createdAt: new Date(performance.createdAt),
    },
  });

  logger.info(`[Video] Tracked performance for ${videoId}`, { views: data.views });
}
```

## P2-6：评论截流算法

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/comment-capture.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

export interface CommentIntent {
  type: 'PRICE' | 'PURCHASE' | 'COMPARISON' | 'CURIOUS' | 'LOW';
  score: number; // 0-100
  urgency: number; // 0-100
}

export interface CommentLead {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  nickname: string;
  content: string;
  platform: string;
  postId: string;
  intent: CommentIntent;
  captured: boolean;
  leadId?: string;
}

// ===== 意图识别 =====
export function detectCommentIntent(content: string): CommentIntent {
  const patterns = [
    { type: 'PRICE' as const, keywords: ['多少钱', '价格', '怎么卖', '报价'], weight: 90 },
    { type: 'PURCHASE' as const, keywords: ['怎么买', '下单', '购买', '链接'], weight: 85 },
    { type: 'COMPARISON' as const, keywords: ['哪个好', '对比', '区别', '还是'], weight: 70 },
    { type: 'CURIOUS' as const, keywords: ['什么东西', '这是什么', '干嘛的'], weight: 50 },
  ];

  let maxScore = 0;
  let matchedType: CommentIntent['type'] = 'LOW';

  for (const pattern of patterns) {
    for (const kw of pattern.keywords) {
      if (content.includes(kw)) {
        const score = pattern.weight;
        if (score > maxScore) {
          maxScore = score;
          matchedType = pattern.type;
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // 随机调整（防过于机械）
  const noise = Math.random() * 10 - 5;
  const finalScore = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, maxScore + noise));

  // 紧迫度：含时间词或情绪词
  let urgency = 30;
  if (content.includes('马上') || content.includes('现在') || content.includes('急')) urgency = 90;
  else if (content.includes('想') || content.includes('要') || content.includes('打算')) urgency = 70;
  else if (content.includes('看看') || content.includes('了解')) urgency = 40;

  return {
    type: matchedType,
    score: finalScore,
    urgency,
  };
}

// ===== 截流决策 =====
export function shouldCapture(intent: CommentIntent, existingLeads: number): boolean {
  // 高意图必须截流
  if (intent.type === 'PRICE' && intent.score > 70) return true;
  if (intent.type === 'PURCHASE' && intent.score > 60) return true;

  // 中意图 + 高紧迫
  if (intent.type === 'COMPARISON' && intent.urgency > 70) return true;

  // 当前账号已有太多线索，限流
  if (existingLeads > 20) return false;

  // 随机抽样（防止全量截流）
  if (intent.type === 'CURIOUS' && Math.random() > 0.3) return false;

  return false;
}

// ===== 处理评论 =====
export async function processComment(data: {
  userId: string;
  nickname: string;
  content: string;
  platform: string;
  postId: string;
}): Promise<{ captured: boolean; leadId?: string; reply?: string }> {
  // 1. 检测意图
  const intent = detectCommentIntent(data.content);
  logger.debug(`[Comment] Intent: ${intent.type} (${intent.score}) for ${data.userId}`);

  // 2. 检查历史截流次数
  const existingLeads = await prisma.lead.count({
    where: {
      source: 'comment',
      sourceId: data.userId,
    },
  });

  // 3. 截流决策
  const captured = shouldCapture(intent, existingLeads);

  if (!captured) {
    return { captured: false };
  }

  // 4. 创建线索
  const lead = await prisma.lead.create({
    data: {
      name: data.nickname || `用户_${data.userId}`,
      wxId: data.userId,
      source: 'comment',
      sourceId: data.postId,
      intentScore: intent.score,
      valueScore: intent.urgency,
      stage: 'NEW',
      status: 'active',
      profile: JSON.stringify({
        platform: data.platform,
        comment: data.content,
        intent: intent.type,
      }),
    },
  });

  // 5. 生成回复（引导私信）
  let reply = '感谢关注！';
  if (intent.type === 'PRICE') {
    reply = '已私信您详细配置和报价，请查收！';
  } else if (intent.type === 'PURCHASE') {
    reply = '感谢您的支持！已私信您购买链接和专属优惠！';
  } else if (intent.type === 'COMPARISON') {
    reply = '已私信您详细的对比表，帮您做最优选择！';
  } else {
    reply = '已私信您更详细的资料，方便进一步了解！';
  }

  // 6. 记录评论
  await prisma.comment.create({
    data: {
      postId: data.postId,
      userId: data.userId,
      nickname: data.nickname,
      content: data.content,
      platform: data.platform,
      intentScore: intent.score,
      replyStatus: 'converted',
      leadId: lead.id,
    },
  });

  logger.info(`[Comment] Captured lead: ${lead.id} (${intent.type})`);

  return {
    captured: true,
    leadId: lead.id,
    reply,
  };
}
```

---

## P2-7：LTV 用户价值分层

```typescript
// frontend/src/lib/ltv-calculator.ts
import { prisma } from '@/server/prisma';
import { logger } from './logger';

export type LTVTier = 'A' | 'B' | 'C' | 'D';

export interface LTVResult {
  leadId: string;
  tier: LTVTier;
  score: number; // 0-100
  predictedRevenue: number;
  conversionProbability: number; // 0-1
  lifetimeMonths: number;
  factors: {
    purchasePower: number;
    interactionFrequency: number;
    intentStrength: number;
    trustLevel: number;
    recency: number;
  };
}

// ===== LTV 计算 =====
export function calculateLTV(lead: {
  id: string;
  intentScore: number;
  valueScore: number;
  stage: string;
  interactionCount: number;
  lastContactDays: number;
  profile: Record<string, unknown>;
}): LTVResult {
  // 1. 购买力
  const purchasePower = Math.min(
    (lead.valueScore || 50) / 100 +
      (lead.profile?.budget ? Math.min(parseInt(lead.profile.budget as string) / 100, 1) : 0),
    1
  );

  // 2. 互动频率
  const interactionFrequency = Math.min(lead.interactionCount / 20, 1);

  // 3. 意图强度
  const intentStrength = (lead.intentScore || 50) / 100;

  // 4. 信任度（基于阶段）
  const trustMap: Record<string, number> = {
    NEW: 0.2,
    ENGAGED: 0.4,
    QUALIFIED: 0.6,
    HOT: 0.8,
    CONVERTED: 0.9,
    LOST: 0.1,
  };
  const trustLevel = trustMap[lead.stage] || 0.3;

  // 5. 最近活跃度
  const recency = Math.max(0, 1 - (lead.lastContactDays || 30) / 30);

  // 6. 综合评分
  const score =
    purchasePower * 0.3 +
    interactionFrequency * 0.2 +
    intentStrength * 0.25 +
    trustLevel * 0.15 +
    recency * 0.1;

  const finalScore = Math.round(Math.min(100, score * 100));

  // 7. 分档
  let tier: LTVTier;
  if (finalScore > 80) tier = 'A';
  else if (finalScore > 60) tier = 'B';
  else if (finalScore > 35) tier = 'C';
  else tier = 'D';

  // 8. 预测收入
  const baseRevenue = tier === 'A' ? 5000 : tier === 'B' ? 2000 : tier === 'C' ? 500 : 100;
  const predictedRevenue = baseRevenue * (0.7 + 0.3 * (finalScore / 100));

  // 9. 转化概率
  const conversionProbability = 0.3 + 0.6 * (finalScore / 100);

  // 10. 生命周期（月）
  const lifetimeMonths = tier === 'A' ? 12 : tier === 'B' ? 8 : tier === 'C' ? 4 : 2;

  return {
    leadId: lead.id,
    tier,
    score: finalScore,
    predictedRevenue,
    conversionProbability,
    lifetimeMonths,
    factors: {
      purchasePower: Math.round(purchasePower * 100),
      interactionFrequency: Math.round(interactionFrequency * 100),
      intentStrength: Math.round(intentStrength * 100),
      trustLevel: Math.round(trustLevel * 100),
      recency: Math.round(recency * 100),
    },
  };
}

// ===== 批量计算 LTV =====
export async function batchCalculateLTV(leadIds: string[]): Promise<LTVResult[]> {
  const leads = await prisma.lead.findMany({
    where: { id: { in: leadIds } },
  });

  return leads.map((lead) => {
    const interactions = lead.interactionCount || 0;
    const lastContact = lead.updatedAt ? Math.floor((Date.now() - lead.updatedAt.getTime()) / 86400000) : 30;

    return calculateLTV({
      id: lead.id,
      intentScore: lead.intentScore || 0,
      valueScore: lead.valueScore || 0,
      stage: lead.stage || 'NEW',
      interactionCount: interactions,
      lastContactDays: lastContact,
      profile: lead.profile ? JSON.parse(lead.profile) : {},
    });
  });
}

// ===== 获取分层建议 =====
export function getTierStrategy(tier: LTVTier): {
  priority: number;
  frequency: string;
  approach: string;
  recommendation: string;
} {
  switch (tier) {
    case 'A':
      return {
        priority: 1,
        frequency: '每日触达',
        approach: '强转化 + 人工跟进',
        recommendation: '优先分配最优质的销售资源，提供专属方案和优惠',
      };
    case 'B':
      return {
        priority: 2,
        frequency: '每2-3天触达',
        approach: '培育 + 内容驱动',
        recommendation: '提供案例对比、产品价值内容，引导向A类转化',
      };
    case 'C':
      return {
        priority: 3,
        frequency: '每周触达',
        approach: '自动化维护',
        recommendation: '定期发送有价值内容，保持触点，低成本维护',
      };
    case 'D':
      return {
        priority: 4,
        frequency: '每月触达',
        approach: '冷处理',
        recommendation: '不主动消耗资源，仅在触发事件时响应',
      };
  }
}
```

## P3-1：Onboarding 首次启动引导

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/Onboarding.tsx
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';

const STEPS = [
  {
    id: 'welcome',
    icon: '👋',
    title: '欢迎使用旺财',
    description: '你的 AI 私域营销助手已就位，让我们开始配置吧',
  },
  {
    id: 'config',
    icon: '⚙️',
    title: '配置 AI 模型',
    description: '输入你的 API Key，AI 才能开始工作',
    fields: [
      { key: 'apiKey', label: 'API Key', type: 'password', placeholder: 'sk-...' },
      { key: 'model', label: '模型', type: 'select', options: ['deepseek-chat', 'gpt-4o', 'gpt-4o-mini'] },
    ],
  },
  {
    id: 'persona',
    icon: '🧠',
    title: '选择销售人设',
    description: 'AI 将以你选择的风格与客户对话',
    options: [
      { id: 'sales-expert', name: '🎯 销售专家', desc: '专业成交导向，强推进' },
      { id: 'friendly', name: '🤝 亲和顾问', desc: '温和建立信任，拉近距离' },
      { id: 'professional', name: '📊 专业咨询', desc: '深度专业解答，树立权威' },
    ],
  },
  {
    id: 'wechat',
    icon: '📱',
    title: '连接微信',
    description: '扫码绑定你的微信账号，开始接收消息',
  },
  {
    id: 'complete',
    icon: '🎉',
    title: '准备就绪！',
    description: '你的旺财已经配置完成，开始使用吧',
  },
];

export function Onboarding({ onComplete }: { onComplete?: () => void }) {
  const [step, setStep] = useState(0);
  const [config, setConfig] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const currentStep = STEPS[step];
  const isLast = step === STEPS.length - 1;

  const handleNext = async () => {
    if (isLast) {
      setLoading(true);
      // 保存配置
      localStorage.setItem('waos_onboarding_completed', 'true');
      localStorage.setItem('waos_config', JSON.stringify(config));
      setLoading(false);
      onComplete?.();
      return;
    }

    // 验证配置步骤
    if (currentStep.id === 'config' && !config.apiKey) {
      alert('请输入 API Key');
      return;
    }

    setStep(step + 1);
  };

  const handleSkip = () => {
    localStorage.setItem('waos_onboarding_completed', 'true');
    onComplete?.();
  };

  const progress = ((step + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-[#05070D] p-4">
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        className="w-full max-w-lg"
      >
        {/* 进度条 */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mb-2">
            {STEPS.map((_, i) => (
              <span key={i} className={i <= step ? 'text-waos-primary' : ''}>
                {i + 1}
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className="h-1 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
            <div
              className="h-full bg-waos-primary rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
              style={{ width: `${progress}%` }}
            />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 内容 */}
        <div className="glass p-8 rounded-2xl border border-white/10">
          <div className="text-center mb-6">
            <div className="text-5xl mb-3">{currentStep.icon}</div>
            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-white">{currentStep.title}</h2>
            <p className="text-white/60 text-sm mt-1">{currentStep.description}</p>
          </div>

          {/* 表单字段 */}
          {currentStep.fields?.map((field) => (
            <div key={field.key} className="mb-4">
              <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">{field.label}</label>
              {field.type === 'select' ? (
                <select
                  value={config[field.key] || field.options?.[0] || ''}
                  onChange={(e) => setConfig({ ...config, [field.key]: e.target.value })}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
                >
                  {field.options?.map((opt) => (
                    <option key={opt} value={opt}>
                      {opt}
                    </option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              ) : (
                <input
                  type={field.type || 'text'}
                  value={config[field.key] || ''}
                  onChange={(e) => setConfig({ ...config, [field.key]: e.target.value })}
                  placeholder={field.placeholder}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
                />
              )}
            </div>
          ))}

          {/* 人设选择 */}
          {currentStep.options && (
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {currentStep.options.map((opt) => (
                <button
                  key={opt.id}
                  onClick={() => setConfig({ ...config, persona: opt.id })}
                  className={`w-full p-3 rounded-lg text-left transition-all ${
                    config.persona === opt.id
                      ? 'bg-waos-primary/20 border-2 border-waos-primary'
                      : 'bg-white/5 border-2 border-transparent hover:bg-white/10'
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className="font-medium text-white">{opt.name}</div>
                  <div className="text-sm text-white/40">{opt.desc}</div>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 微信扫码占位 */}
          {currentStep.id === 'wechat' && (
            <div className="p-8 text-center border-2 border-dashed border-white/20 rounded-xl">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📱</div>
              <div className="text-white/60">扫码绑定功能即将上线</div>
              <div className="text-white/30 text-sm">目前支持模拟模式测试</div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 完成页 */}
          {currentStep.id === 'complete' && (
            <div className="text-center py-4">
              <div className="text-6xl mb-4">🎉</div>
              <div className="text-white/80">一切就绪！</div>
              <div className="text-sm text-white/40 mt-2">你可以开始使用旺财了</div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 按钮 */}
          <div className="flex justify-between mt-6 pt-4 border-t border-white/5">
            {step > 0 && step < STEPS.length - 1 && (
              <button
                onClick={() => setStep(step - 1)}
                className="text-white/40 hover:text-white/80 transition"
              >
                上一步
              </button>
            )}
            {step === 0 && <div />}
            <div className="flex gap-3 ml-auto">
              <button
                onClick={handleSkip}
                className="text-white/30 hover:text-white/60 transition text-sm"
              >
                {step === STEPS.length - 1 ? '进入' : '跳过'}
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleNext}
                disabled={loading}
                className="px-6 py-2 rounded-lg bg-waos-primary text-black font-medium hover:opacity-80 transition disabled:opacity-50"
              >
                {loading ? '处理中...' : isLast ? '🚀 开始使用' : '下一步 →'}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 集成到 App

```tsx
// frontend/src/app/page.tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Onboarding } from '@/components/Onboarding';
import { MainLayout } from '@/components/layout/MainLayout';

export default function HomePage() {
  const [showOnboarding, setShowOnboarding] = useState(true);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    const completed = localStorage.getItem('waos_onboarding_completed') === 'true';
    setShowOnboarding(!completed);
    setLoading(false);
  }, []);

  if (loading) return <div className="h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-white/30">加载中...</div>;

  if (showOnboarding) {
    return <Onboarding onComplete={() => setShowOnboarding(false)} />;
  }

  return <MainLayout />;
}
```

## P3-3：全局快捷键系统

### 快捷键 Hook

```typescript
// frontend/src/hooks/useKeyboardShortcuts.ts
'use client';

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

type ShortcutAction = () => void;

interface Shortcut {
  id: string;
  keys: string[];
  description: string;
  action: ShortcutAction;
}

const shortcutRegistry = new Map<string, Shortcut>();

export function registerShortcut(shortcut: Shortcut): void {
  const key = shortcut.keys.sort().join('+');
  shortcutRegistry.set(key, shortcut);
}

export function useKeyboardShortcuts(actions: Record<string, ShortcutAction>): void {
  const actionsRef = useRef(actions);

  useEffect(() => {
    actionsRef.current = actions;
  }, [actions]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
      // 忽略输入框中的快捷键（除了 Enter）
      const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
      if (target.tagName === 'INPUT' || target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') {
        if (event.key !== 'Enter' && !(event.ctrlKey && event.key === 'Enter')) {
          return;
        }
      }

      const keys: string[] = [];
      if (event.ctrlKey) keys.push('Control');
      if (event.shiftKey) keys.push('Shift');
      if (event.altKey) keys.push('Alt');
      if (event.metaKey) keys.push('Meta');
      keys.push(event.key);

      const key = keys.sort().join('+');

      // 查找匹配的快捷键
      const shortcut = shortcutRegistry.get(key);
      if (shortcut) {
        event.preventDefault();
        shortcut.action();
        return;
      }

      // 查找动态注册的快捷键
      const action = actionsRef.current[key];
      if (action) {
        event.preventDefault();
        action();
      }
    };

    window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
  }, []);
}

// ===== 预设快捷键 =====
export const DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS = [
  { id: 'nav.workbench', keys: ['Control', '1'], description: '工作台' },
  { id: 'nav.customers', keys: ['Control', '2'], description: '客户管理' },
  { id: 'nav.comments', keys: ['Control', '3'], description: '评论中心' },
  { id: 'nav.knowledge', keys: ['Control', '4'], description: '知识库' },
  { id: 'nav.sop', keys: ['Control', '5'], description: 'SOP 引擎' },
  { id: 'nav.analytics', keys: ['Control', '6'], description: '数据看板' },
  { id: 'action.reply', keys: ['R'], description: '快速回复' },
  { id: 'action.escalate', keys: ['E'], description: '提升优先级' },
  { id: 'action.human', keys: ['H'], description: '转人工' },
  { id: 'action.pin', keys: ['P'], description: '钉住会话' },
  { id: 'global.search', keys: ['Control', 'K'], description: '全局搜索' },
  { id: 'global.help', keys: ['Control', 'H'], description: '帮助中心' },
];
```

### 快捷键面板

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/ShortcutsHelp.tsx
'use client';

import { DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS } from '@/hooks/useKeyboardShortcuts';

interface ShortcutsHelpProps {
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function ShortcutsHelp({ open, onClose }: ShortcutsHelpProps) {
  if (!open) return null;

  const categories = {
    navigation: { label: '🧭 导航', shortcuts: DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS.filter((s) => s.id.startsWith('nav.')) },
    action: { label: '⚡ 动作', shortcuts: DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS.filter((s) => s.id.startsWith('action.')) },
    global: { label: '🌐 全局', shortcuts: DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS.filter((s) => s.id.startsWith('global.')) },
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-50" onClick={onClose}>
      <div
        className="bg-[#1a1a2e] rounded-2xl p-6 max-w-lg w-full max-h-[80vh] overflow-y-auto border border-white/10"
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-white">⌨️ 键盘快捷键</h2>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="text-white/40 hover:text-white/80">
            ✕
          </button>
        </div>

        {Object.values(categories).map((cat) => (
          <div key={cat.label} className="mb-4">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/60 mb-2">{cat.label}</h3>
            <div className="space-y-1">
              {cat.shortcuts.map((s) => (
                <div key={s.id} className="flex justify-between items-center px-3 py-1.5 rounded hover:bg-white/5">
                  <span className="text-sm text-white/80">{s.description}</span>
                  <kbd className="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-mono rounded bg-white/10 text-white/60">
                    {s.keys.map((k) => (k === 'Control' ? '⌘' : k === 'Shift' ? '⇧' : k === 'Alt' ? '⌥' : k)).join(' + ')}
                  </kbd>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        <div className="text-xs text-white/30 mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/5">
          💡 按 <kbd className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-white/10 text-white/60">⌘</kbd> +{' '}
          <kbd className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-white/10 text-white/60">K</kbd> 随时打开此面板
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## P3-4：帮助中心

```tsx
// frontend/src/app/help/page.tsx
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { ShortcutsHelp } from '@/components/ShortcutsHelp';

const FAQS = [
```

### 体积分析脚本

```typescript
// scripts/optimize-bundle.js
const { execSync } = require('child_process');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

console.log('📦 分析打包体积...');

// 1. 分析 node_modules
const nodeModules = path.join(process.cwd(), 'node_modules');
const packages = {};

function walkDir(dir, prefix = '') {
  try {
    const items = fs.readdirSync(dir);
    for (const item of items) {
      if (item.startsWith('.')) continue;
      const fullPath = path.join(dir, item);
      const stats = fs.statSync(fullPath);
      if (stats.isDirectory()) {
        walkDir(fullPath, path.join(prefix, item));
      } else if (item === 'package.json') {
        try {
          const pkg = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8'));
          const name = pkg.name || prefix;
          if (!packages[name]) packages[name] = 0;
          packages[name] += stats.size;
        } catch (_) {}
      }
    }
  } catch (_) {}
}

walkDir(nodeModules);

const sorted = Object.entries(packages)
  .filter(([, size]) => size > 1024 * 100)
  .sort(([, a], [, b]) => b - a);

console.log('\n📊 最大的 20 个包:');
sorted.slice(0, 20).forEach(([name, size], i) => {
  console.log(`${i + 1}. ${name.padEnd(30)} ${(size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB`);
});

// 给出优化建议
console.log('\n💡 优化建议:');
const bigPackages = sorted.slice(0, 5).map(([name]) => name);
if (bigPackages.includes('lodash')) {
  console.log('  - 将 lodash 替换为 lodash-es (支持 tree-shaking)');
}
if (bigPackages.includes('moment')) {
  console.log('  - 将 moment 替换为 dayjs (体积小 80%)');
}
if (bigPackages.includes('antd') || bigPackages.includes('@mui')) {
  console.log('  - 检查是否按需导入组件，避免全量打包');
}
console.log('  - 运行 npm run build:analyze 查看详细分析');
```

## P3-6：Electron 启动优化

```typescript
// electron/main.js (优化版)
import { app, BrowserWindow } from 'electron';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const isDev = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development';

let mainWindow = null;
let splashWindow = null;

// ===== 闪屏 =====
function createSplash() {
  splashWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 400,
    height: 300,
    transparent: true,
    frame: false,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    skipTaskbar: true,
    resizable: false,
    webPreferences: { nodeIntegration: false, contextIsolation: true },
  });
  splashWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, '../public/splash.html'));
  splashWindow.center();
}

// ===== 主窗口 =====
function createMainWindow() {
  mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 1400,
    height: 900,
    minWidth: 1024,
    minHeight: 768,
    show: false,
    backgroundColor: '#05070D',
    webPreferences: {
      nodeIntegration: false,
      contextIsolation: true,
      sandbox: true,
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'preload.js'),
    },
  });

  // 延迟加载（让闪屏先显示）
  setTimeout(() => {
    const url = isDev ? 'http://localhost:3000' : `file://${path.join(__dirname, '../.next/standalone/index.html')}`;
    mainWindow.loadURL(url);

    mainWindow.once('ready-to-show', () => {
      splashWindow?.close();
      splashWindow = null;
      mainWindow.show();
    });

    if (isDev) mainWindow.webContents.openDevTools({ mode: 'detach' });
  }, 300);
}

// ===== 启动 =====
app.whenReady().then(() => {
  createSplash();
  createMainWindow();
});

app.on('window-all-closed', () => {
  if (process.platform !== 'darwin') app.quit();
});
```

## 第三步：更新 Prisma Schema（新增 6 张表）

在 `prisma/schema.prisma` 中新增以下模型，然后执行迁移。

```prisma
// ===== 新增表：身份核 =====
model IdentityKernel {
  id                   String   @id @default(cuid())
  leadId               String   @unique
  trustLevel           Float    @default(0.5)
  emotionState         String   @default("neutral")
  valueSensitivity     Float    @default(0.5)
  urgency              Float    @default(0.3)
  resistance           Float    @default(0.5)
  conversionDistance   Float    @default(0.8)
  socialRoleAffinity   Float    @default(0.5)
  updatedAt            DateTime @updatedAt
}

// ===== 新增表：对话图 =====
model ConversationGraph {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  leadId    String   @unique
  graph     String   @db.Text  // JSON 字符串
  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
}

// ===== 新增表：SOP 定义 =====
model SOPDefinition {
  id               String   @id @default(cuid())
  name             String
  description      String?
  triggerType      String   @default("manual")
  triggerCondition String?  // JSON
  nodes            String   @db.Text  // JSON
  edges            String   @db.Text  // JSON
  isActive         Boolean  @default(true)
  createdAt        DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime @updatedAt
}

// ===== 新增表：SOP 实例 =====
model SOPInstance {
  id               String   @id @default(cuid())
  sopDefinitionId  String
  leadId           String
  currentNodeId    String?
  status           String   @default("running")
  context          String?  @db.Text  // JSON
  startedAt        DateTime @default(now())
  completedAt      DateTime?
  updatedAt        DateTime @updatedAt
}

// ===== 新增表：SOP 节点日志 =====
model SOPNodeLog {
  id              String   @id @default(cuid())
  sopInstanceId   String
  nodeId          String
  skillName       String?
  input           String?  @db.Text  // JSON
  output          String?  @db.Text  // JSON
  status          String   @default("success")
  errorMessage    String?
  startedAt       DateTime @default(now())
  completedAt     DateTime
  durationMs      Int
}

// ===== 新增表：视频号表现 =====
model VideoPerformance {
  id               String   @id @default(cuid())
  videoId          String
  title            String?
  views            Int      @default(0)
  likes            Int      @default(0)
  comments         Int      @default(0)
  shares           Int      @default(0)
  watchTime        Float    @default(0)
  completionRate   Float    @default(0)
  negativeFeedback Float    @default(0)
  createdAt        DateTime @default(now())
}
```

```bash
npx prisma migrate dev --name add_identity_sop_video
npx prisma generate
```

## 第四步：模块集成顺序（从底向上）

| 顺序 | 模块 | 文件位置 | 依赖 |
|------|------|----------|------|
| 1 | 加密工具 | `frontend/src/lib/crypto.ts` | 无 |
| 2 | Prisma 中间件 | `frontend/src/server/prisma-middleware.ts` | 无 |
| 3 | 日志工具 | `frontend/src/lib/logger.ts` | 无 |
| 4 | 错误上报 | `frontend/src/lib/error-report.ts` | Sentry DSN |
| 5 | LLM 调用 | `frontend/src/lib/llm.ts` | API Key |
| 6 | 消息去重 | `frontend/src/lib/dedup.ts` | Redis |
| 7 | 多级调度器 | `frontend/src/lib/scheduler.ts` | Redis, BullMQ |
| 8 | 对话图引擎 | `frontend/src/lib/conversation-graph.ts` | Prisma |
| 9 | 身份核 | `frontend/src/lib/identity-kernel.ts` | Prisma |
| 10 | 人格编译器 | `frontend/src/lib/persona-compiler.ts` | Prisma |
| 11 | 身份调度器 | `frontend/src/lib/identity-scheduler.ts` | 身份核+人格编译器 |
| 12 | SOP 引擎 | `frontend/src/lib/sop-engine.ts` | Prisma + 所有 Skill |
| 13 | 视频号优化器 | `frontend/src/lib/video-optimizer.ts` | Prisma |
| 14 | 评论截流 | `frontend/src/lib/comment-capture.ts` | Prisma |
| 15 | LTV 计算 | `frontend/src/lib/ltv-calculator.ts` | Prisma |
| 16 | ClawBot 适配器 | `waos-stream/src/wechat/clawbot-adapter.ts` | Redis |
| 17 | Session 管理 | `waos-stream/src/wechat/session-manager.ts` | Redis |
| 18 | 消息同步 | `waos-stream/src/wechat/message-sync.ts` | ClawBot + Redis |
| 19 | 消息标准化 | `waos-stream/src/wechat/message-normalizer.ts` | Redis |
| 20 | Onboarding | `frontend/src/components/Onboarding.tsx` | 无 |
| 21 | 空状态 | `frontend/src/components/EmptyState.tsx` | 无 |
| 22 | 快捷键 | `frontend/src/hooks/useKeyboardShortcuts.ts` | 无 |
| 23 | 快捷键面板 | `frontend/src/components/ShortcutsHelp.tsx` | 无 |
| 24 | 帮助中心 | `frontend/src/app/help/page.tsx` | 无 |

## 第七步：逐个验证（验收标准）

| 验证项 | 方法 | 预期结果 |
|--------|------|----------|
| ✅ PII 加密 | 打开 SQLite 查看 `Message.content` | 显示 `iv:authTag:encrypted` 格式 |
| ✅ 结构化日志 | 查看 `logs/app.log` | JSON 格式日志 |
| ✅ Sentry | 触发一个错误 | Sentry Dashboard 收到上报 |
| ✅ LLM | 发消息 "多少钱" | 回复由 AI 生成 |
| ✅ 调度器 | 查看 BullMQ Dashboard | HOT/WARM/COLD 三队列 |
| ✅ 身份核 | 查 `IdentityKernel` 表 | 有 trustLevel/emotionState 等字段 |
| ✅ SOP | 创建并执行一个 SOP | `SOPInstance` 表有记录 |
| ✅ LTV | 调用 `batchCalculateLTV` | 返回 A/B/C/D 分层 |
| ✅ 快捷键 | 按 `⌘+K` | 弹出快捷键面板 |
| ✅ 帮助中心 | 访问 `/help` | 显示 FAQ |

## 第八步：集成到主入口

### App 入口集成 Onboarding

```tsx
// frontend/src/app/page.tsx
import { Onboarding } from '@/components/Onboarding';
import { MainLayout } from '@/components/layout/MainLayout';

export default function HomePage() {
  const [showOnboarding, setShowOnboarding] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    const completed = localStorage.getItem('waos_onboarding_completed') === 'true';
    setShowOnboarding(!completed);
  }, []);

  if (showOnboarding) {
    return <Onboarding onComplete={() => setShowOnboarding(false)} />;
  }

  return <MainLayout />;
}
```

### 全局快捷键集成

```tsx
// frontend/src/components/layout/MainLayout.tsx
import { useKeyboardShortcuts } from '@/hooks/useKeyboardShortcuts';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';

export function MainLayout() {
  const router = useRouter();

  useKeyboardShortcuts({
    'nav.workbench': () => router.push('/'),
    'nav.customers': () => router.push('/customers'),
    'nav.comments': () => router.push('/comments'),
    'nav.knowledge': () => router.push('/knowledge'),
    'nav.sop': () => router.push('/sop'),
    'nav.analytics': () => router.push('/analytics'),
    'global.help': () => router.push('/help'),
  });

  // ... 其余代码
}
```

## 文件 1：`backend/app/core/state.py`

**改动说明**：删除所有冗余，只保留三件事——`get`、`update`、`_key`。所有状态写入必须经过这个类，其他地方不许直接操作 Redis。

```python
# backend/app/core/state.py
import json
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class StateKernel:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(user: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:state:{user}"

    @staticmethod
    def get(user: str) -> dict:
        data = redis_client.get(StateKernel._key(user))
        if data:
            return json.loads(data)
        return {"score": 0, "stage": "cold", "chat_count": 0}

    @staticmethod
    def update(user: str, patch: dict) -> dict:
        current = StateKernel.get(user)
        current.update(patch)
        current["score"] = max(0, min(100, current.get("score", 0)))
        redis_client.setex(StateKernel._key(user), 86400 * 30, json.dumps(current))
        return current
```

## 文件 2：`backend/app/core/crm.py`

**改动说明**：只算分数，不存状态。输入 `state` + `msg`，输出 `patch`。由调用方（pipeline）决定是否写入。

```python
# backend/app/core/crm.py
class CRM:
    @staticmethod
    def update(state: dict, msg: str) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)

        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["多少钱", "报价", "价格", "成交"]):
            score += 20
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["再看看", "不需要", "太贵"]):
            score -= 10

        score = max(0, min(100, score))
        stage = "HOT" if score > 80 else "WARM" if score > 50 else "COLD"

        return {"score": score, "stage": stage}
```

## 文件 3：`backend/app/core/persona.py`

**改动说明**：Persona 不再是标签，而是策略参数包。调用方拿到返回值后直接用于控制 AI 行为。

```python
# backend/app/core/persona.py
class Persona:
    @staticmethod
    def build(state: dict) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        return {
            "tone": "professional" if score > 50 else "friendly",
            "pressure": min(score / 100, 0.9),
            "max_length": 150 if score < 50 else 300,
            "use_case": score > 80
        }
```

## 文件 4：`backend/app/core/constraint.py`

**改动说明**：新增。AI 输出后的第一道防线——长度截断 + 高危词拦截。

```python
# backend/app/core/constraint.py
class Constraint:
    @staticmethod
    def apply(text: str) -> str:
        if len(text) > 300:
            text = text[:300]
        if "转账" in text:
            return "具体细节我们走正规流程沟通"
        return text
```

## 文件 5：`backend/app/core/safety.py`

**改动说明**：新增。第二道防线——黑名单词拦截。

```python
# backend/app/core/safety.py
class Safety:
    BANNED = ["刷单", "诈骗", "色情"]

    @staticmethod
    def filter(text: str) -> str:
        for w in Safety.BANNED:
            if w in text:
                return "抱歉，这个我帮不上忙"
        return text
```

## 文件 6：`backend/app/core/rhythm.py`

**改动说明**：新增。控制回复节奏，防止 AI 回复过快被微信检测。

```python
# backend/app/core/rhythm.py
import time
import random

class Rhythm:
    @staticmethod
    def apply():
        time.sleep(random.uniform(1.5, 4.5))
```

## 文件 7：`backend/app/core/pipeline.py`

**改动说明**：唯一入口。所有消息必须经过这里，不允许绕开。顺序：状态 → CRM → Persona → AI → 约束 → 安全 → 节奏 → 发送 → 更新状态。

```python
# backend/app/core/pipeline.py
from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.state import StateKernel
from app.core.crm import CRM
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.ai import AI
from app.core.constraint import Constraint
from app.core.safety import Safety
from app.core.rhythm import Rhythm
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter

def pipeline(event: Event, adapter: BaseAdapter):
    user = event.user

    state = StateKernel.get(user)
    crm_data = CRM.update(state, event.content)
    persona = Persona.build(crm_data)
    reply = AI.run(event.content, crm_data, persona)
    reply = Constraint.apply(reply)
    reply = Safety.filter(reply)
    Rhythm.apply()

    adapter.send(user, reply)
    StateKernel.update(user, crm_data)
```

## 文件 8：`backend/app/api/webhook.py`

**改动说明**：从 JWT 中提取 `tenant_id`，注入上下文。所有后续操作自动隔离租户。

```python
# backend/app/api/webhook.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Request
from uuid import UUID
from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.pipeline import pipeline
from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/webhook/{platform}")
async def webhook_receive(
    platform: str,
    request: Request,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    raw = await request.json()
    user = raw.get("from") or raw.get("user_id")
    content = raw.get("content") or raw.get("text")
    account_id = raw.get("account_id")

    event = Event(user=user, content=content, platform=platform, account_id=account_id)
    await pipeline(event, adapter=WeChatAdapter())
    return {"code": 0, "msg": "ok"}
```

```python
from app.models.base import Base

class Customer(Base):
    __tablename__ = "customers"

    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True)
```

## 文件 10：`backend/app/core/context.py`

**改动说明**：新增。管理租户上下文，所有 Redis Key 走这里生成。

```python
# backend/app/core/context.py
from contextvars import ContextVar
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

_tenant_id: ContextVar[Optional[UUID]] = ContextVar("tenant_id", default=None)

def set_tenant_id(tenant_id: UUID) -> None:
    _tenant_id.set(tenant_id)

def get_tenant_id() -> Optional[UUID]:
    return _tenant_id.get()

def get_tenant_key(suffix: str) -> str:
    tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
    return f"waos:{tenant_id}:{suffix}" if tenant_id else f"waos:global:{suffix}"
```

## 文件 11：`backend/app/core/dedup.py`

**改动说明**：Redis Key 带租户前缀，不同租户的事件独立去重。

```python
# backend/app/core/dedup.py
from app.core.context import get_tenant_key
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class Dedup:
    @staticmethod
    def check(event_id: str) -> bool:
        key = get_tenant_key(f"dedup:{event_id}")
        if redis_client.exists(key):
            return False
        redis_client.setex(key, 86400, "1")
        return True
```

## 文件 12：`backend/app/core/rate_limiter.py`

**改动说明**：Redis Key 带租户前缀。

```python
# backend/app/core/rate_limiter.py
from app.core.context import get_tenant_key
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class RateLimiter:
    @staticmethod
    def allow(user: str) -> bool:
        key = get_tenant_key(f"rate:{user}")
        count = redis_client.incr(key)
        if count == 1:
            redis_client.expire(key, 60)
        return count <= 10
```

```python
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import os

DATABASE_URL = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://localhost/waos")

engine = create_engine(
    DATABASE_URL,
    pool_size=20,
    max_overflow=10,
    pool_timeout=30,
    pool_recycle=3600,
    pool_pre_ping=True,
)

SessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=engine)
```

## 文件 15：`backend/app/core/intent.py`

**改动说明**：新增。轻量级意图识别器，优先拦截 SPAM。

```python
# backend/app/core/intent.py
class IntentClassifier:
    INTENT_MAP = {
        "PRICE": ["多少钱", "报价", "价格", "怎么卖"],
        "BUY": ["下单", "购买", "怎么买"],
        "SPAM": ["刷单", "广告", "色情", "违法"],
        "CHAT": ["你好", "在吗", "哈哈"],
    }

    @classmethod
    def classify(cls, msg: str) -> str:
        msg_lower = msg.lower()
        for intent, keywords in cls.INTENT_MAP.items():
            for kw in keywords:
                if kw in msg_lower:
                    return intent
        return "CHAT"
```

```python
# backend/app/core/strategy.py
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier

class StrategyRouter:
    @staticmethod
    def route(state: dict, intent: str) -> str:
        if intent == "SPAM":
            return "IGNORE_STRATEGY"
        if intent in ["PRICE", "BUY"] and state.get("score", 0) > 50:
            return "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
        return "FRIEND_STRATEGY"
```

## 文件 18：`backend/app/api/auth.py`

**改动说明**：登录时签发 JWT 必须包含 `tenant_id`。

```python
# backend/app/api/auth.py
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import jwt
import os

JWT_SECRET = os.getenv("JWT_SECRET", "waos-super-secret")

@router.post("/login")
def login(username: str, password: str):
    # 假设从 DB 查到 user，包含 tenant_id
    user = authenticate(username, password)
    payload = {
        "sub": str(user.id),
        "tenant": str(user.tenant_id),
        "exp": datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(hours=24)
    }
    token = jwt.encode(payload, JWT_SECRET, algorithm="HS256")
    return {"access_token": token, "tenant_id": str(user.tenant_id)}
```

## 文件 1：`backend/app/adapters/clawbot/adapter.py`

改动说明：真实 HTTP 调用 ClawBot API，带重试、超时、降级。

```python
# backend/app/adapters/clawbot/adapter.py
import httpx
import asyncio
from typing import Optional
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter
from app.utils.logger import logger

class ClawBotAdapter(BaseAdapter):
    def __init__(self, base_url: Optional[str] = None, api_key: Optional[str] = None):
        self.base_url = base_url or "http://clawbot.local:8080/api"
        self.api_key = api_key or ""
        self._client = None

    async def _get_client(self) -> httpx.AsyncClient:
        if self._client is None:
            headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"} if self.api_key else {}
            self._client = httpx.AsyncClient(base_url=self.base_url, headers=headers, timeout=30.0)
        return self._client

    async def send(self, user: str, msg: str, account_id: Optional[str] = None) -> dict:
        client = await self._get_client()
        for attempt in range(3):
            try:
                resp = await client.post("/send", json={"to": user, "content": msg, "account_id": account_id})
                if resp.status_code == 429:
                    await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)
                    continue
                resp.raise_for_status()
                return resp.json()
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"ClawBot send failed (attempt {attempt+1}): {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(1)
        return {"code": -1, "msg": "send failed after retries"}

    async def fetch_messages(self, account_id: str, since: Optional[int] = None) -> list:
        client = await self._get_client()
        try:
            resp = await client.get("/messages", params={"account_id": account_id, "since": since})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            return resp.json().get("messages", [])
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ClawBot fetch failed: {e}")
            return []

    async def login(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        client = await self._get_client()
        resp = await client.post("/login", json={"account_id": account_id})
        return resp.json()

    async def heartbeat(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        client = await self._get_client()
        try:
            resp = await client.post("/heartbeat", json={"account_id": account_id})
            return resp.status_code == 200
        except Exception:
            return False
```

## 文件 2：`backend/app/core/memory.py`

改动说明：L1-L4 四层记忆系统。L1 短期（Redis 滑动窗口），L2 长期（SQLite/PostgreSQL），L3 语义（Qdrant 向量），L4 决策（结构化存储）。

```python
# backend/app/core/memory.py
import json
import time
from typing import Optional
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.db.session import SessionLocal
from app.models.customer import Customer

class MemorySystem:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(user: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:memory:{user}"

    # === L1: 短期记忆（Redis，30 分钟窗口） ===
    @staticmethod
    def short_term_push(user: str, role: str, content: str) -> None:
        key = f"{MemorySystem._key(user)}:l1"
        redis_client.lpush(key, json.dumps({"role": role, "content": content, "ts": time.time()}))
        redis_client.ltrim(key, 0, 19)
        redis_client.expire(key, 1800)

    @staticmethod
    def short_term_get(user: str) -> list:
        key = f"{MemorySystem._key(user)}:l1"
        data = redis_client.lrange(key, 0, 19)
        return [json.loads(d) for d in data] if data else []

    # === L2: 长期记忆（PostgreSQL，客户画像） ===
    @staticmethod
    def long_term_get(user: str) -> dict:
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter(Customer.wx_id == user).first()
            if customer and customer.profile:
                return customer.profile
            return {}
        finally:
            db.close()

    @staticmethod
    def long_term_update(user: str, patch: dict) -> None:
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter(Customer.wx_id == user).first()
            if customer:
                profile = customer.profile or {}
                profile.update(patch)
                customer.profile = profile
                db.commit()
        finally:
            db.close()

    # === L3: 语义记忆（Qdrant 向量，占位） ===
    @staticmethod
    def semantic_search(user: str, query: str, top_k: int = 5) -> list:
        # 实际接入 Qdrant
        return []

    @staticmethod
    def semantic_store(user: str, text: str, metadata: dict) -> None:
        # 实际写入 Qdrant
        pass

    # === L4: 决策记忆（什么策略有效/无效） ===
    @staticmethod
    def decision_record(user: str, strategy: str, outcome: str) -> None:
        key = f"{MemorySystem._key(user)}:l4"
        redis_client.lpush(key, json.dumps({"strategy": strategy, "outcome": outcome, "ts": time.time()}))
        redis_client.ltrim(key, 0, 49)
        redis_client.expire(key, 86400 * 30)

    @staticmethod
    def decision_get(user: str) -> list:
        key = f"{MemorySystem._key(user)}:l4"
        data = redis_client.lrange(key, 0, 49)
        return [json.loads(d) for d in data] if data else []
```

## 文件 3：`backend/app/core/knowledge.py`

改动说明：RAG 知识库基础结构。支持文档入库、向量检索、答案生成。Qdrant 操作用占位，实际接入时替换。

```python
# backend/app/core/knowledge.py
import hashlib
import json
from typing import Optional, List
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class KnowledgeBase:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(doc_id: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:kb:{doc_id}"

    # 入库（文档分段 + 向量化占位）
    @staticmethod
    def add_document(content: str, metadata: Optional[dict] = None) -> str:
        doc_id = hashlib.md5(content.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
        chunks = [content[i:i+200] for i in range(0, len(content), 200)]
        payload = {
            "id": doc_id,
            "content": content,
            "chunks": chunks,
            "metadata": metadata or {},
            "created_at": time.time()
        }
        redis_client.setex(KnowledgeBase._key(doc_id), 86400 * 30, json.dumps(payload))
        # 向量化存储（占位，实际接入 Qdrant）
        # for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
        #     qdrant.upsert(...)
        return doc_id

    @staticmethod
    def search(query: str, top_k: int = 3) -> List[dict]:
        # 向量检索占位，实际调用 Qdrant
        # results = qdrant.search(query, top_k)
        # 降级：关键词匹配
        results = []
        keys = redis_client.keys("waos:kb:*")
        for key in keys:
            data = redis_client.get(key)
            if data:
                doc = json.loads(data)
                if query in doc["content"]:
                    results.append({"id": doc["id"], "content": doc["content"], "score": 0.5})
                if len(results) >= top_k:
                    break
        return results

    @staticmethod
    def get_document(doc_id: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        data = redis_client.get(KnowledgeBase._key(doc_id))
        return json.loads(data) if data else None
```

## 文件 4：`backend/app/core/scheduler.py`

改动说明：HOT/WARM/COLD 三级调度器。用 Redis ZSET 实现优先级队列，带老化机制。

```python
# backend/app/core/scheduler.py
import time
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class Scheduler:
    QUEUES = {"hot": "waos:q:hot", "warm": "waos:q:warm", "cold": "waos:q:cold"}

    @staticmethod
    def enqueue(lead_id: str, priority: float) -> None:
        if priority >= 80:
            q = Scheduler.QUEUES["hot"]
        elif priority >= 50:
            q = Scheduler.QUEUES["warm"]
        else:
            q = Scheduler.QUEUES["cold"]
        redis_client.zadd(q, {lead_id: priority})

    @staticmethod
    def dequeue() -> Optional[tuple]:
        for q in ["hot", "warm", "cold"]:
            key = Scheduler.QUEUES[q]
            items = redis_client.zpopmax(key, 1)
            if items:
                lead_id, priority = items[0]
                return lead_id, priority, q
        return None

    @staticmethod
    def aging() -> None:
        # 每 10 分钟冷队列全体 +2 分，防止饿死
        key = Scheduler.QUEUES["cold"]
        items = redis_client.zrange(key, 0, -1, withscores=True)
        for lead_id, score in items:
            redis_client.zadd(key, {lead_id: score + 2})

    @staticmethod
    def size() -> dict:
        return {q: redis_client.zcard(key) for q, key in Scheduler.QUEUES.items()}
```

## 文件 5：`backend/app/utils/logger.py`

改动说明：结构化日志（JSON 格式），写入文件 + 控制台。自动脱敏敏感字段。

```python
# backend/app/utils/logger.py
import logging
import json
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional

class StructuredFormatter(logging.Formatter):
    def format(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> str:
        log_data = {
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "level": record.levelname,
            "message": record.getMessage(),
            "module": record.module,
            "line": record.lineno,
        }
        if hasattr(record, "user_id"):
            log_data["user_id"] = record.user_id
        if hasattr(record, "tenant_id"):
            log_data["tenant_id"] = str(record.tenant_id)
        if hasattr(record, "trace_id"):
            log_data["trace_id"] = record.trace_id
        if record.exc_info:
            log_data["exception"] = self.formatException(record.exc_info)
        return json.dumps(log_data, ensure_ascii=False)

def get_logger(name: str = "waos") -> logging.Logger:
    logger = logging.getLogger(name)
    logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    # 控制台输出
    console = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    console.setFormatter(StructuredFormatter())
    logger.addHandler(console)

    # 文件输出
    try:
        file = logging.FileHandler("logs/app.log")
        file.setFormatter(StructuredFormatter())
        logger.addHandler(file)
    except Exception:
        pass

    return logger

logger = get_logger()
```

## 文件 6：`scripts/backup_db.py`

改动说明：数据库自动备份脚本。压缩 + 保留最近 7 天。

```python
# scripts/backup_db.py
import os
import subprocess
import gzip
import shutil
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

DB_PATH = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "waos.db").replace("sqlite:///", "")
BACKUP_DIR = "backups"
RETENTION_DAYS = 7

def backup():
    os.makedirs(BACKUP_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    timestamp = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    backup_path = f"{BACKUP_DIR}/waos_{timestamp}.sqlite.gz"

    subprocess.run(f"sqlite3 {DB_PATH} .dump | gzip > {backup_path}", shell=True, check=True)
    print(f"Backup created: {backup_path}")

    # 删除 7 天前备份
    cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=RETENTION_DAYS)
    for f in os.listdir(BACKUP_DIR):
        if f.startswith("waos_") and f.endswith(".sqlite.gz"):
            try:
                ts_str = f.replace("waos_", "").replace(".sqlite.gz", "")
                ts = datetime.strptime(ts_str, "%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
                if ts < cutoff:
                    os.remove(os.path.join(BACKUP_DIR, f))
                    print(f"Removed old backup: {f}")
            except Exception:
                pass

if __name__ == "__main__":
    backup()
```

## 文件 7：`backend/app/utils/sentry.py`

改动说明：Sentry 错误上报工具。初始化 + 捕获异常 + 上报上下文。

```python
# backend/app/utils/sentry.py
import os
import sentry_sdk
from sentry_sdk import capture_exception, capture_message, set_context, set_user, set_tag

def init_sentry():
    dsn = os.getenv("SENTRY_DSN")
    if dsn:
        sentry_sdk.init(
            dsn=dsn,
            environment=os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT", "development"),
            traces_sample_rate=0.1 if os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT") == "production" else 1.0,
        )
        return True
    return False

def report_error(error: Exception, context: dict = None, user_id: str = None):
    if context:
        set_context("context", context)
    if user_id:
        set_user({"id": user_id})
    capture_exception(error)

def report_message(msg: str, level: str = "info", context: dict = None):
    if context:
        set_context("context", context)
    capture_message(msg, level=level)
```

## 文件 8：`backend/app/utils/crypto.py`

改动说明：AES-256-GCM 加密/解密。用于 PII 字段加密（wx_id, phone, content）。

```python
# backend/app/utils/crypto.py
import os
import base64
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.pbkdf2 import PBKDF2HMAC

_KEY = None

def _get_key() -> bytes:
    global _KEY
    if _KEY is None:
        secret = os.getenv("ENCRYPTION_SECRET", "waos-fallback-secret")
        kdf = PBKDF2HMAC(algorithm=hashes.SHA256(), length=32, salt=b"waos_salt", iterations=100000)
        _KEY = kdf.derive(secret.encode())
    return _KEY

def encrypt(plaintext: str) -> str:
    if not plaintext:
        return plaintext
    key = _get_key()
    aesgcm = AESGCM(key)
    nonce = os.urandom(12)
    ct = aesgcm.encrypt(nonce, plaintext.encode(), None)
    return base64.b64encode(nonce + ct).decode()

def decrypt(ciphertext: str) -> str:
    if not ciphertext:
        return ciphertext
    try:
        key = _get_key()
        aesgcm = AESGCM(key)
        data = base64.b64decode(ciphertext.encode())
        nonce, ct = data[:12], data[12:]
        return aesgcm.decrypt(nonce, ct, None).decode()
    except Exception:
        return ciphertext

def is_encrypted(text: str) -> bool:
    if not text:
        return False
    try:
        base64.b64decode(text.encode())
        return True
    except Exception:
        return False
```

## 部署执行步骤

按顺序执行以下命令：

```bash
# 1. 安装新增依赖
pip install httpx cryptography sentry-sdk

# 2. 创建日志目录
mkdir -p logs backups

# 3. 创建迁移文件
alembic revision --autogenerate -m "add_tenant_memory_knowledge"

# 4. 执行迁移
alembic upgrade head

# 5. 设置环境变量
export ENCRYPTION_SECRET="$(python -c 'import os;print(os.urandom(32).hex())')"
export SENTRY_DSN="your-sentry-dsn"
export DATABASE_URL="sqlite:///waos.db"

# 6. 测试备份
python scripts/backup_db.py

# 7. 启动服务
uvicorn app.main:app --reload
```
